Ko min tɔ bɔlen bɔlen na Diriisa Togola - Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ, Sogɛli Kokala Mayiga, n’a ka kumalaseli minisiri, Haruna Turehi, bilasira, nin ntɛnɛndon zuwɛnkalo tile 28 san 2021, kunnafonidilaw ka soba la walasa ka kunnafonidilaw ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn.
Nin dusukunnako taama la kunnafonidilaw ka soba la, kun ye ka kunnafonidilaw kunnafoni cɛmancɛlafanga gɔfɛrɛnaman ka baara fɔlɔw kan, minnu ye dugukolo lakana, politiki ani fangabulonkow yɛlɛmaniw ye, ani hadamadenyako kɛlɛyali ye.
Minisiri ɛmɔgɔ ye sababu sɔrɔ walasa ka Jamana Labɛnni Sɛbɛnw ɛnabɔli ɛnabɔli ɲɛnabɔli nata jira kunnafonidilaw ye.
Ani fana kalataw ɲɛnabɔli cakɛda kelen sigili, min bɛna nata la,
A tun bɛ kunnafonidilaw ka soba perezidan ɲɛna.
A ka weleli kumalaseli kɔnɔ, kunnafonidilaw ka soba perezidan, Danti, ye hakililatigɛ gɔfɛrɛnaman fɛ, ka bilasirali kɛ Mali kunnafonidilaw ma dɛsɛ.
A kɛtɔla ka nin taama nafa sɔrɔ, a ye Mali ɲɛmɔgɔya ɲɛmɔgɔ ka gɛlɛya dalen ɲini, gɛlɛyaw kan, minnu bɛ kunnafonidilaw ka donkibaruw ka donkibaruya la.
Segin tɛ se ka kɛ kasɔrɔ kunnafonidilaw segin tɛ yen.
A y’o dantigɛ.
A ka fɔ la, gɛlɛyaw, minnu bɛ Mali kunnafonidilaw fɛ, o ye, dɔwɛrɛw cɛla, sɛbɛn kura min bɛ tali kɛ kibaru ɲagali ɲagali kan, kunnafonidilaw minɛni ka jalatigɛliw, kunnafonidilaw ka dɛmɛni minɛni ma hakililatigɛ sɔrɔ kabini san saba, lɛrɛ jɔyɔrɔw, minnu tɛ dɛmɛnen tɛ kɛ ka kɛ a yɔrɔ kɛrɛfɛjɔyɔrɔw kan, ani kunnafonidilaw ka soba lakurayali ɲini.
PEYƐMU ye kunnafonidilaw hakililatigɛ yaasa ka ɲɛnabɔcogo sɔrɔ nin dɛsɛw la.
A ka taama kun ye, Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Sogɛli Kokala Mayiga bɛn’a fɔ ko.
Cɛmancɛlafanga Perezidan ka ɲɛmɔgɔya kan, an y’a latigɛ ka cɛmancɛlafanga taabolo dusu, sennateli taabolo di ni Mali mɔgɔw ka donni ɲini ye.
Wa k’a fɔ u la ko cɛmancɛlafanga sigilen don tile saba kan.
K’a da a kan.
Pɔlɔsili fɔlɔ ye lakanako bolo, waati min na lakanako yɛlɛmani tɛna sɔrɔ, fasodenw bɛna to halibi k’u sɛgɛsɛgɛ cɛmancɛlafanga ka se ka gɛlɛyaw ɲɛnabɔ.
O ɲininkali bɛ sɔrɔdasiw ka ɲɛmɔgɔba bolo.
Min ye dakun filanan ko ye, min ye politiki dakun ye, politiki ani fangabulonkow yɛlɛmaniw bɛ gɔfɛrɛnaman bolo.

a y’o hakililatigɛ.

PEYƐMU y’a lahidu k’a fɔ ko donjatesɛbɛn kura, min bɛna sɔrɔ gɔfɛrɛnaman fɛ, bɛna kɛ bɛnkanw kɔnɔ, politikitɔnw bɛɛ ani jɛrɛjɛkuluw ɲɛmɔgɔw bɛna kumaɲɔgɔnya kɛ.

A kɛtɔla ka kuma hadamadenya jɔnjɔn ka tiɲɛni kan, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la IYƐNITEYƐMU ka bagabagaliw kan, PEYƐMU y’a hakililatigɛ dɛmɛni, ko kumafalenw bɛ to ni sendikiw ɲɛmɔgɔw ye, walasa ka ɲangili bali min tɛ mɔgɔw la.
Aliyu Badara Jara Giyamu Soro minɛnna Konowari kiriso fɛ ni ɲangili ye kaso kɛli ye.
Konowari Minisiri ɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ lakodɔnna ni Jamana lakanako ɲinini ye.
A ka awoka Fufussiata Banba Lamini, a ka Soul taabolo ɲɛmɔgɔ, depitebulon kɔrɔ, Bɛn Sok, bɛ san 20 kofɔ u kan.
Min ye Alain Lobognon ko ye, o ye Simɔni ani Rigobɛri Soro ani Falicieb Sekɔngow ye.
U minɛna ni kalo 17 kaso ye foroba sariya gɛlɛya kosɔn.
Kiriso b’a latigɛ fana Giyamu Soro ka politikitɔn, Kelenyatɔnw ani fasodenw bɛ ɲɔgɔn cɛ ( ZESEYƐSI ) tilali.
Sɛbɛn kɔlɔsili ye rfi.fr kan - kumalaselisɛbɛn dɔ kɔnɔ, min labɔra nin dɔgɔkun na, Kɛli Ansar ani Faraɲɔgɔnkankulu ye ɲɔgɔnye lakodɔn ni nisɔn caman ye nin dɔgɔkun in Gundamu, ni ko kun jɔyɔrɔ jɔnjɔnw dɔ ye, Taawudɛni marabolo mara tilali koɲɛnabɔli koɲɛnabɔli ta.
O cogo la, kumalaselisɛbɛn y’a fara a kan, Taawudɛni marabolo, bi, o ye ɲɛnabɔcogo belebele ye, min ka kan ka dusu don ani min ka jama ka kan ka bilasira ani k’a kologɛlɛya.
« A ka kan k’a kɛ misali ani taamasiyɛn ye, min tɔgɔ bɛ ka kɛ yɔrɔ wɛrɛw ye, minnu fara ɲɔgɔn kan, n’a bɛ to tiɲɛni ye, k’a bɛn jamaw ka ɲɛsinnenw ma.
Jɛkulu minnu y’a sɛbɛn, u y’u kɛ k’u kɛ k’u kɛ k’u kɛ k’u ye kɛnɛ bila fan bɛɛ la walasa ka nin marabolo kɛ tiɲɛ ye, min bɛ ka tɛmɛ politiki mɔgɔw ani mɔgɔw cɛsiri », Kolatilenjɛkulu y’o dantigɛ.
Yanni a k’a fara a kan ko nin dusukasi ani dantigɛli misali, min ka kan ka dɔgɔya yɔrɔ wɛrɛ wɛrɛ la, janko Lakɛba marabolo, min ɲininkalen don forow bɛɛ kɔnɔ ani min makɔnɔnen don Faguibini Sɛgɛrɛtigi jamaw ani mɔgɔ caman wɛrɛw fɛ.
« I n’a fɔ an ka saratiwaati b’a fɔ cogo min, an bɛ bɛn hakilinaw bɛɛ kɔnɔ ani an b’a ɲini latigɛbagaw ani minnu sen b’u sen don u ka taa bɛnɲini hukumu kɔnɔ, sigidajamaw bɛɛ fɔlenw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, ka ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn ɲɛmɔgɔya sigili la, min tɛ mɔgɔ si bila ɲɔgɔn na », a y’a kuncɛ ten.
Berɛhima Jalo Koɲɛ fɔlɔ, min kiri kɛra Moti Kasitigɛlaw ka Kiriso fɛ, ntɛnɛndon zuwɛnkalo tile 21 san 2021, tun bɛ Jamana minisiri ɲɔgɔn cɛla Umaru Kadiga (Bɛrɛgɛrɛgu, Bankasi sɛrikili ), min jalaki bɛ Nuhumu Sidibe ka kú.
A lakodɔnnen k’a jalaki ni kow ye, minnu tun bɛ kiri la a la, Umaru Kadiga kaso k’a bila abada.
Kow!
A ko ninnu bɛ bɔ sɛbɛn kɔnɔ.
Feburuyekalo tile 18, san 2019, Bedugu, Fakala dugukolo komini, Jene sɛrikili la, sɔgɔma kɔnɔ, Umaru Gadiaga taara dugukolo marigotɔ la kalafili fan dɔ kama.
Taama kɔnɔ, a y’a denmisɛn Nuhumu Sidibe sɔrɔ, min si bɛ san 13 ɲɔgɔnna, u ka bagan kɔnɔ.
Kumafalenw kɔfɔlen kɔfɛ u ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, Umaru Gadiaga bɛ masikɛtigi caman kɛ Nuhumu Sidibe la a ka kɔnɔn yɔrɔ wɛrɛw kan, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw ani ɲɔgɔn.
Nuhumu y’i sinsin a ka sɔrɔ la wa a y’i gɛlɛya yɔrɔw kan.
Umaru taara a bɛnidenw fɛ, k’a fa ka ɲɛmɔgɔya kɛ duguba ɲɛmɔgɔ ye.
Sɛgɛsɛgɛli ɲɛmɔgɔya kɔfɛ, min bolodalen don Jene zandaramaw ka marabolo bolofara fɛ, Umaru Kadiga bila ɲangili kɔnɔ.
Mɔgɔ jalakilen y’a jɔ kow la, minnu jalakilen don, kasɔrɔ gɛlɛya t’a la.
A y’a ɲɛfɔ ko san 2019 feburuyekalo tile 18 san, a y’a cɛ denmisɛn Nuhumu Sidibe sɔrɔ u ka baarada kɔnɔ, min, i n’a fɔ a ka daminɛna, y’a daminɛ ka ɲangili kɛ a la kasɔrɔ kun t’a la.
Wa walasa k’a laban ni ɲɔgɔn ye, a y’i sɔrɔ Nuhumu Sidibe fɛ walasa k’a mɔgɔ tun bɛ a kɔnɔ ni makɛti ye waati caman.
O sɛbɛn sɛbɛnni tun bɛ kɛ k’a sɔrɔ Umaru Kadiga ka jɔyɔrɔtigiya sɔrɔ denmisɛn Nuhumu Sidibe ka ku la.
Umaru tɛmɛna k’a kɛ muguya ye.
Nka kɛcogoya walima hakilila kɛcogoya tun tɛ dɛsɛ.
O cogo de la, kow ɲininkali kɛra murutili ye, kirisariya sariyasen 199 ani 201 hukumu kɔnɔ.
O siratigɛ la, jalakiw kunnafoni kɔnɔ, minnu bɛ se ka kɛ Umaru Kadiga kan, k’a kɛ Dɛgugu, Fakala dugujukɔrɔfɛjɛkulu sɛrikili ye, san 2019 feburuyekalo tile 18 la, k’a kɛnɛ kan ni kɛcogo ye Nuhumu Sidibe ye, kow ye, minnu labɛnnen don ani k’u ɲangi kirisariya sariyasunba sariyasen 199 ani 1 ani 201 fɛ.
Mɔgɔ jalakilen b’a sɔn kow la, minnu kiri b’a la. Kunnafonidiminɛnw ka kɔnɔ, mɔgɔ jalakilen ka kirikɛyɔrɔ bataki n°2 t’a ka kaso si dantigɛ.
kunnafoni minnu sɔrɔla a yɛrɛmahɔrɔnya kan, bɛ ɲɔgɔn na.
Nka dɔgɔtɔrɔ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen, min kɛra walasa k’a ka miirina kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya kɛ, a ka san 2019 desanburukalo tile 11 laselisɛbɛn kɔnɔ, y’a jira k’a tɛ dɔgɔya dɔwɛrɛ walima dɔgɔya dɔwɛrɛ si sɔrɔ a ka ɲangili jɔyɔrɔtigiya kan.
O kun ninnu na, Kiritigɛlaw y’u ka murutili kɛ kow laɲini ani k’a dantigɛ ko mɔgɔ jalakilen Umaru Kadiga ka ɲɔgɔn kan, kow lakɔlɔsili b’u laɲini ka kɛ cogoya kosɛbɛ.
O la kiriso y’a ka jalakili dantigɛ Moti kiriso ɲɛkɔrɔ.
Kuma kɔnɔ ntɛnɛndon zuwɛnkalo tile 21 san 2021, Umaru Gadiaga, kasɔrɔ a ma jɔnjɔnw sɔrɔ, sɔnna kow la, minnu tun kiri b’a la, n’a ka baara gɛlɛya nin cogo la a ka awoka, Simɔni Legu, ma.
A mɔgɔ n’a ka mɔgɔ ninnu ye maramafɛn sɔrɔ, o mɔgɔ tɛ fɛɛrɛ wɛrɛ sɔrɔ k’a ɲini kiriso ka bɛnɲini ɲini.
Bawo, a ka kɔrɔfɔw la, Umaru Gadiaga t’a miiri jɔyɔrɔw la.
« N ka mɔgɔ cɛbɔ bɛ dɔgɔn, a t’a miiri hakilinaw dɔgɔya.
A tɛ hakilina kologɛlɛyalen ye.
N kɛlen k’a sɔn kow la, minnu kiri b’a la, n b’a ɲini Kiritigɛbulon fɛ ni ko cogoyaw, minnu tɛmɛnen don », a y’o dantigɛ.
Nka forobakiritigɛla y’a sɛmɛntiya k’a fɔ ko mɔgɔ jalakilen b’a ka fanga bɛɛ kɛ ani k’a ka wale lakodɔnna.
A y’a sɔrɔ k’a ko kɛlenw tiɲɛtigiya kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen tɛ dɔwɛrɛ.
Mɛtiri Legu ka ɲininkaliw ma lamɛn Kiritigɛlaw fɛ, o min ye Umaru Kadiga sɔrɔ jalaki la ni k’a ɲangili ye mɔgɔ siɲɛ na.

Kɔlɔsili kɔnɔ ( 2 – 1 ).
Sɛgɛsɛgɛli kun ye.
Nin sɛgɛsɛgɛli, Sibi dugujukɔrɔfɛnw komini ka baaraw ɲɛnabɔli kan, bɛ tali kɛ san 2017 zanwiyekalo tile 1 la ka taa san 2019 desanburukalo tile 31 la waati kɔnɔ.
A laɲini ye ka hakililatigɛ ko Sibi dugujukɔrɔfɛnw ka Komini ( SEYƐRIYƐSI ) bɛ ɲɛnabɔ ni sɔrɔko, kɛcogo ani kɛcogo saratiw ye ani ka bɛn sariyaw ani sariyaw ma, minnu bɛ senna.
Sɛgɛsɛgɛli baaraw kɛra kɔnɔna kɔnɔn sɛgɛsɛgɛli kan, gɔfɛrɛnamanko, nafolokow ani nafolokow ɲɛnabɔli, dugujukɔrɔw ani dugujukɔrɔw ɲɛnabɔli, fasodenya ɲɛnabɔli, baarakɛlaw ɲɛnabɔli, fasodenya ɲɛnabɔli an’a sigidajamaw ka sebagaya ɲɛnabɔli kokɛcogoyaw kan.
Fan dɔ fɛ, BVG ka ci ye dantigɛlisɛbɛnw jɔyɔrɔtigiw sɛbɛn, n’u bilasiraliw bilasira, minnu bɛ se ka baaraw kɛcogoya ɲɛnabɔ ani fan wɛrɛ fɛ, ka nafoloko kɛcogoya juguw sɔrɔ, sariyasunba ani sariyasunba labɛnw sɔsɔliw la.
BVEZU ka dantigɛliw walasa ka mara ka gɛlɛyaw ɲɛnabɔcogoyaw ɲɛnabɔcogoya.
Sibi dugujukɔrɔfɛla komini ka kolatigɛjɛkulu ka kan :
Ka baarakɛjɛkulu sigilenw ka baara ɲɛnabɔli hakililatigɛ.
Sibi dugujukɔrɔfɛnw komini Mɛri ka kan ka kɛ
ka ɲɛnabɔli kɛ foroba ye, k’a bɛn sariyaw ma, minnu bɛ senna.
ka Komini ka baaraw kɛcogoya sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛ waati bɛɛ.
ka nafolokow tiɲɛtigiya taabolo labato.
ka nafolokow marabolo sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛ i n’a fɔ sariya min bɛ senna.
ka Sibi dugukolo ani kɔrɔfɛnw dugujukɔrɔfɛnni ɛmɔgɔyaso baarabolodali waleyali kɛ.
ka sigifɛnw ani sigifɛnw tɛ sigifɛnw bɛɛ lakodɔn, minnu ka kan ka bila Komini la, ani ka kokɛta dɔw ta walasa u ka donni kama komini dugukolo kɔnɔ.
Ka hakililatigɛ fasodenya sɛbɛnw sɛbɛnw datuguli ani minɛni na san bɛɛ desanburukalo tile 31.
ka forobabaarakɛlaw sɛgɛsɛgɛli ani ɲɛnabɔli kɛ i n’a fɔ sariya min bɛ senna.
Ka hakililatigɛ komini kɔnɔkow nafolokow labato ka kɛ i n’a fɔ sariya min bɛ senna.
ka baarakɛjɛkuluw sigi, ka bɛn sɛbɛnw ma, minnu bɛ sen kan, fɛnw ani baarakɛyɔrɔw sɔrɔli tuma na.
Kati kubeda kuntigi ka kan :
ka dantigɛlisɛbɛnw ani fasodenya sɛbɛnw sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛ.
Sɛbɛnbaga ka kan :
Ka Sibi dugujukɔrɔfɛnw yɔrɔmarakafo yɔrɔw ani takw bɛɛ tali kɛ i n’a fɔ lempo jɔyɔrɔw ye.
ka nafolokow marabolo sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛ i n’a fɔ sariya min bɛ senna.
Nafolokow kɔlɔsilikɛla ka kan :
ka Komini nafoloko cogoya bɛɛ laselisɛbɛn sabananw kɛ.
Sibi dugujukɔrɔfɛmarakafo ka Nafolokow Kɛbaga ka kan :
ka hakililatigɛ kɛ, min ɲini bɛnkansɛbɛn fɛ, min bɛ senna,
Sibi dugujukɔrɔfɛmarakafo ɛmɔgɔ ka kan :
ka hakililatigɛ kɛ, min ɲini bɛnkansɛbɛn fɛ, min bɛ senna,
Nafolokow ɲɔgɔn cɛsiriw.
Nafolokow kɛcogoya juguw bakuruba, minnu bɔlen bɛ nin kan, bɛ sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 27 435 650 la.

yamaruyasɛbɛnw, minnu bɛ tali kɛ sariyasɔsɔliw la, sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 1 114 150 ye.
wari hakɛ jɔnjɔnw kɔnɔ, minnu tɛ sariyasɔsɔw la, ka se Sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 24 522 000 ma.
wari hakɛ minnu tɛ jɔyɔrɔtigiya sɔrɔ, ka se sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 1 799 500 ma.
Sibi dugujukɔrɔfɛnw komini ɲɛnabɔli sɛgɛsɛgɛli kologɛlɛyali bɛ tali kɛ sɛgɛsɛgɛlikɛla ɛmɔgɔyaso ni Inyɔrɔpeyɛn tɔgɔlamɔgɔw cɛ Mali la baaraɲɔgɔnya hukumu kɔnɔ.
A b’a ɲini ka hakililatigɛ ko dugujukɔrɔfɛnw ani dugujukɔrɔfɛnw kominiw, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la, ani Sibi ta, b’u jɔyɔrɔw an’u jɔyɔrɔtigiyaw labato cogoya la, cɛmancɛlafanga waleyali la ani o kɛra, ka bɛn sariya ma, min bɛ senna.

U kɛtɔla ka ɲɔgɔn cɛmancɛyɔrɔ belebele tɛmɛni kan, min bilala helikɔpitɛri dɔ fɛ, ani k’a ɲɔgɔn cɛ ni marito ye, u tun na Siniw ka Kominisi Tɔnba ka san cɛ san ɲɛnajɛ ɲɛnajɛ ɲɛnajɛ ɲɛnajɛ.
Wa a yɛlɛmabaara dayɛlɛni na, a tun bɛ i n’a fɔ a taamasiyɛn tun tɛ se ka jɛya sɔrɔ.
Pariti, min bɛ fanga la kabini san 1949, kasɔrɔ a ma deli abada, b’a ɲini ka Sini ɲɛmɔgɔya to ɲɛ.
A ko in ye sababu ye Siniw ka fanga bolo k’a ka baaraw jira, kabini a sigili kɛlen kɔnɔlɔsilikalo la san 1921 Shanghai, Faransi cɛmancɛlafanga kɔrɔ kɔnɔ.
Ni kɔrɔfɔ kɛlen ye perezidan Sisi Zinpigi ka fasodenya la, n’a bɛ mɔgɔ jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ la.
K’a sɔrɔ fanga belebele ye, Sini tɛna yɛrɛ sɔrɔ jamana wɛrɛw fɛ, i n’a fɔ Tugalikaw ka koloniyali wa Japon ka wulikajɔ waati (1931 – 1945) la.
San cɛ san kama, Siniw fanga, min ye jamaw ɲɛnabɔli kɛnɛdaba ye, ye alamisadon belebele ye.
Jɔnjɔn ka jiginni kɔfɛ, jɔnjɔn 100 bɛ yɔrɔ jiginni kɔnɔ, ni helikopitɛri wari hakɛ ɲɔgɔnna ye.
U bɛ kɔlɔsilikɛlɛw kɔfɛ, o kɔfɛ lakɔlɔsilikɛlɛkulu dɔ kɔfɛ, min bɛ mɔgɔ caman taamasiyɛn bila Sini faaba kan.
A kɛtɔla k’a yɛrɛ k’a fɔ ko Mɔgɔ Mɔgɔ ye, sisan Siniw ka nimoro 1 bɛ nin waleyali mɔgɔ sɔrɔ, min lakodɔnnen don Siniw caman fɛ, yaasa k’a ka fanga sɔrɔ.
O bɛɛ kɛ ni ka gɔfɛrɛnaman sigibaga ka politiki sigibagaw ka mɔgɔ miliyɔn tan ni ɲɔgɔn caman sɔrɔbɔli ye (Grand Bɔnd ka taa ɲɛ, Dɔnko Cɛmancɛlafanga ) walima minnu ye 1989 demokarasiɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw ka gɛlɛya sɔrɔbɔli ye nin yɔrɔ kelen kan Tiananmen.
PESEYƐSI Sekeretɛri zenerali y’a ka kuma daminɛ kumakan ni kumakan ye.
Cɛɲɔgɔnw, cɛɲɔgɔnw?
A b’a ka kɔrɔfɔ kumalaseliw cɛsiri, n’a y’a hakililatigɛ k’a fɔ ko Marikisi bɛ to jamana kɔlɔsili ye, sɔrɔko yɛlɛmaniw n’u ta bɛɛ, minnu bɛ kɛ kabini san 40 bɛ minnu na, sɔrɔ sugufiyɛ sɔrɔ kosɔn.
A kɔrɔfɔ ka ca ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ ye waati kelen ye.
Mɔgɔw, minnu bɔra su kelen na walasa ka se ka na ɲɛnajɛ ma ani ka sɛgɛsɛgɛli jɔyɔrɔ caman sɔrɔ, i n’a fɔ a b’u yɛrɛ sɔrɔ.
O n’a ta bɛɛ, perezidan b’a dɔn waati min na k’a ka kɔfɔ k’a ka lamɛnniw sɔrɔ.
Vɛn bɛ yɛlɛma wa kiimɛ bɛ na.
Mɔgɔw b’u yɛlɛma i n’a fɔ cɛ kelen tɛ mɔgɔ kelen ye, n’a tɛ mɔgɔ tɛ sɛbɛn ye, min sɔrɔra u la.
Kɔnɔni seginna k’a kuma laban na, kasɔrɔ Diɲɛmɔgɔw bɛ ɲɔgɔn kan, yann’a ka kulɔbɔw ani kulɔbɔw caman bɔ.
Mɔgɔw b’a ka mɔgɔ kɛrɛfɛjɔw la, jama b’u yɛlɛma ni ka jama gɛlɛya ɲɔgɔn cɛ, Ode ka taa fasodenya la.
Kamalen, min si bɛ san 25 la, n’a ban b’a tɔgɔ fɔ, b’a fɔ n’a ye dusukasi ye ɲɛnajɛ fɛ, k’a da a kan a ye Pariti mɔgɔ ye kabini san kelen kɔnɔ.
Ne nisɔndiyalen bɛ k’an dilanna an waati la.
A y’o fɔ Faransi-Pɛrizi cakɛda ma.
Sigida jama yɛlɛnni, min tɛ bolodalen t’a la, ye gɛlɛya kɛ sirabakanboli sirabakanw siratigɛ la.
O n’a ta bɛɛ ni jɔnjɔn 3 ye dugukolo kan, ka bɔ dugukolo cɛmancɛyɔrɔ ma kɛrɛfɛjɔyɔrɔ ye.
Hali ni Bamakɔ tɛ baaraw ka cɛmancɛyɔrɔ sɔrɔ, dugukolo cɛmancɛyɔrɔ, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen kan, mara caman bɛ yɔrɔ min na.
Kɛrɛfɛjɛkɛrɛjɛkɛrɛjɛkɛrɛjɛkɛrɛjɛkɛrɛjɛkɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw ka kan ka tɛmɛ sɔgɔma ka taa sɔgɔma ka taa sɔgɔma.
K’a daminɛ sɔgɔma nɛgɛkanɲɛ 6 la, Bamakɔ – Senu jɔnjɔn siratigɛ taamasiyɛnna.
Mɔgɔ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw ka bolimafɛnw, sigidajamafɛnw ka bolimafɛnw, bisikili saba, takisiw, motow..., bɛ hakilijigin kɛ walasa k’u ka tɛmɛsiraw sɔrɔ.
Tiɲɛ na, dusukasi b’a la.
Lamini Jire ka fɔ la, Sotrama bolifɛnbaga.
O gɛlɛyaw bɛ yɔrɔ sɔrɔ polisi dɔw ka ɲɛnabɔcogoya kɔnɔ, minnu, k’a sɔrɔ ka taabolo ɲɛnabɔcogo ɲɛnabɔ, bɛ mɔgɔw tiɲɛni.
Pɔn Fahidi bolodalen don ni peyato tɛmɛ ye.
O n’a ta bɛɛ, nin tɛmɛni fana bɛ motobolila mɔgɔw fɛ, ni ɲɛnabɔcogo si t’a lasɔrɔ mɔgɔw ye.
Jɔyɔrɔ ka taa cɛmancɛyɔrɔ la, o ye gɛlɛya ye.
Aliw Tarawore ka fɔ la, sendikɛlikɛla, sirabakan gɛlɛya kunw Bamakɔ b’a ɲɛfɔ, dɔwɛrɛw cɛla polisi dɔw kɛcogoya, sirabakanw kɛlɛya, bisikiliw, mototakisiw fɛ.
ɛmɔgɔw ka kan ka kokɛta dɔw ta walasa sirabakanboli ka gɛlɛya.
A ko ten.
Kalabani – Kura – Dabanani siratigɛ ( dugu cɛmancɛla ) taara ɲɛ ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ ye.
Fulimini Aminata Goyita, sebagaya feerela Wɔnida sugu la.
Polisi kolatigɛla Jakaridi Jara b’a jate ko : polisiw ka maganw n’a ta bɛɛ ka sirabakan sariyaw labato, mɔgɔ dɔw b’a la ka baara gɛlɛya u la.
O de bɛ gɛlɛya kɛ dɔwɛrɛw la sirabakanboli kɔnɔ.
Sirabakan yɛlɛmana n’a ta bɛɛ, min bɛ na sirabakan ka gɛlɛya Bamakɔ, sɔrɔdasi sigibagaw bɛ gɛlɛya sɔrɔ halibi ka sɔrɔ sirabakan yɛlɛma waati nataw la.
Jɔnjɔn wɛrɛ mago bɛ kɛ Bamakɔ Nizɛri dugukolo kan.
Inza Tarawore ( degelikaramɔgɔ ) Hamani angi kɔkɔrɔdon jɛkulu y’a fɔ, zuwɛnkalo tile 29, kunnafonidilajɛ dɔ senfɛ, k’a ka ɲɛmɔgɔ ka mɔgɔ jalaki kama, ko min bɛ fɔ ko « diyagoya kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲini ye Mali basikɛtiboli federason na ».
A bɛ bisigikuma dɔw dantigɛ ka sin Hamani angi ma, n’a bɛɛ ka kɔkɔrɔdon di Kayi tɔgɔlamɔgɔ ma sɔrɔ.
Nin waati gɛlɛya la an bɛ min kɔnɔ, ni fɛn dɔ bɛ yen min kɔnɔ an bɛ ɲɛsinnen don bi, o ye Mali basikɛti ye.
An ye ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw ye jamakulu bɛɛ kɔnɔ, ɲɛmɔgɔw ka dusu kɔnɔ, Hamani angi bɛ yen, minnu cɛla.
Ka tɛmɛ k’a kɛ Mali basikɛtiboli federason perezidan ye, ka tɛmɛ k’a kɛ a ye farikoloɲɛnajɛw minisiri ye, a ka cɛsiriw fɛ, nin Kayi denmisɛn ye Mali darapo bila jan na, fɔlɔ la Afiriki (FIBA Afiriki ) la, o kɔfɛ diɲɛ basikɛtiboli cakɛda, FIBA diɲɛ kɔnɔ.
A ka kan k’a bilasira, k’a kɔkɔrɔdon don.
Yusufu Sidibe, Hamani angi kɔkɔrɔdon Jɛkulu mɔgɔ dɔ y’o fɔ.
A ka kumaw la, ni Hamani angi bɛ gɛlɛya kɔnɔ, Kayi bɛɛ de bɛ gɛlɛya kɔnɔ, fana Mali ani Afiriki bɛɛ kama.
K’a da a kan, a y’a fara a kan, Mali de bɛ sisan sɛgɛsɛgɛ, Mali de bɛ sɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛ.
Jalakiliw, k’a da a kan an bɛ sɛgɛsɛgɛliw, mara ani kiriso wɛrɛw, minnu bɛ senna, jaabiw makɔnɔ.
Ka ɲɛfɔli bɛɛ kɛ nin bisigikumaw kan, sɛbɛn kɛli kama.
Yusufu Sidibe y’o kɔkɔrɔdon.
Sɛgɛsɛgɛli caman kɔfɛ Mali basikɛtiboli federason perezidan kɔrɔ kan, laselisɛbɛn, Mbaye Konte, ye Malidenw wele k’u nin koɲɛ ta k’a sɛbɛn Hamani angi ka juguya sɛbɛn.
Burama Kamara Nin dusukunnako de ye sisan mɔgɔ minnu bɛ baarakɛjɛkulu mɔgɔw la, Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ kura Sogɛli K. Mayiga ka taama kɔfɛ Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ, Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Bubu Sise, min sigilen don.
Mɔgɔw y’a sɔrɔ nin Sogɛli ka latigɛ ye ka Bubu ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn sɔrɔ.
Mɔgɔw b’a jate ko Sogɛli yɛrɛ yɛrɛ ye Bubu mara gɛlɛya dantigɛ wa a y’a kɛlɛ k’a sɔrɔ fo ka bɔ fanga la.
A tɛ dɛsɛ ka gɛlɛya sɔrɔ a koɲɛ kan, u bolo, Sogɛli ma mago abada Bubu kolatigɛlaw ma.
O laban b’a miiri k’a fɔ ko labɛnni tɛ dɔwɛrɛ de ka kan.
U hakili b’a la ko nin taama tun bɛ kɛ ka bɔ Bubu la, hali n’o tɛ fɛn wɛrɛ ye.
Mɔgɔ dɔ tun bɛ se ka jate k’a fɔ ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn tɔgɔlamɔgɔw kan ko Sogɛli y’i mago k’i yɛrɛ nɔgɔya ani k’a kɛ cogoya ye, mɔgɔ mɔgɔ dɔ y’o ɲɛfɔ.
O n’a ta bɛɛ, u bɛ miiri k’a fɔ ko Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ ka kan ka nin siriki minɛ yaasa k’i yɛlɛma a ka baara la, bawo, waati caman tɛ yen a la.
Ibarahima Njaayi - Fɛnw don janko, i n’a fɔ sogo, tulu, sɔrɔ, sɔrɔ, ris.
Kabini waati dɔ la, an bɛ magoɲɛfɛn fɔlɔ dɔw sɔngɔw yɛlɛnni sɔrɔ, min bɛ magoɲɛfɛn fɔlɔ dɔw la, Mali sugu kɔnɔ.
O n’a ta bɛɛ, gɔfɛrɛnaman ka maganw bɛ minnu na, ka mago fɔlɔfɛnfɛn fɔlɔw sɔngɔw lataaɲɛ ani ɲɔgɔn cɛ, yaasa Mali sannikɛlaw ka nin mago fɛn ninnu sɔngɔ sɔngɔw la, minnu bɛ se ka sɔngɔ la, n’a kɛtɔla ka dɛmɛ kɛ u la.
Nka, o bɛɛ n’a ta bɛɛ, jagokɛla dɔw, minnu sɔsɔli b’u la, b’u to u ka sɔngɔ yɛlɛnni ye.
Ka sin nin cogoya ma, kumalaselisɛbɛn dɔ kɔnɔ, min labɔra dɔgɔkun tɛmɛnen kɔnɔ, Gɔfɛrɛnaman, ka tɛmɛ DEZEYƐSISE fɛ, b’a ɲini ka jama hakililatigɛ ko a b’a ka sɔrɔta lakana.
O cogo la, fɛn dɔw sɔngɔ, minnu bɛ bɔli kɛ caman na, sɔngɔ yɛlɛmana, a y’o kunnafoni kɛ.
Kumalaselisɛbɛn ka fɔ la, nin sɔngɔ dantigɛlisɛbɛnw labato, minnu bɛ tali kɛ dugukolo bɛɛ kan, tɛmɛna kɛ wajibi ye mɔgɔ bɛɛ bolo.
Nin sɔngɔw tiɲɛni kama, DEZEYƐSISE ka kumalaselisɛbɛn ye sannikɛlaw kunnafoni ko a ka kɔlɔsilikɛjɛkuluw bɛ kɛnɛ kan, yaasa k’u lakana ni ɲagaliw ye, minnu sirilen don jagoko ɲagaliw la.
O gɔfɛrɛnaman ka magan, min bɛ sɔngɔw yɛrɛmahɔrɔnya taabolo la, min sigilen don sariyasunw fɛ, minnu bɛ jagoko ɲɛnabɔli kɛ Mali jamana kɔnɔ, ka bon, a y’o ɲɛfɔ.
Yanni a ka wele bila sannikɛlaw fɛ, u ka sɔsɔli bɛɛ laseli, min sɔsɔli bɛɛ la, Diɲɛ ani ɔgɔndan ɛmɔgɔyaso ka baaradaw fɛ.
A ƐMUTure - Perezidan Emaniɛli Makorɔni b’a fanga ka bɔ Mali la n’a ka jamakuluw ye.
K’a sɔrɔ ko ultimatumu ka gɛlɛya ka waleya.
O de bɛ sɔrɔ ntɛnɛndon tɛmɛnen laseli la Kolonɛli Asimi Goyita ni Faransi tɔgɔlamɔgɔ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw cɛ.
Faransi jamana perezidan ani politikimɔgɔ Emanuyɛli Makoron tɔgɔlamɔgɔ, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la danfaralenw ncininw, minnu dilen bɛ forobakɛliw kɔnɔ.
Mali Cɛmancɛlafanga perezidan, Kolonɛli Asimi Goyita, y’o sɛbɛn.
Makɔnadiw.
O cogo la, mɛkalo tile 24 tɛmɛnen kɔfɛ Mali la, Faransi perezidan, Emanuyɛli Makoron, tun y’a ŋaniya bila ka Barikani sɔrɔdasiw senbɔ jamana kɔnɔ.
Kumaɲɔgɔnkunbɛn dɔ la karidon kunnafonidisɛbɛn ( ZIDE ) la, Faransi perezidan tun b’a sɛmɛntiya ko Faransi bɛna bɔ a ka jamakuluw bɔ, n’a y’a sɔrɔ Mali ka « silamɛya kɛcogoya ɲuman » la, Jamana kɔnɔni filanan kɔfɛ kalo tile 9 kɔnɔ.
Faransi, a tun b’a fɔ ko, ni cɛ 5100 ɲɔgɔnna ye Barikani kɔnɔ, b’a kɔkɔrɔdon Mali ma, min bɛ ka ɲɛsin ɲɔgɔn cɛjugu damatɛmɛ ma kabini san 2012 kaɲaka fanfɛ ani k’a ye jamana dugukolo lakana gɛlɛya kɔnɔ, yann’a ka taa jamana cɛmancɛ la.
Wa Mɔgɔ Makoron, i n’a fɔ IYƐNI, ka « Jamana caman, minnu tɛ se ka sɔn » dantigɛ, perezidan Ba N’Daw ani Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ, Mukutari Wani minɛni kɔfɛ.
A tɛ se ka sɔn?
An tɛmɛna!
K’a sɔrɔ ko ntɛnɛndon tɛmɛnen, i n’a fɔ Mali mɔgɔ kura ka tigiyɔrɔ fɔlɔ b’a sɛmɛntiya cogo min, Emanuyɛli Makoron ye cidenkulu dɔ wele ka Asimi Goyita ye.
ntɛnɛndon, n ye Makorɔni perezidan, Faranki Parisi ani Emirali Zan Filifu Roland ka lasigiden kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw sɔrɔ.
Anw y’a kumafalen kɛ cɛsiriko kan, minnu sirilen bɛ kɛlɛli la ka sin tɔrɔfɛnw ma ani Sahɛli lakanabaliya ma.
mɔgɔ b’o kalan Kuluba masurunnamɔgɔ ka tweet kɔnɔ.
Mɔgɔ b’u ɲininkan, o tuma, n’a bɛ se ka kɛ makɔnɔdasiw ye ncininw ye walasa k’u dusukasi.

Faransi Jamana ɲɛmɔgɔ tun y’a sɛmɛntiya o tuma k’a ye « bataki laseli » ta Afiriki tilebin ɲɛmɔgɔw ma ko « a tɛna to jamana kɔnɔ, yɔrɔ min na demokarasi sariya ani cɛmancɛlafanga tɛ yen ».
A b’a hakilijigin kɛ k’ale y’a fɔ kabini san saba « kɔfɛjɔkulu caman kɔnɔ an tun ka kan ka miiri bɔli la ».

Bruno D SECBEDJI - Jɛkulu ɲɛmɔgɔya dɔ labɛn ɲɛmɔgɔya la, k’a ɲɛsin waati yɛlɛmaniw kɛlɛli ani kɛlɛli la, o de ye tile 10 baaraɲɔgɔnye laɲini ye, min bɛ kɛ Segu la.
Mɔgɔ saba, minnu bɔra Segu Karamɔgɔyaso la, jamana kalanso, kalanso ani inini baarada cɛmancɛyɔrɔw ani mɔgɔ cɛmancɛyɔrɔw la, b’u sen don nin baarada la, min kɛra IYƐNESKO ka kɔkɔrɔdon ye.
Kɔlɔsilikɛlaw ɲɛnabɔli kɛcogoya la, Mali Jamana gɔfɛrɛnaman ye Dɔgɔtɔrɔba sɛbɛn filanan ta, min taamasiyɛnna ka ɲɛnabɔli ɲɛnabɔli ɲɛnabɔli kan min bɛ mɔgɔw bolo, ni ɲɔgɔn cogoya bɛɛ ka ɲɛnabɔli ye, ni ɲɔgɔn cogoya bɛɛ ka ɲɛnabɔli ye, ni ɲɔgɔn cogoya bɛɛ ka ɲɛnabɔli ye.
Jamana Kalanso minisiriso, ni IYƐNESKO ka dɛmɛ ye, ye kalanso labɛnni, degelikaramɔgɔw labɛnni ani degelikaramɔgɔw ɲɛnabɔli baarabolodali caman dayɛlɛ, minnu sirilen don kalanso la, k’a ɲɛnabɔli kɛ waati yɛlɛmaniw la ani kɛlɛli la.
Kɔlɔsiliw sugandili kɔfɛ, nin baaraɲɔgɔnkunbɛn bɛ fɛɛrɛ yɛrɛ-yɛrɛ sɔrɔ walasa ka kalan ɲɛmɔgɔw faamuya ani k’u waleya kɛcogoya ɲumanw la yaasa ka laselikaramɔgɔw kɛlɛli la kɛlɛli la waati cɛmancɛlafanga kɔnɔ.
Nin tile 10 baaraɲɔgɔnkunbɛn bɛ sɔrɔ baarabolodali hukumu kɔnɔ, min bɛ karidon kɛcogoya kologɛlɛyali kologɛlɛya kologɛlɛya kɔnɔ, k’a kɛ sababu ye kɛlɛli ani kɛlɛli kɛ waati yɛlɛmaniw la.
Nin baarabolodali belebele kun ye ka sigi lakɔliw kɔnɔ, ka tɛmɛ lakɔli baarabolodaliw fɛ, cogo min na den bɛɛ bɛna se ka kalan walasa ka waleyaw ta, minnu bɛ kɛlɛli ani kɛlɛli la, waati yɛlɛma kɛlɛli an’u kɔlɔsili la.
A ka kuma dayɛlɛli kɔnɔ, Jamana Kalanso minisiri sekeretɛri zenerali tɔgɔlamɔgɔ ye wele kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la mɔgɔ minnu sen b’u sen don u ka baara labɛnni kɛ ni ɲuman ye.
Nin ɲɛmɔgɔya ka kan ka kɛ ɲuman ye ani a ka laɲini ye k’a kɛlɛli daminɛ ani k’a kɛ cogoya yɛlɛmaniw kɛlɛli taabolo taabolo ye, ka tɛmɛ degelikalan ani kalanw kɛli fɛ.
A y’a kuncɛ ten.
Madamu Diko Umaru Diko, min bɛ IYƐNESKO kɔnɔn kɛnɛkow ani kɛnɛkow baarabolodaliw ɲɛmɔgɔya, y’i sinsin IYƐNESKO ka bilasirali kan Mali gɔfɛrɛnaman fɛ, a ka baaraw kɛlɛli la k’a ɲɛsin klima yɛlɛmani ma, min bɛ diɲɛ bɛɛ fanga la.
Alɛbɛri Kalambiri - Kolatigɛla Segu la. O labɛnnen kɛra zuwɛnkalo tile 24 ka taa tile 27 la Denmisɛnw ani farikoloɲɛnajɛw ɲɛnabɔli Tɔn ( APJS ) fɛ, jamanaw cɛ farikoloɲɛnajɛ ɲɛnajɛ ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn tako 5nan, min kɛra farikoloɲɛnajɛ kunkanw kɔnɔ.
yiriwali, bɛn ani hadamadenya bɛnɲini.
ani k’a ka farikoloɲɛnajɛ jɛkuluw ani farikoloɲɛnajɛ jɛkuluw fara ɲɔgɔn kan, a y’a ka lahidu bɛɛ labato.
A bilalen jamana cɛmancɛlafanga perezidan, Kolonɛli Asimi Goyita, ka ɲɛmɔgɔya kɔnɔ, ani denmisɛnw ani farikoloɲɛnajɛw minisiri fɛ, fasodenyakalan ani fasodenya ɲɛnabɔli bɛ min bolo, Mosa Agi Atahɛri, jamanaw cɛ farikoloɲɛnajɛ ɲɛnabɔli ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn tako 5nan, min kɛra zuwɛnkalo tile 24 ka taa tile 27 la, ye jamana federason caman, farikoloɲɛnajɛ jɛkuluw fara ɲɔgɔn kan Bamakɔ.
kulɔbuw, cɛsiriw ani dojo koɲɛfɔlen kɔnɔ farikoloɲɛnajɛ kuncɛw.
yiriwali, bɛn ani hadamadenya bɛnɲini.
Nin san, nin ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn labɛnna ni baara caman ye, i n’a fɔ i n’a fɔ.
3×3 basikɛtiboli ɲɔgɔndanw, Marakaña, galala ntolatan dɔ, farikoloɲɛnajɛ yɔrɔw, federasonw ani farikoloɲɛnajɛ jɛkuluw ka ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw, ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw, ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw, ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw, farikoloɲɛnajɛ yɔrɔw, ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw, Kulukɔrɔ marabolo kɔnɔn, ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn ni ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw ye, minnu sigilen don amana.
A daminɛna faraɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw ani farikoloɲɛnajɛ tɔnw ka taamasiyɛn fɛ, nin ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn dayɛlɛni ɲɛnajɛ, alamisadon zuwɛnkalo tile 24 Salamatu Mayiga farikoloɲɛnajɛ pala kɔnɔ, o kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la, Komini 4nan mɛri ka kumaw fɛ ani diɲɛ farikoloɲɛnajɛ ɲɛnajɛ ɲɛnajɛ ɲɛnajɛ ɲɛnajɛ ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu ( FIS ) labɛnnen, Mmu Si Aminata Maku Tarawore, fɛ.
Si ka fɔ la, farikoloɲɛnajɛ ye jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ ye, min kama mɔgɔ bɛ mɔgɔ ka kalan don bɛɛ, danaya ani diinɛ fɛ.
K’a fɔ ko nin ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kuncɛ ye hakililatigɛ, hakilijiginw ani kumafalenw sigi farikoloɲɛnajɛ fɛ farikoloɲɛnajɛ fɛ sɔrɔlenw kan Mali sɔrɔ ani hadamadenyako yiriwali taabolo kɔnɔ.
A ka fɔ la, FIS ye jamanaw cɛ farikoloɲɛnajɛ ɲɔgɔndan ɲɔgɔnye ye Mali kɔnɔ, min bɛ APJS ka fɛɛrɛw taabolo kɔnɔ, minnu ka laɲini ye ka degelikaramɔgɔya ɲuman sɔrɔ, k’a ɲɛnabɔcogoya ɲɛnabɔ ani bɛn ɲɛnabɔ, yaasa ka cogoya ɲumanw sigi Mali kɔnɔ, ka Diɲɛtɔnba ka yiriwali ɲɛnabɔcogoya ɲɛnabɔcogoya ɲɛnabɔcogoya ɲɛnabɔcogoya kama.
FIS kolatigɛla ka kuma kɔfɔlen kɔfɛ, jama y’a hakɛ sɔrɔ k’a kɛ kɔlɔsilikɛyɔrɔw dantigɛli ye, n’u kɔfɛ ɲɔgɔn caman ka fara ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn bolodiɲɔgɔnma kɛbagaw fɛ, i n’a fɔ OMS, UNESCO, IYƐNISEYƐFU, adwɛrɛ.
Nin FIS tako 5nan daminɛni kuntaala Denmisɛnw ani Farikoloɲɛnajɛw minisiri, Fasodenyakalan ani fasodenya ɲɛnabɔli bɛ min bolo, Mosa Agi Atahɛri, fɛ.
Mɔgɔ bɛn’a fɔ ko nin ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn hakilina belebele ye sisan an ka jamana yɔrɔ min na, k’a da a kan a bɛ bɛn hakilina sɔrɔ farikoloɲɛnajɛ fɛ, n’a bɛ bɛn hakilina sɔrɔ ni ɲɔgɔn cɛsiriw sɛbɛn ni ɲɔgɔn cɛsiriw sɛbɛn, minnu bɛ tali kɛ baarakɛbagaw ye, yaasa farikoloɲɛnajɛ kɛ bɛn taamasiyɛn ye, min ɲininen don Mali denw bɛɛ fɛ.
O de kosɔn, a ye ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn labɛnnikɛlaw barikada, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la Si Aminata Maku Tarawore.
Minisiri Agi Atahɛri ka fɔ la, nin tako bɛna danaya di farikoloɲɛnajɛ jɛkulu baarakɛbagaw ma, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la farikoloɲɛnajɛ jɛkuluw ani jɛkuluw ma.
O kɛra sababu ye k’a bɛna dɛmɛ kɛ farikoloɲɛnajɛ ɲɛnajɛ ɲɛnabɔli la ani k’a bɛna denmisɛnw ka danaya ani ɲininiw ɲinini farikoloɲɛnajɛ yɔrɔw kɔnɔ.
ɔgɔndan wɛrɛw senfɛ, 3×3 basikɛtiboli ɲɔgɔndan kɔnɔ, minnu finaliw ntolanci kɛra Lafiabugu Caba tɛnɛn na, musow kɔnɔ, Bamakɔ musow ye ɲɔgɔn sɔrɔ Komini 4nan tɔn kan, ni tɛmɛ 1-6.
Cɛw ka fan fɛ, Bamakɔ Ɛsitadi maliyɛn ye taamasiyɛn 8 – 7 sɔrɔ Falade tɔn ɲɛkɔrɔ.
Galasa ntolatan, min tun bɛ APJS mɔgɔw ɲɔgɔnna ni MINISIMA Cɛki tɔndenw ye, ye sɔrɔdasiw ka sebagaya sɔrɔ APJS kan ( 5 – 2 ).
K’a jate k’a fɔ ko nin jamanaw cɛ farikoloɲɛnajɛ ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn tako 5nan ye farikoloɲɛnajɛ ɲɛmɔgɔ caman fara ɲɔgɔn kan jamana ani diɲɛ kɔnɔ, farikoloɲɛnajɛ kɔrɔw, mɔgɔ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw, ani dɔwɛrɛw cɛla.
Safiatu Kulibali fɛ - Mɔgɔba ɲumanw ka baaraw kɔnɔ, minnu kɛra nin kalo labanw na, Konowari perezidan ni a tɔgɔtɔrɔ cɛ, dɔlakelen tora tiɲɛ kɔnɔ.
Mali Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ ani Afiriki Faransi mɔgɔ kɔrɔ,
Konowari perezidansigikalata laban senfɛ, ɔkutɔburukalo tile 31 san 2020, min ye Alasani Watara ( ADO) seginna ka sarati sabanan kama, min sɔsɔli bɛ a tɔgɔlamɔgɔw fɛ, Sumɛli Bubey Mayiga tun bɛ Sahɛli ni Sahari jamanaw ka Jɛkulu ( SEYƐN – SAD ) ka ɲɛmɔgɔya ɲɛmɔgɔya.
Kalata kɔfɛ, Mali Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ bilala Konowari perezidan fɛ Abijan.
An ka kunnafoniw ka fɔ la, cɛ fila y’a fɔ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la, ka jamana bɛnɲini kɛ cogoya ɲuman kɛ, sisan ADO tun seginna ka na, ani o la, ka Loran Bagibo seginni bali, min ɲɛsigilen tun b’a la ka ɲɛsin a ɲininiw kan.
Pari – Brugɛli - A kumafalen kɔnɔ, a y’a miiri k’a fɔ ko Sumɛli Bubayi Mayiga tun bɛ se ka kɛ nin laban na.
ADO tun ye Maki Sali ani Mahamadu Isufu ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn sɔrɔ, dɔwɛrɛw cɛla.
K’a sɔrɔ ko gɔfɛrɛnaman kuntigi kɔrɔ tɛ ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn na ni Bagibo ye ( ni min tun ye jamanaw cɛ hadamadenyakɛbagaw ka bɔlɔlɔ barokɛyɔrɔ kelenw ta) kabini san tan.
O tuma de la Giyɛli Dɛlibɛrɛli tɔgɔ y’a tɔgɔ sɔrɔ, min gɛlɛya kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la Hamɛdi Bakayoko fɛ, Konowari Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ, min fatura marisikalo tile 10.
Kɔkankow ɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ, IYƐRI Faransi ka Afiriki ni Moyɛni ɛmɔgɔyaso la, ye misiyɔn caman kɛnɛ kan, minnu cɛsiri bɛ fankelenfɛjamanaw kɔnɔ.
A bɛ jɔnjɔn fila sɔrɔ.
Bubu ka cɛɲɔgɔn cɛ,
A tolen don Bagibo la fana, a y’a to a ka taama ka taa o tuma min na o tun minɛna Hayi, o kɔfɛ Brisɛli, yɔrɔ min na perezidan kɔrɔ tun bɛ sigi k’a yɛrɛmahɔrɔnya kɔnɔ.
nowanburukalo tile 9, Dɛlberɛli taara Brisɛli.
Loran Bagibo y’a hakililatigɛ ko mɔgɔ bɛ se ka cɛfɔli kɛ ni Mali ɲɛmɔgɔ ye.
Perezidan kɔrɔ ka jaabi.
gɛlɛya si tɛ, a tun labɛnna k’u sɔrɔ.
« Mama Wodi y’a jaabi k’a fɔ ko ŋaniya si tun tɛ ka kontiw labɛn. nowanburukalo tile 11, Denbɛrɛli seginna ka Jamana ɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ ye, nin siɲɛ na Sumeyulu Bubayi Mayiga ka fara ɲɔgɔn kan.
Mɔgɔ fila, minnu cɛsiri, y’a ɲɛfɔ Bagibo la ko Alasani Watara tun labɛnnen don k’a bila ka bɔ jamana bɛnɲini kama.
Mama Wodi y’u jaabi k’a fɔ ko ŋaniya si tun tɛ ka kontiw labɛn ani k’a tun bɛ hakilina kelen na ni perezidan ye.
Kumaɲɔgɔnya labanw. Nin ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn fɔlɔ kɔfɛ, Sumɛli Bubayi Mayiga ye laselisɛbɛn dɔ bila Alasani Watara ma, min y’a dusu don k’a ka ɲɔgɔn cɛɲiɲɔgɔnya kɔlɔsili tɛmɛ.
Mɔgɔ tɛmɛnenw kɔnɔ, Giyɛli Ɛlɛli taara Brisɛli siɲɛ fila yaasa ka ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kɛ Bagibo ye.
Marisikalo tile 31 na, Jamana ɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ banna diɲɛ kiriso (SEPEYI) fɛ.
Zuwɛnkalo tile 9, Dɛlibɛrɛli seginna bagibo la siɲɛ laban na, nin siɲɛ in na Sumeyulu Bubayi Mayiga bilasira.
Jɔnjɔnw kɔnɔ, minnu kumafalenw kɛra tile damadɔ, ka tɛmɛ ɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ ka segin Abijan, zuwɛnkalo tile 17, tun bɛ yen.
a ka banki konti bɔli, a ka kɛnɛ baarakɛden kɔrɔ bilali, Kolonɛli Noribɛri Kusi Dua bilali, a ka lakana mɔgɔ tanw sigili, minnu sirilen don a kan, ani waatilabaarali dɔ, yaasa ka baaraw labɛn, a bɛna minɛn Cocody dugukolo kɔnɔ.
Farafina denmisɛnw fɛ. Kululi dakun kɔfɛ, jamana musow ka ntolatan ŋanaya ntolatan bɛ na daminɛ a dakun filanan ani laban na, kabini zuwɛnkalo tile 24 nata la, ni AYƐSI ka Kare don fɔlɔ ye.
Nin ŋanayaɲini ɲɔgɔndan kɔfɛ ni 4 ye, ntolatantɔn, min bɛna kuru hakɛ caman sɔrɔ, bɛna kɛ Mali ŋanayaɲini ye.
Mali ŋanaya kura bɛna dɔn zuluyekalo tile 14, AYƐSI ka Kare don 6nan ani laban kɔfɛ.
AS Kare dɔ, min bɛna ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn ntolatantɔn 4 fɛ, minnu bɛna ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn ta ka taa ni seginni kama, ntolatan 6 mumɛ kɔnɔ.
ŋanaya jɔnjɔn tigi, Bamakɔ Ɛsitadi maliyɛn bɛ na sɔrɔ jɔnjɔn sɔrɔ ka sin AS Ereyali ma ( Pulu A ( 2nan ), Joliba ASE ani arela Kereyatɛri 11nan ma, minnu ye Pulu B ( 1nan ani 2nan ) laban, k’u ka AYƐSI Kare sɛbɛn sɛbɛntigiya.
O kɔrɔ ye k’a fɔ ko nin ŋanayaɲini dakun laban bɛna ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kɛ ni ntolatantɔn 4 ɲumanw ye ntolatan dakun kɔnɔ.
AYƐSI ka Kare tɔgɔlamɔgɔ fɔlɔ senfɛ, ŋaniya bɛna kɛ Bamakɔ Ɛsitadi maliyɛn ye ŋanaya jɔnjɔn ye.
ka ntolatan dayɛlɛ ka sin Pulu B filanan ma, Niarela Kereyatɛri Unes ma.
O kɔfɛ, an bɛna jɔ Bamakɔ Joliba ASE Ereyali ɲɛfɔli la.
Ni kulu 4 ninnu bɛna kɛlɛ sɔrɔ, min sɔrɔla ŋanaya tɔgɔ kama, kulɔbu 4 wɛrɛw ka kan ka yɛlɛmani kɛ yaasa ka jamana ntolatan mɔgɔw sɔrɔ.
IYƐSI Buguni, SEYƐSI ( Seware ), Kulukɔrɔ AYƐSI anan ani Gawo Soni ASE ko don.
K’u labanna jɔyɔrɔ fila labanw la, minnu bɛ tali kɛ u ka kulɔbu kelenw la, nin kulɔbu 4 de tara jɔyɔrɔ filanan na.

K 11, nk 18, s 2, f 5, g 11, cd 10, ct 37, -27 AS ka Kare Tɔgɔlamɔgɔw Tɔgɔlamɔgɔw Alamisadon zuwɛnkalo tile 24 Ɛsitadi maliyɛn-Onze Kereyatɛri tɔgɔla fɔlɔ, Ɛsitadi maliyɛn-Onze Kereyatɛri tɔgɔla fɔlɔ, Ɛsitadi maliyɛn-Doliba tɔgɔla fɔlɔ, Ɛsitadi maliyɛn-Doliba tɔgɔla fɔlɔ, Ɛsitadi maliyɛn-Doliba tɔgɔla fɔlɔ, Ɛsitadi maliyɛn-Doliba tɔgɔla fɔlɔ, Ɛsitadi maliyɛn-
Marabolo kɔlɔsilikɛjɛkulu kɔnɔ, Samba tun bɛ yɛlɛma, tun bɛ yɛlɛma ka bɔ a ka sɛgɛsɛgɛyɔrɔ la ani k’i yɛlɛma kiriso kɔnɔ.
Dɔgɔkun na, a mɔgɔ tun bɛ mɔgɔ ka gɛlɛya la, a tun bɛ gɛlɛya gɛlɛya n’a muso yɛlɛma ka gɛlɛya n’a muso yɛlɛma ka gɛlɛya n’a muso yɛlɛma ka gɛlɛya n’a muso yɛlɛma ka gɛlɛya n’a muso yɛlɛma ka gɛlɛya n’a muso yɛlɛma ka gɛlɛya n’a muso yɛlɛma ka gɛlɛya n’a muso yɛlɛma ka gɛlɛya n’a muso ka gɛlɛya n’a muso yɛrɛma ka gɛlɛya n’
Kadiya muso ka gɛlɛya la, mɔgɔ tun bɛ mɔgɔ ka danaya sɔrɔ.
Nin Sidi ka mɔgɔ cɛ tun y’a ɲini ka wele bila su kɔnɔ, kasɔrɔ a tun y’i yɛrɛ bila a cɛ fɛ, min taara ka bɔ jamana kɔrɔnfɛ? Gɛlɛya tun ka kan ka dugujukɔrɔfɛnw dɔw lasɔrɔ, minnu sɔrɔla hadamadenw kɔnɔ.
Diɲɛ tun b’a sɛbɛn ni ɲɔgɔn cɛw, ɲɔgɔn cɛw sɛbɛn.
Gɛlɛya gɛlɛya tun tɛmɛna denmisɛn muso bɛɛ fɛ, waati min na a ka talifoni tun bɛ sonyali. O bɔlen kɔ yen, muso tun ma foyi si sɔrɔ ka talifoni kumafalen na.
A tun y’a yɛrɛ sɔrɔ a kɔnɔ yaasa ka fɛn min tun ka kan sɔrɔ.
K’a ɲɛfɔ, k’a fɔ k’a fɔ k’a kɛ furu ye, k’a ka danaya sɔrɔ, o tun tɛ gɛlɛya ye a yɛrɛ la.
Gɛlɛya gɛlɛya la Kadiya tun ka dɛsɛ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen ye ka ɲɛsin mɔgɔ tɔgɔ min ma kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen ye.
K’a ka waati an’a ka mɔgɔ jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ ɲini k’a ɲini k’a bɛnɲini kumaw ɲini.
A ka so kɔnɔn ko min tɛ dɔgɔyalen ye, a tun b’a la k’a bɛ sɛgɛsɛgɛli gɛlɛya sɛgɛsɛgɛ waati laban na ka jigiya sɔrɔ ko ɲɔgɔnna kɛra.
Waatiw tun bɛ ka tɛmɛ, gɛlɛya tun bɛ ka yɛlɛmɛ.
Wa a ka gɛlɛya ka bɔ a ka so la tun kɛra gɛlɛya ye.
A tun ka kɛ gɛlɛya ye min ka kan ka kɛ a cɛ ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ ye jɔyɔrɔ tɛmɛnen kɔnɔ.
A tun bɛ na kɛ gɛlɛya ye mɔgɔ bisigiyalen dɔ cɛ la, minnu tun bɛ na k’a fɔ ko a t’a yɛrɛ ma kɛnɛ kan.
Kadiya tun b’a ka hakilila kɛcogoya kɛcogoya kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya kɔnɔ ani a ka ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya kɔnɔ.
A cɛɲɔgɔn ka mɔgɔ tɔgɔlɔlɔw kɔnɔ, mɔgɔ tun ka kan ka gɛlɛya kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la.
Wa, muso ka ɲɛsinnenw kɔnɔ, min ɲɔgɔnna ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ ye, jogoɲumanya tun tɛmɛna kosɛbɛ.
A kɛtɔla ka dɔgɔya kelen ni a denmisɛn ye dɔgɔtɔrɔ fitinin kɔnɔ, a tun tɛ se k’a sɔrɔ cɛ musow yɛrɛmahɔrɔnya la.
A sigili sɔgɔma tun y’a kɛ dusukasi yɛrɛ ye min na a tun miiri k’a tun ka kan ka don bɛɛ ta ka bɔ so la.
A cɛ tun tɛ waati fila walima saba tɛ san kɔnɔ.
Kadiya tun bɛ gɛlɛya gɛlɛya kɔnɔ min tun bɛ a kan.
Nafoloko mago - Cɛmancɛyɔrɔ belebele, min ɲɔgɔnna tun b’a la, tun b’a miiri ka sin npogotigi dɔ la, ka tɛmɛ muso dɔ tun b’a miiri ka cɛɲɔgɔn cɛɲɔgɔn cɛ.
Wari min sɔrɔla ka bɔ ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw la, tun bɛ fanga sɔrɔ ka ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw kɛ.
A ka kɔlɔsiliw, jɔnjɔnw, silamɛtigiw ani jɔnjɔnw tun bɛ garidi-yɔrɔtigi dɔ fara ɲɔgɔn kan, min tun bɛ sɔrɔ kaban.
Tuma tɛmɛnen, tɔgɔw tun y’u yɛlɛma.
A baarakɛɲɔgɔnw tɔgɔlamɔgɔw tɔgɔlamɔgɔw sɛbɛn tun y’i yɛlɛmaba, i n’a fɔ a ka garidi-yɔrɔtigi.
O tun ye jaabi gɛlɛya sɔrɔ kin kɔnɔ.
San fila tun tɛmɛna, fɛn bɛɛ tun bɛ cɛ ka cɛɲɔgɔn jalakiliw bɔ a cɛɲɔgɔnw tun bɛ ka kunnafoni kɛ Kadiya yɛlɛma yɛlɛma yɛlɛma ye. Fɛn bɛɛ tun bɛ dɛmɛ kɛ ka yɛlɛma dɔ fara ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw kan.
Sɛnɛ ani mɔgɔ hakili, Samba tun b’a laɲini.
K’a kɛ waati dɔwɛrɛw ye, a tun b’a kan ka donjatesɛbɛn ɲɛsinnen don a kan.
Sisan, an tun bɛ Ayidi Ɛli Fitr ka ɲɛnajɛ fila kɔnɔ. A muso ka dusukunnamɔgɔya kofɔlenw bɛɛ tun b’a dusukunnamɔgɔya kɔnɔn, kabini kalo caman kɔnɔ, tun b’a la ka ɲɔgɔn sɔrɔ, kasɔrɔ fɔli t’a la, k’a sɔrɔ a ka ɲɔgɔnna kɔnɔ.
Baarada, i n’a fɔ mɔgɔ tun t’a la, tun tɛ se ka kɛ dɔwɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw sɛbɛnnen ye kɔnɔ.
A tun ka kan ka tɛmɛ k’a kumafalen kɛ sɔgɔma.
A gɛlɛya tun bɛ mɔgɔ kan min tun ye danaya sɛbɛn a la fo a ka donw laban na.
A tun t’a dɔn a la wa a t’a dɔn mɔgɔ wɛrɛ t’a la.
O n’a ta bɔlen na, hɛrɛ kunw dayɛlɛna a bolo, min tun t’a fɛ k’a sɔrɔ i n’a fɔ a ka filanan, nka a tun bɛ denmisɛn min bɔra u ka kanu na.
A ka cɛɲɔgɔnw ka gɛlɛyaw kan ani kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la a ka denmisɛn min tun y’a yɛlɛmana Bamako nin kin kɔnɔ, yɔrɔ min na a muso bɛna sigi, a tun y’i sɔrɔ k’i sɔn a furu hakilina ma, n’a kɛra cogoya ye k’a yɛrɛ bila, n’a tun bɛ ɲɔgɔn cogoya kɔnɔ, n’a tun bɛ ɲɛmɔgɔya ɲɛnabɔli sariyaw ɲɛnabɔ. Kadiya tun tɛ yɛrɛmahɔrɔ ye k’a ka ɲɛnabɔli ɲɛnabɔ.
a cɛ, min tɛ dɔgɔya, tun tɛ se ka ɲɔgɔn sɔrɔ a la ni ɲɔgɔn cɛjugu ye.
Nka, kabini diinɛ furu tɛmɛnenw la, Samba ntolatanna ɲuman tun bɛ sɔrɔ denmisɛn naaniw la walasa ka jɔnjɔnw di, musow kɔnɔ, dusukunw, wɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw, sinsinw, kulukuluw, ɲɔgɔnfuruw ani ɲɔgɔnfuruw di.
O fɛn ninnu lakɔlɔsili bɛɛ, Matu tun y’u sɔrɔ kasɔrɔ a ma waati sɔrɔ k’a ɲininkan dantigɛ.
O caman tun b’a la k’a fɔ k’a ka fɛn mago b’a la, kasɔrɔ a ka mɔgɔ fɛn minnu tun b’a la.
Mɔgɔ bɛɛ, min laban b’a dɔn bonya, ɲumanya, hakili la, tɛna gɛlɛya sɔrɔ.
Kadiya tun tɛ yɔrɔ jan ka nin ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn sɔrɔ.
kalo damadɔ kɔnɔ, ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn ɲuman tun b’a to a ka san 26 ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw bɛɛ bila ɲɔgɔn kan.
Sibiri tun bɛ mɔgɔw ka jɛkulu dɔ la, minnu tun bɛ jɔnjɔn sɔrɔ a ɲɛ na ani a kɔnɔn.
Kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya, min tɛmɛnen don, n’a ka cɛɲɔgɔn cɛ tun y’a latigɛ k’a ka Kadiya baarakɛyɔrɔw lasɔrɔ waati bɛɛ.
Sibiri, min tun bɛ gɛlɛya gɛlɛya suguya kɔnɔ, tun y’i sɛgɛsɛgɛ ko a tun t’a furu walima a furu si tun t’a la.
Ka dɔgɔn o la, a tun ye hakililatigɛw di o siratigɛ la.
A ɲɛfɔli laban na, cɛ dɔ tun bɛ ɲininkali ɲini a la, min kɛra yɛlɛmaba ye.

a tun y’o fɔ ni gɛlɛya ye.
A jaabi tun ye nɔgɔyali kosɛbɛ.
Kadia y’a sɛmɛntiya ne ye mɔgɔ kelen ye, a ma den sɔrɔ.
Samba tun t’a miiri ka gɛlɛya nin bisigikuma kan.
Kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la, a tun ka mago k’i sɔrɔ taama gɛlɛn ani mago gɛlɛn kɔfɛ.
Dɔgɔkun tɛmɛnen, a ka batariw tun bɛna jɔyɔrɔ kosɛbɛ walasa ka dusukunnakow dayɛlɛ.
Kadiya tun y’a ɲini ka bɔ a kanu la, ka bɔ kiriso la tɛmɛnen kɔnɔ, n’o ma kɛ, a ko cogoya nɔgɔyalenw kɛra sababu ye.
A tun b’a ban ni ɲangata ye waati caman.
A kɔrɔtalen tun y’i pereperelatigɛ.
O la, a tun y’a ɲɔgɔn fɛ, n’a y’a yɔrɔ ka bɔ a ka so kɔnɔ, n’a y’a ka mɔgɔ yɛrɛw bɛɛ lasɔrɔ, minnu sɔrɔ tɛmɛnen don a cɛ ka bɔli kɔfɛ.
Zɔrizi Faransuwa Tarawore - A ka tile 3 kɔlɔsili senfɛ Mali dugukolo kan.
ko Kameruni ntolatanna kɔrɔ, Samuyɛli Eto’o Fili y’a lahidu k’a ka Sefa wari miliyɔn 20 dɛmɛ kɛ Mali Jɛkulu miiri dɛsɛbɛnw (AMALIDEYƐMU ) ma Bamakɔ komini 4nan kɔnɔ.
A weleyalen Mamadu Lamini Sangare fɛ n’a bɛ fɔ a ma Mɔmu, Parisi, Bubakari Sidiiki Sangare ( BSS ) kupu finali belebele la, Duala denni y’a lasɔrɔ alamisadon zuwɛnkalo tile 11 san 2021, Modibo Keyita Senu Jɔnjɔnfɛjɔyɔrɔ la.
Karidon zuwɛnkalo tile 13 san 2021, walasa ka hakililatigɛ di Bamakɔ, Samuyɛli Eto’o Fili ye BESEYƐSI tɔn bilasira Lafiabugu AYƐMƆLIDEYƐMU la.
Nin taama tɔgɔlamɔgɔ belebele senfɛ nin mɔgɔ minnu ka dɛsɛ ani n’u ka dɛsɛ ye, ɲɔgɔndɛmɛ ka wele b’a lahidu k’an ka wari miliyɔn 20 don, kabini ntɛnɛndon zuwɛnkalo tile 14, ani ka denmusonin, min ka dɛsɛ tɛ dɛsɛ labɛn, min ka kan ka taa Ɛsipaɲi, a ka ɲɛnabɔliw kama.
Laji Adama, tɔn mɔgɔ dɔ, min ɲɔgɔnna an ka dɛmɛnenw fɛ, y’a hakililatigɛ k’a fɔ ko Samuyɛli Eto’o Fili, a ka na, y’u ka Sefa wari miliyɔn 10 sɛmɛntiya.
Yaan’a k’a dantigɛ ko a b’a lahidu ka Sefa wari miliyɔn 10 minnu tora kabini san nata daminɛ.
O bɔlen kɔ yen, Kameruni kɔrɔ y’a dantigɛ Afiriki jɔnjɔn nata kan ko a ka jamana b’a labɛn ka san nata labɛn.
Kameruni Jamana ani Kameruni mɔgɔw ye baara ɲuman kɛ.
An ye gɛlɛyaw dɔn, kalo damadɔ bɛ yen, nka o bɛɛ bɔ an kɔfɛ.
Kameruni bɛ se ka ɲini ka diɲɛ jɔnjɔn dɔ labɛn.
A y’o dantigɛ.
Diɲɛ ntolatan ntolatan ntolatan ntolatan finali dɔ la.
Nin finali kɛra a ka don kɔfɛ, sibiridon zuwɛnkalo tile 12 san 2021, Lafiyabugu Sofa ntolatankɛnɛ kan.
O ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn senfɛ, labɛnnen waati kɔfɛ, celu tun ye 0 – 0 ye.
Kɔlɔsiliw kɔfɛ ni kuruw ye, Kapu Lafiabugu tɔn bɛna nin ɲɔgɔndan fɔlɔ ɲɛnajɛ sɔrɔ, ni Dakaraka motow kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn ɲɔgɔn kan, k’a da Sefa wari miliyɔn kelen kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen tɔn kama ( Hamudali tɔn ASAPIN ) ma.
Walasa k’a sɔrɔ ka kɛ nin ko ye mɔgɔ sɛbɛnnikɛlaba ye, Samuyɛli Eto’o y’a yɛrɛ sɛbɛnna a yɛrɛ kan yɔrɔ kɔnɔ min y’a ban diɲɛmɔgɔw ma.
Lamini BAGAYOGO - Bulkasumbugu Kulubuleni kin, Bamakɔ disiriki Komini 1nan kɔnɔ, tun bɛ binni na jumadon in na.
K’a kɛ sababu ye, sigida mɔgɔw y’u yɛlɛma alamisadon tɛmɛnen kɔnɔ, walasa k’u sɔrɔ u ka sinsɛnni yɔrɔ minɛnna bar-yɔrɔ dɔ dayɛlɛni ma.
Fɛn bɛ daminɛna alamisadon kɔlɔsili kɔfɛ, tuma min na sɛkisɛdi belebele mɔgɔw, minnu ɲɛmɔgɔya bɛ Imamu ɲɛmɔgɔya fɛ, y’u yɛrɛ bila hadamaden Salifu Keyita ka so la, k’u ka sɔsɔli kɛli kɛ u ka baara sigili la, k’a ka kuleta yɔrɔ n’u ka baarakɛyɔrɔ lakodɔnnenya la.
N’o tɛ barokɛyɔrɔ dɔ dayɛlɛli la Bulkasumbugu dɔgɔtɔrɔso ɲɛkɔrɔ.
Salifu Keyita, sɔrɔdasiw gɛlɛya.
an t’a bɛnkansɛbɛn na bar dɔ dayɛlɛli kama, min bɛ sɛkisɛbɛn na.
Mɔgɔ minnu bɛ tɔgɔlamɔgɔw ɲɛsinnen don.
A tɛmɛnen kɔnɔ, arɔndiseman 12nan polisi kulu dɔ ye yɔrɔ bila yɔrɔw la walasa k’a ɲɛsin diinɛw ka nin bɔli ɲɔgɔnna cogoya ma.
Sɔrɔdasiw b’u bolo, waati dɔw kɔnɔ.
y’u ka bɛnkansɛbɛn dantigɛ wa u ma dɛsɛ k’u ka dusukasi dantigɛ.
U ye barow ani bɛnɲini yɔrɔ wɛrɛw fara ɲɔgɔn kan u ka komini kɔnɔ.
O waati la, hadamaden Salif Keyita ma kuma fɔ koɲɛ kan halibi.
T. KAMARA A ka lakanabaliya kɔnɔ, a ka lakanabaliya bɛɛ kɛlɛli la, Kayi arɔndiseman 2nan polisiso, min ɲɛmɔgɔya b’a ɲɛmɔgɔya polisi Komisɛri kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen Mustafaa Jakité fɛ, y’a sinsin Kulun – Bankasisi taabolo siratigɛlaw kan, n’u bɛ tɛmɛ Dag – Digi jɔnjɔn jɔnjɔn fɛ.
K’a da polisi kunnafonisunw kan, mɛkalo tile 16 ka taa tile 17 san 2021, sɔgɔma nɛgɛkanɲɛ 2 ɲɛfɛ, kunnafonidila dɔ, min tɔgɔ tɔgɔla, y’a lase Kayi arɔndiseman filanan polisiso la, k’a fɔ sirabakanbagaw ka cɛkulu dɔ bɛ Kulun – Bankasisi taamasiyɛn kan, ka tɛmɛ Dag – Digi jɔnjɔn jɔnjɔn fɛ.
Ani k’a fara a kan ko nin binkannikɛlaw tun ye mɔgɔ dɔw tali kɛ kaban u ka fɛnw la.
O tɛmɛnen kɔnɔ, Kayi arɔndiseman 2nan polisiso ka ɲininikɛkulu dɔ y’a ta yɔrɔw la yaasa ka kow lakodɔn ani ka mɔgɔ bisigilenw minɛ.
A yɔrɔ kɔnɔ, sɛgɛsɛgɛlikɛlaw y’a jira k’a fɔ ko mɔgɔ wɔɔɔrɔ tun bɛ mɔgɔ wɔrɔ lakodɔnnenw la mɔgɔ fila fɛ, minnu bɛ maramafɛn belebele dɔ fanga kɔnɔ ( sansi bɛɛ nɛgɛsɛgɛli kelen, fɛnsɛgɛli lakodɔnnen) ani moto saba lakodɔnnen don so kɔnɔ.
Kuru dɔ tun bɛ ka tɛmɛ Gudɔrɔni kɔnɔ, o kuru dɔ tun labɛnnen don plakɛ kelen na, wa laban wɛrɛ tun bɛ kɛ binkannikɛlaw dɔ fɛ.
U tun b’a kɛ nin jɔnjɔn ye walasa ka motobolow bɔ, yann’u ka bila u ka sɔrɔw la.
U ɲininkalenw ani ɲininkalenw kɔnɔ, a b’a jira k’a fɔ k’a fɔ k’u bolibaga fila y’u jaabi Bama Guta (san 18) ani Sumayila Togo tɔgɔw ma (san 24), lakɔlɔsilikɛlaw bɛɛ.
U bilala polisiso la, sɛgɛsɛgɛliw kɛlenw kama, sɛgɛsɛgɛlikɛlaw fila sɔnna kow la, kasɔrɔ u ma jalaki sɔrɔ.
O la, sɛgɛsɛgɛli ɲɛmɔgɔya kɔfɛ, u bilala Kayi Arɔndiseman 2nan polisiso ka sɛgɛsɛgɛli kunnafoni kɔfɛ, mɛkalo tile 18 san 2021.
U bilala u bilali sarati kɔnɔ.
Sisan, u bɛ kumafalen kɛ u ka sugandili kan dugujukɔrɔfɛnw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, arayiw ka galabu cɛmancɛyɔrɔ cɛmancɛyɔrɔ la.
Bubakari Payitawo Cɛmancɛlafanga Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ, Sogɛli Kokala Mayiga, ka kan ka don bɛɛ a ka kɔrɔfɛjɔw ban.
Ni walasa ka jamana jɔnjɔn sɔrɔ, o b’a fɔ ko a tɛ labɛnnen ye baara kama.
Baara tɔgɔlamɔgɔ, min ye fanga juguya ni ATT ani IBEKA hukumu kɔnɔ, ka kan ka hakilijigin sɛbɛn ni ɲɛnabɔcogo sɔrɔ jamana mago bɛ min kan.
K’a kɛ Ɛmusɛnki Ɛrɛfupe tɔgɔlamɔgɔ ye, min ye Mali jamana ka gɔfɛrɛnaman cogoya sɛgɛsɛgɛ ani k’a sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛ, yann’a ka IBEKA ban, Sogɛli ka kan ka hakilijigin dɔ sɔrɔ, cogo min bɛ tali kɛ cogo min na.

Isimayɛli AYIDARA fɛ.
Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Bubu Sise ye Jamana ani Demokarasi Kelenyatɔn ( IYƐRIDE ) sugandi k’a ka walisiw bila.
IBEKA Minisiri ɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ ani laban, fo ka taa san 2018 utikalo tile 18 fanga sɔrɔ, ye Jene bolofara sugandi, a ka dugukolo sigi, i n’a fɔ a ka daminɛko ta. Nka, tiɲɛ na, bolofara sɔrɔkow sekeretɛri jɔyɔrɔ, min taara a la, bɛ i n’a fɔ perezidansigikalata ɲɛmɔgɔya daminɛ taamasiyɛnnen tɛ sɔrɔ.
Nin ye sebagaya fɔlɔ ye kaban, IBEKA Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ y’a ka donni fɔlɔfɔli kɛ fanga kuntigi fatura ka pariti la.
Mamadu Igɔri Jara seginni tun ye bankɛri kɛ cɛbɔ ye, min tun bɛ degelikaramɔgɔya makɔnɔ.
O tuma, IYƐRIDE, n’a ka ɲɛmɔgɔ fatura ka mɔgɔ jɔnjɔn na, tun tɛ se ka mɔgɔ jɔnjɔn sɔrɔ, min bɛ se ka ɲɛmɔgɔya dɛsɛbɛn, min bɛ se ka ɲɛmɔgɔya dɛsɛbɛn kɛ.
IBEKA ka nafolokow ka Hotel ɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ, yɔrɔ min na a tun bɛ Bubu Sise ɲɛmɔgɔya kɔrɔ, min tun bɛ san 2018 perezidansigikalata cɛbɔya kɔrɔ, ka sin a ka ɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ ma, tun kɛra dɔgɔkun damadɔ fɛ Sumayila Sise ka fatuli gɛlɛya kɔfɛ.
O cogo de la, Bubu Sise ka donni koɲɛ tun bɛ mɔgɔw kɔnɔ kabini kalo caman, hali tuma min na dugubakɔrɔfɛrɛnaman kɔrɔ tun donna yɛlɛmaba kɔnɔ walasa ka bɔlɔlɔsila la, min tun b’a ɲɛsin, k’a ɲɛfɔli ɲinini kama.
Pariti mɔgɔ denmisɛnw caman tun y’u yɛrɛ yɛrɛ sɔrɔ ƐMISƐNKI – ƐRƐFIPE kɔnɔ, yɔrɔ min na pariti y’a ka ɲɛmɔgɔya, min ye Mali fanga fɔlɔ ye, yɛrɛ sɔrɔ, yɛlɛma.
FSD, hali n’o ɲɛmɔgɔya bɛ Sogɛli Kokala Mayiga fɛ waati kɔnɔ, ƐMISƐMU 5 Fɛrɛtigi ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu kolatilenna tun bɛ i ko faraɲɔgɔnkankulu, min sigilen don IYƐRIDE kɔnɔ, ka tɛmɛ pariti tun ma don faraɲɔgɔnkankulu la.
Tiɲɛ bɛɛ la, Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Bubu Sise bɛ mɔgɔ jɔyɔrɔ belebele bila pariti kɔnɔ ani min ka kan ka jate walasa ka fanga ni ɲɔgɔn cɛsiri cɛsiri, k’a da a kɔnɔ ani ɲɔgɔn cɛsiri kan bawo, hali n’a ta bɛɛ, Minisiri ɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ kɔkɔrɔdonbagaw bɛ politikitɔn kelen ɲɛmɔgɔw ɲɛnabɔ.
Bubu Sise ka wele bila ɲɛsinnenw tun bɛ i n’a fɔ fɛn wɛrɛ ye min bɛ se ka sɔrɔ, walima ka tɛmɛ ka pariti hakililatigɛ caman na perezidansigikalata nata kɔnɔ.
Jɔnjɔn, min sɔsɔli bɛ walima min jigi b’a la?
O n’a ta bɛɛ, garidi kɔrɔ tun b’a la k’a fɔ pariti kelenya ɲɛmɔgɔya la, a tun y’a fɔ k’a hakililatigɛ k’a fɔ k’a fɔ ko perezidansigikalata nata cɛbɔyɔrɔw tun bɛ dayɛlɛ jɔyɔrɔtigiya kɔnɔ, n’a y’a sɛbɛn sɛbɛntigiya ye, n’a tɛ sɛbɛnnen tɛ mɔgɔw ye.
Kɔfɛjɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ, IYƐRIDE kɛra kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya ye pariti ncininw ani politikimɔgɔw, minnu sirilen don, min bɛ ɲɔgɔnna kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la.
Nka filɛlikɛla caman b’a hakililatigɛ mɔgɔ kura ka nafoloko kɛnɛ kan, min tɛ dɛsɛ.
K’a kɛ tiɲɛ ye walima k’a kɛ tiɲɛ ye, Bubu Sise fana makɔnɔna k’a ka degelikalan sɛbɛn bɛɛ walima fan dɔ fɛ, min nafoloko fanba tun bɛ da a perezidan fatura mɔgɔ kelen kan.
Garidi denmisɛn, min ye baara caman kɛ Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ ka na, sumayila Sise cɛɲɔgɔnjugu kɔrɔw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛɲɔgɔn cɛ, minnu bɛ nin fanga ni ɲɔgɔn cɛsiri sɔrɔ degelikaramɔgɔw kɔnɔ.
O cogo kelen na, garidi min tun bɛ cɛ, min tun labɛnna Mamadu Igɔri Jara kan waati kɔnɔ, y’a sɔrɔ nin waati kɔnɔn ni ɲɔgɔn cɛbɔw bɔli ye.
Zenerali Sɛki Jara ka den, SEDEYAWO ka kɔfɛjɔyɔrɔw ɲɛmɔgɔ, a ka fatuli gɛlɛya kɔnɔni waati kɔnɔn awiriyɔnna kasaara dɔ kɔnɔn Nizɛri, tun b’a yɛrɛ ye cɛbɔ ka degelikaramɔgɔw kɔnɔ ani IBEKA ka fatuli ɲɛsigi, san 2013 ani san 2018 perezidansigikalataw la.
Tiɲɛ na, IYƐRIDE kelenya bɛ i n’a fɔ cɛsiriko ye min jɔda ka jɔda jɔda bɛɛ ka tɛmɛ perezidansigikalata nata ɲɛ, Bubu Sise ka kan ka ɲɔgɔn fɔlɔ ka ɲɔgɔn sɔrɔ wa o kɔlɔsili bɛ na sɔrɔ tiɲɛ na!
Musa Ture - Gawo marabolo gɔfɛrɛnɛri y’a latigɛ k’a jira k’a fɔ k’a bɛ ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn sɔrɔ ni lakanabaliya ye, min bɛ ka ɲɛsin a ka jamana dugukolo kɔnɔ.
Sɔrɔko baarakɛbaga Abudulayi Kone ka binni kɔfɛ, n’a tɔgɔ bɔ a tɔgɔ tɔgɔ la Abudulayi Oputain ka binni kɔfɛ, a ka binni kɔrɔfɛ, Kolonɛli Sidiki Samake y’a to kokɛcogo saba fɛ.
Fɔlɔ ye dugukolo sigili ye, min bɛna kɛ, kabini nin ntɛnɛndon, wa min bɛna tile tan ni duuru kɔnɔ, min bɛna ta, min bɛna segin ka segin, jamana ani mɔgɔw ka kannabilaw bɛna kɛ fanga kɔnɔ, min bɛna kɛ sɔgɔma nɛgɛkanɲɛ 21 ni sɔgɔma nɛgɛkanɲɛ 5 cɛ.
Kɔlɔsiliw tɛ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw ye marabolo sɛbɛnnen kɔnɔ.
Walasa k’a ka kiri sɔrɔli kɛnɛ kan, marabolo mara ɲɛmɔgɔyaso y’a latigɛ k’a bɔli kɛ walasa ka mɔgɔw ka maramafɛnw yɛlɛma ka taa denmisɛnw ka ntolatanw ye forobakɛliw senfɛ.
Walasa k’a ɲɛnabɔ a koɲɛ kan, san 2021 feburuyekalo tile 12 latigɛlisɛbɛn n° 0057 b’a ban ntolatanna ɲɛnajɛw ɲɛnajɛ ɲɛnajɛ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la ntolatanna ɲɛnajɛw ɲɛnajɛ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya kɔnɔ.
Mɔgɔ minnu bɛ nin ban sariyasun sɛbɛn sɔsɔ, kasɔrɔ ɲangiliw tɛ minnu bolodalen don a siratigɛ la, b’u bila minɛnni na ani polisi ka maramafɛn kɛli kokɛcogow la, hali ni maramafɛn minɛnen bɛ tali kɛ ka bolimafɛn kɛ bolimafɛn kelen ye, min tɛ mɔgɔ sɔrɔ.
O tɛ fɛn bɛɛ ye.
Gawo gɔfɛrɛnɛri ka kokɛta kologɛlɛw fana bɛ yɔrɔ minnu tɔgɔ tɛ mɔgɔ tɔgɔ tɛmɛnenw ye.
K’a fara maramafɛntigiw ani lakanakɛbagaw ka bolodiɲɔgɔnw kɔfɛ, walima u ka jamanaw cɛ bolodiɲɔgɔnw tɔgɔlamɔgɔw kɔfɛ, bolimafɛn bɛɛ minɛnen t’a ta ka taama dugukolow kɔnɔ walima ka dugukolow kɛlɛw, dugukolow kɛlɛw, mɔgɔw cɛ, dɔwɛrɛw cɛla.
A b’a jira k’a fɔ ko sigida sariyasɛbɛn kuraw bɛ i n’a fɔ u b’a fɔ u tɛ se ka kɛ sababu ye dugukolo kɔnɔ, min kɔlɔsili bɛ jamana fanga bolo, min bɛ waati bɛɛ kɔnɔ.
Nka, u ka kanu bɛna sɔrɔ ka lakanako wulikajɔ sɔrɔ jamana bɛ min na ani minnu tɛ min na.
Keyita - A kɛra foroba ye, kumakanw, minnu tun sirilen bɛ kabini waati caman, labanna k’u kɛ tiɲɛ ye.
Mali Minisiri ɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ, Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Bubu Sise ye a ka walisiw bila IYƐRIDE la, Sumayila Sise bugunatigɛ pariti la.
A sigira sibiridon zuwɛnkalo tile 26 san 2021, ka Jene IYƐRIDE bolofara sɔrɔko sɛbɛnnikɛlaba ye.
Mali perezidansigikalata cɛbɔ kɔrɔ Mamadu Igɔri Jara ka donni kɔfɛ IYƐRIDE la, Mali Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ, Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Bubu Sise, sɔrɔ ani nafolokow minisiri kɔrɔ, y’a ka walisiw bila pariti belebele ye.
A sigira Jene IYƐRIDE bolofara sɔrɔko koɲɛw sekeretɛri la.
A ka donni labɛnna, sibiridon zuwɛnkalo tile 26 san 2021, Jene pariti bolofara lajɛrɛ kama.
A ko cogoya la, pariti ɲɛmɔgɔya ye cidenkulu dɔ wele walasa ka baaraw kɔlɔsili.
O ye forobabaara ye, Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Bubu Sise sigira Jene IYƐRIDE bolofara sɔrɔko sɛbɛnnikɛlaba ye.
A bolofara ka lajɛba baaraw ɲɛmɔgɔya tun bɛ U. ƐRIDE ka jamana biro perezidan, Madani Tarawore, Befɔni Sise, ani Sekeretɛri zenerali kɔkan, Gagu Dukure, ka ɲɛmɔgɔya fɛ.
O ye bataki ye, min tun bɛ se ka kalan Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ, Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Bubu Sise, ka Facebook sanfɛ.
A bilalen an ka dɔgɔtɔrɔw fɛ, sibiridon zuwɛnkalo tile 26 san 2021, k’a ka jaabiw sɔrɔ nin don na, IYƐRIDE Sekeretɛri zenerali, Dawuda Ture, y’a jira k’a fɔ ko pariti dayɛlɛna donni bɛɛ la.
IYƐRIDE ye pariti ye min dayɛlɛ kabini a sigili la.
An ka sɛbɛnw dayɛlɛna senbɔliw la.
Dɔnni bɛɛ ye weleli ye.
Pariti de bɛ dayɛlɛ Malidenw bɛɛ ma ani hali Afiriki mɔgɔw ma minnu bɛ Mali la.
Min ye pariti cɛbɔ sugandili ye san 2022 perezidansigikalata kama, IYƐRIDE sekeretɛri zenerali, Dawuda Ture, y’a dantigɛ ko nin ko in bɛna labɛn waati nata la.
Waati nata, mɔgɔ bɛ wele bila cɛbɔya la, ni tɔndenw bɛ se ka wele bila cɛbɔya la, taabolow bɛ yen walasa ka cɛbɔya sɔrɔ.
A y’a kuncɛ ten.
Agibu Sogodogo ka fɔ la, « N ka kanu tun bɛ ka kɛ n ka kin cɛ kasobon na, nka ni ntolatan ye, n bɛ n ka jamana sɔrɔbagaw cɛ la » Bariselɔni ntolatanna kɔrɔ bolo, diɲɛ kɔnɔ, ko ɲuman ye, o ye ka sɛmɛntiya mɔgɔ wɛrɛw la.
« Kabini waati dɔ la, ne y’a faamu ko mɔgɔ wɛrɛw bilasirali ye ko ye jɔda jɔda ye dɔgɔkun kɔnɔ.
I n’a fɔ n ka mɔgɔba Bubakari Sidiki Sangare, BƐSIYƐSI perezidan, y’o kɛ ni ntolatan ɲɔgɔndan labɛnni ye denmisɛnw kama.
Nin dusukunnako, denmisɛnw ye min sɔrɔ, nin ɲɔgɔndan fɛ, tɛ sɔngɔ sɔrɔ, ani o de kosɔn, n b’a ɲini aw fɛ, ka tɛmɛ ka denmisɛnw dɛmɛ kɛ Mali ka hɛrɛ kama.
Nin kɛlɛ kama, ne labɛnnen don ka aw bilasira », a y’o ɲɛfɔ.
A kɛtɔla k’a ka baara kan, Duala denni y’a dantigɛ k’a bɔra denmisɛn dɔ la, min y’a ŋaniya dɛsɛ waati dɔw la.
« Ne ye kin kɔnɔn den ye, n ka kanu tun bɛ n ka kin cɛmancɛ kaso la, nka ni ntolatan ye, n ye n ka jamana nafasabagaw cɛ.
Denmisɛnw, minnu ye BSS jɔnjɔn finali tan, tun nisɔndiyara kosɛbɛ n ye, nka u ma faamuya cogo min kɛra san 27 kɔnɔ, n tun b’u jɔyɔrɔ la.
N tun ka dɛsɛ ye, kasɔrɔ n tun t’a ɲini t’a la waati t’a la, nka don dɔ tun bɛ n ka ntolatan kɛ.
N ye nin sababu sɔrɔ ka taa n kɛlɛ ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ dɔw ye ani fana n y’a hakili yɛrɛ sɔrɔ ka baara gɛlɛya.
O kosɔn, ne b’a fɔ ne yɛrɛ waati dɔw la ko ɲɛsigi ye baara ye », a y’a da tulow kan, yann’a ka fara a kan ko ale y’i kɛlɛ, hali n’a sɔrɔ a ma nɔgɔya.
« A jɔnjɔn jɔnjɔn bɛ dɔgɔya kɔnɔ, o ye k’i mɔgɔ jɔyɔrɔtigiya.
Ne y’a daminɛ siɲɛ caman wa ne hakili bɛ don min na ne y’a fɔ n ka fa ma ko n bɛna baarasɛbɛn bolonɔbilasɛbɛn bolonɔbilasɛbɛn bolonɔbilasɛbɛn bolonɔbilasɛbɛn bolonɔbilasɛbɛn bolonɔbilasɛbɛn bolonɔbilasɛbɛn bolonɔbilasɛbɛn bolonɔbilasɛbɛn bolonɔbilasɛbɛn bolonɔbilasɛbɛn bolonɔbilasɛbɛn bolonɔbilasɛbɛn bolonɔbilasɛbɛn bolonɔbilasɛbɛn bolonɔbilasɛbɛn bolonɔbilasɛbɛn bolonɔ
N ka fa y’a fɔ n ka den ma, an tɛna dɔgɔya sɔrɔ abada.
San damadɔ kɔfɛ, ne tun bɛ fɛn minɛ kalo kɔnɔ, n tun bɛ fɛn minɛ filanan kɔnɔ ani n y’a fɔ n ka fa ma o tuma o yɔrɔ de ye Kɛlɛyako ye.
Ne bɛ fɛ ka kunnafoni dɔ kɛ i ye.
Mɔgɔ min b’a ka nafoloko lakɔlɔsi a ka so kasɔrɔ foyi si ma kɛ, nin nafoloko tɛ yɛlɛmana.
Mɔgɔ min bɛ jɔyɔrɔ bila banki la, hali ni o ye 20% sɔrɔ, a bɛ sɔrɔ dɔgɔya.
O de ye ne kɛ n bɔli la Reyali Madiritɔri, yɔrɔ min na n tun tɛ ntolatan ta ka taa Mɔriɲiki, yɔrɔ min na n y’a daminɛ ka ntolatan daminɛ.
Nin sababu ye ne sɔrɔ ni bɔlɔlɔsili ye dɔgɔkun kelen-kelen bɛɛ, o de y’a to ne ka kɛ cogo min ye bi », a y’o fɔ.
Ani k’a ɲini mɔgɔ denmisɛnw fɛ u ka dusu sɔrɔ ka latigɛ ɲumanw ta diɲɛ kɔnɔ.
Samuyɛli Eto’o Fili y’a ka kuma kuncɛ ni pereperelatigɛ k’a fɔ ko Mali ye jamanaw dɔlakelen ye minnu na bagabagalenw ye diɲɛ kɔnɔ.
« Bi, an tɛ se ka sɔn ka kɛ dɔgɔya ye, nka an b’a la k’a da a kan an b’a sɔn.
Ka bagabagali ye hakilina dɔ ye ani wariko t’a la ka wari sɔrɔ, nka hakilina dɔ ye », a y’o pereperelatigɛ.
Mahamadu Tarawore.
An ka jamana lakanako cogoya bɛ gɛlɛya kan ka tɛmɛ gɛlɛya kan bawo tɔrɔnnabilaw kɛra Mali jama dɔgɔtɔrɔw ka don bɛɛ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen ye.
Buguni kɔlɔsilikɛyɔrɔ, min bɛ polisikɛyɔrɔ, Duumani, zandarama ani Sɛnɛkɛyɔrɔ kɛyɔrɔsilikɛyɔrɔ la, kɛra sɔrɔdasi dɔ ye, sibiridon don ka taa karidon mɛkalo tile 30 tɛmɛnen, sɔgɔma nɛgɛkanɲɛ 3 waati kɔnɔ, min kɛra sɔrɔdasi mɔgɔw fɛ, minnu tɛ mɔgɔ lakana ɲɛmɔgɔw ka kɛcogoya lakana, n’a kɛra, juguman na, mɔgɔ duuru kɛra, polisi kɔlɔsilikɛbaga dɔ bɛ minnu na, ani fasoden
Kunnafonisunw bɛ bɛnɲɔgɔn na, sɔrɔdasiw y’u na motow la kulu fila kɔnɔ.
Jɛkulu fɔlɔ taara peyazi jɔyɔrɔ la ani filanan taara polisi jɔyɔrɔ la.
Ani k’a tɛmɛna kɛ k’a fɔ ko n’u bila ka jɔyɔrɔ kɛnɛyɔrɔ la, sɔsɔlikɛlaw, minnu tun bɛ peyazi jɔyɔrɔ la, y’u ka dɛmɛ di.
O la, u ka maramafɛnw sɔrɔli ye dusukasi sɛbɛn bila.
Wa nin yɛlɛnni kɔnɔ, mɔgɔ minnu tun sigilen don polisi jɔyɔrɔ la, y’a daminɛ ka sɔrɔ jama kan.
U ka murutili gɛlɛya kɔnɔ, sɔrɔdasiw ye mɔgɔ duuru ku, jamana polisi tɔgɔlamɔgɔ dɔ bɛ minnu na.
U ye mobili fila wuli fana.
Nin tariku kɔnɔ, o ye, ko nin jamakulu y’a sɔrɔ ka nin lakanabaara ɲɛmɔgɔya sɔrɔ ani k’u yɛlɛma tiɲɛ na, kasɔrɔ maramafɛntigiw ani lakanakɛbagaw ka kɛlɛya si si t’a la.
Juguman na ko, i n’a fɔ an ka kunnafonisunw y’a dantigɛ cogo min, dugujukɔrɔfɛnw ani dugujukɔrɔfɛnw baarakɛlaw ye sɔrɔbagaw minɛ u ka bɔli la wa u ye ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn sɔrɔ u ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
Ani k’a fara a kan ko nin ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn senfɛ, a jɛkulu mɔgɔw dɔlakelen, min ye maramafɛn daminɛ ka sin Buguni jɔyɔrɔ ma, ye bal dɔ sɔrɔ.
Ani fana, u ye yamaruyasɛbɛn dɔw bila, mɔgɔw ka fotow bɛ bɔ kaban bɔlɔlɔ sanfɛ, wa ɲinini yamaruyasɛbɛn daminɛna nin cogo la walasa ka mɔgɔ minnu sen bɛ kɛ.
A lakanali kɔfɛ, i n’a fɔ anw ɲɛmɔgɔw tun b’a dɔn a kɛ, Buguni marabolo Gɔfɛrɛnɛri, Zenerali Keba Sangare, taara yɔrɔw la walasa k’a kɛ tiɲɛniw ye.
O kɔfɛ, sɔrɔdasi kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw ka marabolo kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw (Forsati) bilala dugu kɔnɔ walasa ka latigɛli walew kama.
Ani fana, Buguni marabolo ɲɛmɔgɔyaso ɲɛmɔgɔ y’a sababu kɛ ka wele bila jamaw ma, ka baaraɲɔgɔnya jɛlen kɛ ni kɔfɛjɔw ani lakanakɛbagaw ye, bawo, kunnafonisunw, minnu bɛ sɛbɛn sɛbɛn na, san wɔɔrɔ bɛ min na, tun ye sɔrɔdasiɲɛmɔgɔw ye don senfɛ ani tun y’u laseli a denbayaw ma, minnu tun tɛ yɛrɛ hakililatigɛ.
Gɔfɛrɛnɛri y’a ɲini kɔfɛjɔw ani lakanakɛbagaw fɛ, u ka bila hakililatigɛ kɔnɔ.
O kɔfɛ, a taara Buguni SESƐRƐFU la walasa k’a ɲini ka lakɔlɔsi lakɔlɔsi mɔgɔ wolonfila sɔrɔlenw la, minnu na saba bɛ kɛ gɛlɛya kɔnɔ.
An y’a jate k’a fɔ k’a sɛbɛn kɛra mɔgɔ duuru ye, minnu na polisi dɔlakelen, Marabolo Sɛnɛyɛrɛ ɛmɔgɔyaso ka fitini baarakɛbaga dɔ, bolifɛnbaga fila ani mɔgɔ kelen tɛ mɔgɔ sɔrɔ.
Bubakari Payitawo Walasa k’a ka jamakuluw wulikajɔ ka taa kalata kɛlɛ nataw kama, Politikitɔn Faamuyali ɛmɔgɔya kama ( ARIP ) min ɲɛmɔgɔya bɛ Cemani Hubɛri Kulibali bolo, ye nin kalata jɛkulu musow ani denmisɛnw ka kolatilenjɛkuluw ka birow ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn, alamisadon tɛmɛnen.
Nin ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn, min jɔda bɛ mɔgɔ, min bɛ se ka cɛbɔya la perezidansigikalata nata la, ka baarabolodali kɔnɔ, Minisiri kɔrɔ Cemani Hubɛri Kulibali, kɛra Amite Hotel kɔnɔ.
A tun bɛ ARIPU mɔgɔw politikitɔnw perezidan caman perezidan kɔnɔ, i n’a fɔ Hamadi Sangare PJA, Musa Umaru Jawara n’a bɛ fɔ a ma Bati Mali ɛmɔgɔya pariti Bati, n’o tɛ dɔwɛrɛ ye Faraɲɔgɔnkan ɛmɔgɔ, Seyidu Umaru Ture FACW ka ɲɛmɔgɔya ye.
ARIPU ka faraɲɔgɔnkankulu perezidan, politikitɔnw ni tɔn caman bɛ min na, y’a da tulow kan ka Cɛmancɛlafanga ɲɛmɔgɔw bilasira yaasa u ka ciw la ɲɛnabɔ.
O bɛ fɔlɔ la kalataw labɛnni kan, minnu bɛ se ka kɛ waati dantigɛlen kɔnɔ.
