UEFA mɔgɔw ka faraɲɔgɔnkanjɛkuluw jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ bɛ minnu na, Pɔli Jɛsi, tariku karamɔgɔ Faransi-Kɔnde Inivɛrɛsite la, b’o hakilijigin kɛ.
Ntolatantɔn bi naani naani naani na.
« Fatiba » hakilina kɔnɔ, ntolatan b’a to a ka kumalaseli ni Erɔpu tɔgɔw ye, k’a ka kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya taamasiyɛn.
K’a kɛ sɛbɛn wɛrɛ la, Ukrani ntolatannaw b’a ko in ɲɛfɔ.
Kasɔrɔ IYEFA y’a ɲini a dantigɛlisɛbɛn bɔli la.
politiki kiritigɛla,
U ka mɔgɔ tɛmɛnen kɔrɔbagaw ka gɛlɛya, u ka tɔgɔtigiya bɛ jamana kɔgɔfɛjɔw yɛlɛma halibi, min bɛ Crimée dugukolo kɔnɔ, i n’a fɔ ONI b’a sɔnna cogo min.
Wa o bɛ, Risi ka sɔsɔsɔliw n’a ta bɛɛ, min ye nin dugukolo fara ɲɔgɔn kan san 2014 ani min ye ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw sɔrɔ nin sugandiliw la.
Kunnafonisun: Lemonde.fr
Mali jamana basikɛtiboli tɔn musow, minnu ka ca ni san 18 ye, ntolatanna mɔgɔw y’u sɛmɛntiya k’u ye diyagoya kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲiniw kɛ u ka degelikaramɔgɔba fɛ, nka Mali basikɛtiboli federason, hali n’a sɔrɔ k’u kunnafoni kɛra, ma kɛnɛ kan, Human Rights Watch y’o dantigɛ bi.
Amadu Banba, min si bɛ san 51 la, jamana basikɛtiboli musow ka tɔn degelikaramɔgɔba ye, minnu tɛ san 2016 bɛ san 18 bɔ kabini, tun na kɛ ka ntolatanna tɔgɔ saba hakili walima kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲini kɛ ani k’u ka baaraɲɔgɔnyaɲini kɛ, tuma min u y’u ban k’u kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲiniw kɛ a ye, Human Rights Watch ka ɲininkalenw ka fɔ la.
O kɔfɛ Human Rights Watch ye sɛbɛn sɛbɛn diɲɛ basikɛtiboli federason ( FIBA ) ma, nin farikoloɲɛnajɛ ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu diɲɛ kɔnɔ, ka ɲɛfɔli kɛ diyagoya kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲini bisigikumaw kan Mali kɔnɔ, FIBA ye taabolo fɔlɔ ta, min jɔda kosɛbɛ, ka sɛgɛsɛgɛli jaabiw makɔnɔ, degelikaramɔgɔw ani jɔyɔrɔtigiw, minnu tun ye nin ɲɔgɔnnaɲiniw kɛ walima minnu tun y’a dɔn.
FIBA perezidan, Hamani angi, min ye Mali fasoden ye, y’i senbɔ waatilabaara la sɛgɛsɛgɛli kuntaala kama.
Human Rights Watch ye kumaɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kɛ ni mɔgɔ saba ye, minnu ka kan, n’u denbaya mɔgɔw ye, minnu y’u ka basikɛtiboli federason ka ɲangaliw kofɔ Bamba fɛ.
Kasɔrɔ federason ma baara kɛ ka jaabi kɛ nin sɔsɔliw ma, nka a y’i mago k’a banba ka ɲangiliw tiɲɛni ni lahidu di mɔgɔ minnu bɛ jamana tɔn kɔnɔ, u ka tiɲɛni kɔnɔ.
Mɔgɔ jalakilenw cɛla, dɔw kɛra diɲɛ ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw senfɛ, musow ka kupudimuso minnu ka ca ni san 19 ye FIBA la san 2019 ani san 18 tɛmɛnenw ka Afiriki ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn san 2020.
FIBA ka san 19 tɛmɛnenw musow ka diɲɛ basikɛtiboli kupudimuso san 2021 bɛna kɛ Hɔngiri k’a ta utikalo tile 7 la ka taa 15 la wa Mali ye kulu 16 kelen ye, minnu sen don a ɲɔgɔndan na.
Mali la, mɔgɔ minnu sigilen b’u denbaya mɔgɔw n’u ka denbaya mɔgɔw y’u ka diyagoya kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲini kɛli kɛ Bamba fɛ kabini san 2016, a ka san fɔlɔ k’a kɛ degelikaramɔgɔ jɔnjɔn ye.
A d’a fara a kan, jamana musow ka tɔn basikɛtikɛlamuso kɔrɔ, minnu ka ca ni san 18 ye, a tɔgɔ, i n’a fɔ mɔgɔ damadɔw tɔgɔw tɔgɔ yɛlɛmana u ka lakana kama, kafoɲɔgɔnya kɛ ani ka ɲangili kɛ Bamba fɛ, a ka fa ka fɔ la a ye kow laseli kɛ.
A y’a dantigɛ k’a kafoɲɔgɔnya daminɛna tuma min na Ajara, min si bɛ san 17 la, tun b’a ɲini ka jɔyɔrɔ sɔrɔ tɔn kɔnɔ : Banba y’a wele wa a y’a fɔ ko a tun bɛ fɛ ka cɛɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kɛ a ye ani ko a ka kan ka cɛɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kɛ a ye walasa ka jɔyɔrɔ sɔrɔ tɔn kɛ. Ajara banna.
FIBA ka jamanaw cɛ ɲɔgɔndan dɔ senfɛ, nin ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kɔnɔ, o kɛra diyagoyaɲɔgɔnyaɲini ye : a [Bamba] seginna Hotel soba kɔnɔ, sɔgɔma nɛgɛkanɲɛ 2 waati la.
A y’a ɲɔgɔn sɔrɔ, a y’a sɔrɔ a kɔnɔn fan dɔw la.
A y’a tɛgɛw bila a ka kulutu kɔnɔ. Ajara y’i bɔ soba la.
O kɔlɔsili kɔfɛ, Banba y’a Azala ntolatan waati dɔgɔya kosɛbɛ ntolatantɔn kɔnɔ.
Tɔn ntolatanna kɔrɔ mɔgɔ fila wɛrɛw ye nin koɲumanw ɲɛfɔ.
Mariyama (sɔrɔdasi) y’a dantigɛ Human Rights Watch ma ko a tun bɛ san 15 kɔnɔ, Banba y’a ɲini kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲini kɛ ale ye a ka Hotel soba kɔnɔ, ntolatantɔn ka taama dɔ senfɛ FIBA ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn dɔ kama, ani k’a bila ntolatantɔn kɔnɔ, a ban kɔfɛ.
Mariyama y’a sɛmɛntiya fana ko Banba tun bɛ kaso kulu denmusoninw taamasiyɛn, n’u tun b’a waleya kofɔ.
Denmisɛn sabanan, Umaru (sɔrɔdasi la), y’a sɛmɛntiya ko a tun bɛ san 17 na, Banba y’a ɲini k’a tɔgɔ sɔrɔ ani k’a ka cɛɲiɲiniw kɛ a ye.
Ne y’a ban, a ma to n ka ntolatan.
A y’an bila ntolatanw fara ɲɔgɔn kan. Ntolatanna mɔgɔw y’a sɛmɛntiya Human Rights Watch ma ko Banba tun bɛ diyagoya ni musow ka jamana ntolatan ntolatan tɔn mɔgɔ wɛrɛw ye, minnu ka ca ni san 18 ye, ka diyagoya ka diyagoya kɛ diyagoya ka sin ntolatan waati, wari ani farikoloɲɛnajɛ yɔrɔw ma.
Mali la, kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲini kɛ ni mɔgɔw ye minnu si bɛ san 15 la ka taa san 21 la sariyasɔsɔ tɛ sariyasɔsɔ ye hali n’a sɛbɛnbaga ye mɔgɔ kan min bɛ mɔgɔ kan walima a b’a ka kalan walima a ka ɲɛnabɔli jɔyɔrɔ bɛ min na, walima a ka baarakɛla bɛ min na.
A ka filɛli baara hukumu kɔnɔ ani k’a ka don FIBA la sariyaw kɔnɔ, Mali basikɛtiboli federason ka jɔyɔrɔ de ye ka ntolatannaw ani ntolatannaw lakana ka ɲɛnabɔliw la ani ka degelikaramɔgɔ minnu bɛ ɲɛnabɔli kɛ ɲangiliw ani ladonniw fɛ.
Ka kɛnɛ kan denmisɛnw ani denmisɛnw hakɛw lakanali dakun duuru fɔ la, minnu bɛ FIBA farati la, mɔgɔw ni ntolatanna n’u ka degelikaramɔgɔw fɛ kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲini kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲini ani kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲiniw kɔnɔ, k’a fara u ka degelikaramɔgɔw fɛ denmisɛnw kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲiniw kan.
Kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲini ani kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲini bɛ se ka nɔ bila mɔgɔ mɔgɔ minnu bɛ mɔgɔ kɔnɔn ani minɛn na, i n’a fɔ mɔgɔ minnu bɛ mɔgɔ kɔnɔn, i n’a fɔ mɔgɔ ka gɛlɛya kɔnɔn, i n’a fɔ mɔgɔ ka gɛlɛya kɔnɔn, i n’a fɔ mɔgɔ ka gɛlɛya kɔnɔn, i n’a fɔ mɔgɔ ka gɛlɛya kɔnɔn.
Fa, min y’a denmusonin, Ajara, ka koɲɛfɔli ɲɛfɔ, y’a dantigɛ ko o, ntolatanna mɔgɔ belebele kosɛbɛ, tun y’i senbɔ basikɛtiboli la, Banba ka wulikajɔ kɔfɛ.
A bɛ kɔlɔlɔsili la wa a tɛ foyi si kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen ye waati la.
A sɔrɔla ka gɛlɛya. Denmusoninw b’a bali k’u ka jɔyɔrɔ tɛ tɔn kɔnɔ walima k’u ɲɔgɔnna ni jaabi wɛrɛw ye, o la, cogoya gɛlɛya don kosɛbɛ.
Ahimari Mayiga, Afiriki ni Mali farikoloɲɛnajɛ denmisɛnw ka Lakana sigibaga, ntolatannaw ani ntolatannaw ka Lakana Tɔn dɔ y’o dantigɛ.
Cogo bɛɛ la, Mali basikɛtiboli federason jɔyɔrɔ tun ka kan ka ntolatannaw lakana, nka mɔgɔ si t’a sɔrɔ ko nin ntolatanna denmisɛn ninnu cogoya tɛ se ka kɛ.
Mariyama y’a dantigɛ ko Banba ye musow ka basikɛtiboli tɔn degelikaramɔgɔ sabanan ye min kan bisigikuma dɔw lasera federason ma.
Sɔrɔdasi ɲangata ye gɛlɛya gɛlɛya ye Mali kɔnɔ, farikoloɲɛnajɛ diɲɛ kɔfɛ.
Jamana sɛgɛsɛgɛliw cakɛbulon ka san 2018 sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛra sababu ye k’a jira k’a fɔ ko musow ani musow fanba, minnu si bɛ san 15 ka taa san 49 la, ye nin ɲangata sɔrɔ.
Ni Zezolɛnpikikiw ye Japon kɔnɔ ani FIBA ka san 19 tɔgɔlamɔgɔw ka Diɲɛ basikɛtiboli jɔnjɔn, minnu bɛ sɔrɔ gafe la, FIBA ani SIWO ka kan ka fɛɛrɛw ta ka taa gafe la, walasa ka degelikaramɔgɔw bɛɛ, minnu bɛ misaliw kɛ ani basikɛtiboli ɲɛmɔgɔw bɛɛ, minnu y’u ka jɔyɔrɔ kɛ ka Mali ntolatannaw lakana.
Human Rights Watch Ne y’a ɲini ka sɔrɔ yaasa ka ɲɛfɔli bɛɛ kɛ nin koɲɛ kan.
Kasɔrɔ n’o tɛ El Hadji ( an ka baarakɛbaga ), ne ma dɔn kow la, minnu bisigilen don.
Wa Bɛn ye sɛbɛn ye ne la!
O de ye Hamani angi n’a bɛ fɔ a mɔgɔ bɛ fɔ an ye dantigɛ ntɛnɛndon tɛmɛnen ( zuwɛnkalo tile 14 san 2021) a y’an wele k’an kunnafoni a ka latigɛ kan ani fana k’an hakililatigɛ a ka juguya la.
Gɛlɛya gɛlɛya ani ɲɔgɔn cɛ, min bɛ mɔgɔ sɔrɔ, o y’a jɔyɔrɔ ɲuman ta ka ɲɛsin mɔgɔya, ɲɔgɔn cɛ, ɲɔgɔn cɛ ma.
Ka waati bila waati kɔnɔ yaasa k’a gɛlɛya!
An ye nin gɛlɛya sɔrɔ ka sin ale ma, tile damadɔ kɛra, ka tɛmɛ cɛ dɔ ka kanali fɛ Ameriki.
An tun b’a dɔn ko Maliden bɛ se ka kɛ mɔgɔ muso gɛlɛya ye a bɛɛɲɔgɔn fɛ, k’a sababu kɛ ŋaniya walima n’a ka gɛlɛya ka bɔ a la.
Nka, an tun b’a ban k’a miiri ko Hamani angi kɔlɔlɔsiliw bɛna sɔn ka dɛsɛbɛn bila fana, ka cɛ dɔ fara ɲɔgɔn kan, o la, basikɛtiboli ani hali farikoloɲɛnajɛ ɲɛmɔgɔyaso kɔnɔna yɛlɛmani ka tɛmɛ a ka kan.
An tun ka kan ka makɔnɔ a bɛɛ la, o kɔfɛ, Hayidara Ayisata Sise n’a bɛ fɔ a ma Sato ( Cɛmancɛlafanga Jamana depite kɔrɔ ani SEYƐNITE kolatigɛjɛkulu mɔgɔ kɔrɔ) tun y’a lamɛn, mɛkalo tɛmɛnen, Malidenw fɛ, minnu sigilen don Afiriki tilebinyanfan na, yaasa a ka kɛ Afiriki tilebinyanfan depitebulon perezidanti ye.
Farafina woroduguyanfan ani cɛmancɛmancɛfan bɛɛ, i n’a fɔ Magɛrɛbu y’a sɔrɔ a kɔrɔfɛ, a ka ɲɔgɔn cɛbagaw yɛrɛw fɛ, k’a da a kan mɔgɔ dɔw tun b’u yɛrɛ dusukasi ni nin ɲɔgɔn cɛbɔya ye.
Ni mɔgɔ ka gɛlɛya ye, mɔgɔ bɛ mɔgɔ tɔw mago juguya la.
A lakodɔnnen k’a da a kan k’a da tempɛlɛ batitigi kan Mali mɔgɔ ɲuman bɛɛ ka kan ka gɛlɛya. Ni Mali kɛra basikɛtiboli tempɛlɛ ye, janko musow ka kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la, Hamani angi ye a sigibaga ye.
A taamasiyɛnna ni a ka baaraw ɲɛnabɔli ɲɛsɔrɔli ye ani k’a kɛ fɛɛrɛ yiriwali yecogo ye, k’a kɛ fɛɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya ye.
A y’a ( basikɛti ) to a ka bɔ a ka dusukasi la ani a ka bonya kɛ Afiriki ani diɲɛ kɔnɔ.
Yɛlɛma galabu, a y’a sɔrɔ Afiriki basikɛti la, k’a kɛ FIFBA / Afiriki perezidan ye, o kɔfɛ FIBA perezidan ye.
Basikɛti Ligi Afirika walima Afiriki basikɛtiboli Ligi (NIBE ɲɛnabɔlɔsili Afiriki version ) tako fɔlɔ b’o sɛmɛntiya mɛkalo tile 16 ka taa bila a tile 30 la Kigali, Ruwanda la!
K’a da a kan ko a ka perezidanya kɔnɔ Mali y’a ka bangu jɔnjɔn fɔlɔ sɔrɔ ( jama farikoloɲɛnajɛ kɔnɔ) kulɔbuw (Joliba musow, san 1995 ) ani jamana jamakuluw ( Samatasɛgɛ musow, san 2007 Dakaro, Senegali la).
Ni o ye nin ɲɛmɔgɔ ka bonya sɔrɔ ani k’a ɲɛnabɔ ni bonya ɲɛnabɔli ye Afiriki ani diɲɛ fan bɛɛ kɔnɔ, a yɛrɛ ka jamana kɔnɔ, nin taama y’a ka bonya kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la, dɛsɛli, hakililatigɛ caman.
Nka, den mɔgɔ min b’a la, Hamani y’a dɛmɛ sɔrɔ halibi ka sɛgɛsɛgɛli sɛbɛnw la, minnu man tɛmɛna ka tɛmɛ a la kabini a y’i cɛsiri a ka ɲɛmɔgɔya ɲɛnabɔcogoya fɛ.
Wa, sɔsɔli t’a la, u b’a yɛrɛ sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɔnɔ ( u t’a laɲini ka baara kɛ ni ɲɔgɔn yɛlɛma ye) kabini Hamani angi y’a latigɛ k’i senbɔ waatilabaara kɔnɔ, karidon tɛmɛnen ( zuwɛnkalo tile 13 san 2021) walasa FIBA ka sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛ a yɛrɛ kan, diyagoya kafoɲɔgɔnyaɲini bisigikumaw kan, ntolatanna tan ni ɲɔgɔn caman kan (mɔgɔ denmisɛnw bisigilenw waati la) Mali la.
Ne ma sen don abada ani ne ma jalakiliw dɔn abada, minnu cɛsiri b’a ka bataki kɔnɔ, a y’o sɛbɛn Niyɔriki Tayimu la.
O bɔlen kɔ yen, Niyɔriki kunnafonidisɛbɛn faseri t’a jira foyi si la ko perezidan angi ye ntolatanna musow diyagoya kafoɲɔgɔnya kɛ Mali kɔnɔ.
Nka, i n’a fɔ a y’a dantigɛ an ma, farikoloɲɛnajɛ kɔnɔn hakilina ani hakilina tun bɛ fɛ k’a bila sɛgɛsɛgɛlikɛlaw bolo, a ka waatilabaara bila kɔfɛ. Mɔgɔ minnu bɛ baara kɛ sɛbɛn ni angi Kɔrɔ walima minnu y’a ɲɔgɔn fɛ, y’a yɛrɛ sɔrɔ k’a ka nin kabali kalan.
Wa o kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la, k’a da a kan ɲɛmɔgɔ tɛ min bɛ sɔrɔ ntolatannaw ani ntolatanna musow farikolo ani hadamadenya la, a y’u nafaw lakana halibi.
K’a kɛ an ye laban na?
Munna Malidenw kɛra gɛlɛya ye, ka se k’u ka nafaw jira diɲɛ fɛ?, an ka denmisɛn kumalasela Kasiim Tarawore y’a ɲininkali a ka Fesibuki tɔgɔyɔrɔ kan.
Wa k’a hakilijigin kɛ ko nin ko in sɛbɛn bɛɛ bilala fo Bamakɔ.
U b’a miiri ka Hamani angi nɔgɔya, nka k’a tɛmɛ o kɔfɛ, Mali de b’a nɔgɔya.
Afiriki dɔ, min bɛ FIBA ɲɛmɔgɔya la, k’a fara Maliden dɔ kan, o ka kan ka kɛ sɔrɔdasi ye an bolo.
K’a da a kan, dusukasi don, minnu mɔgɔ dɔw ma se ka minɛ abada, wa u ye baarabolodali dɔ fara ɲɔgɔn kan walasa k’a bɔ a la.
Wa hali farati kɛ ka jamana tɔgɔya sɔrɔ, ma kɛ k’u ban u ka gɛlɛya la.
O tɛ gɛlɛya, k’a da a kan mɔgɔ tɛ se ka ɲɔgɔn cɛsiri, fasoɲɔgɔn cɛsiri, fasoɲɔgɔn cɛsiri sisan.
ani ka Hamani angi gɛlɛya nin taabolo la.
Wa i n’a fɔ miiri min dɔnnen b’a fɔ cogo min, Kiritigɛla dɔ bɛ yen, min bɛ wele bila waati la ani min ye mɔgɔ bɛɛ bila a yɔrɔ la!
Loran Bagibo ka segin Konowari cɛmancɛla tilebin kɔnɔ a ka dugubakɔnɔ Mama la, o y’a ka kiri kofɔ ntɛnɛndon diɲɛmɔgɔw ka ɲangili Kiritigɛla fɛ.
« Ne tɛ ɲangibaga ye ». Nin y’a siɲɛ fɔlɔ ye kabini a seginni ka na Konowari, perezidan kɔrɔ Loran Bagibo ye kuma fɔ, ntɛnɛndon zuwɛnkalo tile 28, a ka kiri an’a ka bɔli kan Diɲɛ Kɔrɔfɛjɛkulu ( SEPSEYI ) fɛ, k’a sɛmɛntiya k’a tun bilala ka taa Haayi bawo « mɔgɔ ɲangibaga dɔ tun ka kan ka bɔ a la ».
« SEYIPEYƐSI, o tun tɛ sɛbɛn ye, cɛ tun ka kan ka cɛɲɔgɔn cɛ, ɲɔgɔn cɛɲɔgɔn cɛɲɔgɔn cɛ, o tuma an ye n bila yɔrɔ la », Loran Bagibo y’o dantigɛ Mama, a ka dugubada, Konowari cɛmancɛla tilebin kɔnɔ.
Nka, a y’a fara a kan, diɲɛmɔgɔw ɲɛmɔgɔw, a ka pariti ɲɛmɔgɔw ani kunnafonidilaw ɲɛmɔgɔw ɲɛ, « n tɛ gɛlɛya, k’a da a kan n tun seginna n na ni ɲangibaga jɔyɔrɔ ye, i bɛ yen i bɛna gɛlɛya yan ».
K’a sɔrɔ Loran Bagibo, marisikalo laban, SEYIPEYƐSI fɛ, min na a tun jalakira kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la ni ɲangata ye ka sin hadamadenya ma, o kɛra sababu ye a seginni ka na Konowari.
« Mɔgɔ belebelew, minnu t’an dɔn, minnu bɛ an ka kɛlɛkɛlɛw kɔfɛ yen, y’a dɔn k’a fɔ ko ne ( tun ma kɛ ɲangibaga ) tɛ ne ye.
N bɛ fɛn bɛɛ kɛ, nka n tɛ n ye ɲangibaga ye », Loran Bagibo y’o sɛmɛntiya dɛmɛnniw kɔnɔ.
A tun y’a ɲɛfɔ ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kɔfɛ ni dantigɛli ɲɛmɔgɔw ye, minnu cɛsiri bɛ kɛ musow danfaralenw kɔnɔ, minnu bɛ bɔra a ka cɛmancɛsiri fan bɛɛ fanfɛ, n’u ye « bɛnɲini » ci di a ma.
« Bɛnɲini bɛɛ » « A yɛrɛ tun b’a laɲini bɛnɲini kama.
Fo ka sinsin a ka jama kan walasa Konowari fasojama wele ka bɛnɲini bɛɛ la”, Mama « dugukolow ɲɛmɔgɔ », sigida ɲɛmɔgɔba dɔ, Joseph Goli Obu, y’o dantigɛ AYƐFIPE la, mɔgɔ jɔnjɔnw kan.
Nin taamasiyɛnw ɲɛmɔgɔw ka kan fana k’u sen don ɲɛnajɛ kɔnɔ, min bɛ fɛ « yɛlɛmali » ma, i n’a fɔ a ka taamasiyɛn taamasiyɛn b’a la mɔgɔ min kaso kɛra ani k’a bila.
« Taradon, n bɛna n bɛnɲini ɲɛnabɔ, n bɛna ɲini a fɛ, a ka bɛnɲini baara la, a ka kuma fɔlɔw ka taa faso ma bɛnɲini hukumu kɔnɔ », dugukolow ɲɛmɔgɔ y’o sɛmɛntiya, n’a ka mɔgɔw y’a sɛmɛntiya k’a bila ɲɛnabɔli kama nin ɲɛnajɛ kama.
« Jamana kɔnɔ, ni du mɔgɔ dɔ bɔra gɛlɛya cogoya la, mɔgɔ b’a laɲini.
O de b’a la k’a yɛlɛma a ka durɔn kɔnɔ, sɔgɔma ɲɛ fɔlɔ, yann’a ka ɲɔgɔn sɔrɔ, ni maramaw ni taamasiyɛn kɛrɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛfɛsɛ.
Mama forobakɛyɔrɔ kɔnɔ, dugu sigibagaw y’u jigi k’u kan, k’u dantigɛ ani k’u gɛlɛya, k’a fɔ perezidan kɔrɔ ka na k’u kuma.
« Bagibo seginna ka bɛn don jamana kɔnɔ », Brigiti Kudu, min sigilen don Zebizeku dugukolo mɔgɔw la, b’o fɔ.
« N nisɔndiyalen don, nin don kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen don.
Perezidan Bagibo ka kannabila ye.
Mɔgɔ b’a fɛ k’a lamɛn, k’a b’a fɔ k’a fɔ k’a fɔ k’a fɔ k’a fɔ ko kelen durɔn durɔn ye”, a ka fan fɛ, Beatrice Jɛje, min bɛ bɔ Kpakeku la, y’o dantigɛ kumaden dɔ, min « bɛn ani bɛnɲini sɛbɛn » tɔgɔ la.
Mɔgɔ wari caman y’a laɲini barika kɛ, karidon, Mama, tile tan, a seginni kɔ Abijan kɔfɛ.
Kɔlɔsilikɛlaw ni a tɔgɔlamɔgɔw cɛɲɔgɔn caman fɛ, minnu tun t’a la ka bɔ a ka taa Abijan zuwɛnkalo tile 17 na, k’a kɔlɔsili kɛ a tun bɛ fɛ k’a bila jɔnjɔn jɔnjɔn na.
Loran Bagibo, min bɛ fanga la kabini 2000 la, tun minɛna awirilikalo san 2011 Abijan, o kɔfɛ a bila kalo saba tɛmɛnen kɔnɔ CPI la yaasa k’i kiri ka ɲangiliw kama, minnu kɛra san 2010 perezidansigikalata laban kɔfɛ.
A ban k’a ka dɛsɛ sɔrɔ ka sin Alasani Watara ma, o tun ye kalata kɔfɛ gɛlɛya kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen ye, min kɛra mɔgɔ 3 000 fatura ye.
A bilalen kɛ ɔkutɔburukalo san 2020 sarati sabanan kama, min sɔsɔli bɛ sɔsɔ, Alasani Watara y’a ka sɛbɛn di Loran Bagibo seginni ma tile damadɔ a ka kalafili kɔfɛ.
Ni AƐFUPE ye Jamana labɛnni minisiri, min bɛ cakɛbulonw cɛkow ɲɛmɔgɔya, Ibarahima Ikasima Mayiga, a ka dusukasi taama kɔnɔ Jamana cakɛbulonw la kabini a ka sigili la, y’a ta ntɛnɛndon zuwɛnkalo tile 28 san 2021, Jamana ɛmɔgɔ ka biro la, min ɲɛmɔgɔya bɛ Sanogo Aminata Male ɲɛmɔgɔya fɛ.
Nin taama, min ye Sanogo n’a baarakɛɲɔgɔnw yɛrɛ ye, kɛra baara ɲɔgɔnye ta fan fila ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, min kɛra Mali Jamana seginni kan.
An y’a ɲini fɔlɔ la ka taa Jamana ɛmɔgɔyaso biro kɔnɔ.
Minisiri Ikasa y’o fɔ, k’a da a kan cakɛbulon ye, min bɛ jamana ni fasodenw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
Min ye nin cakɛbulon kan, a ko ten, walasa ka jamana cogoya tiɲɛ di, Jamana fasodenw b’a miiri cogo min na, ka yɛlɛma, ka hakililatigɛ.
Bi.
Jamana ɛmɔgɔ kɔnɔ, Perezidan Ibarahima Ikasa Mayiga ka dɛmɛ, an ye fɛɛrɛ sɔrɔ walasa ka Jamana sigi.
K’a da a kan ko dɔgɔya, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya de bɛ se ka cogoyaw faamuya ani ka ɲɛnabɔcogow ɲinini.
Wa o la, Minisiri y’o tɛmɛna, an y’a sɔrɔ k’a jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ la.
An ye Jamana labɛnni labɛnni kɛcogoya sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛ.
taabolo sɛgɛsɛgɛliw, Jamana ni a hadamadenya baarakɛɲɔgɔn caman cɛ, politikiw ani fasodenw kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw cɛ.
A kɛra dɛsɛgɛsɛgɛli ye.
Waati damadɔ kɔnɔ, minisiri Ibarahima Ikasa Mayiga b’a sɔn, an tun bɛ na taama sɔrɔ dusukun na, nka nin taama y’a yɛlɛma ka kɛ baarasigi ye, walasa ka hakilijigin kɛ an ka Jamana kan, kabini sariyasunba la ka taa fasodenya la, fasodenya kɛcogo kan, cogoya la ka fasodenya labɛnni waati kɔnɔ, yaasa a ka kɛ Jamana cɛmancɛ la, fɔlɔ la ani laban na.
O de ye an ka taama kɛcogo ye.
Wa a kɛra lakɔli yɛrɛ ye an bolo.
An bɛ Jamana baarakɛla dɔ ka lamɛnni kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la, min y’a ɲɛnabɔ kirisow la, kabini sigida la fo ka taa sanfɛ, jamana kirisow, i n’a fɔ marabolo kɔnɔ kirisow, n bɛ kuma fɔ yen SEDEYAWO kan, nka fana min tɛmɛna Jamana kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen bɛɛ fɛ, walasa ka filɛli, faamuya, sɛgɛsɛgɛli.
O de kosɔn an ye bi.
Nin tɛ daminɛ ye.
An bɛna segin sɔngɔ yaasa ka ɲɛnabɔcogow sɛgɛsɛgɛli ka ɲɛsin forow danfaralenw ma, jamana ɲɔgɔnye la, min tun bɛ Jamana ɛmɔgɔ ka ɲɛnajɛ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya kɔnɔ, i n’a fɔ jamana kumaɲɔgɔnya, min bɛ sen bɛ sen bɛ jamana ɲɛmɔgɔya la, min sigida tun bɛ Jamana ɛmɔgɔ ka ɲɛmɔgɔya kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya kɔnɔ.
Kumaɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw don cɛmancɛlafanga kan, taamasiyɛn wɛrɛw an’a ka don cɛmancɛlafanga, ɲɔgɔn cɛmancɛlafanga, ɲɔgɔn cɛmancɛlafanga, ɲɔgɔn cɛmancɛlafanga, kalanso, kiriso, adw. O ye sugandiliw ye, nka fo ka taa sugandili ɲumanw fɛ ani ka Mali kura sigi.
O de ye an ye sebagaya sɔrɔ yan.
An y’a jira k’a fɔ ko a bɛ se ka kɛ cogo min na.
Sisan, cogoya caman kɔnɔ, ka nin bɛɛ sɔrɔ, ka ɲɛnabɔcogow sɔrɔ, minnu labɛnnen don ka waleya cɛmancɛlafanga tɔgɔw kama ani kɔfɛ, ni ɲɛmɔgɔ sigilen kuraw ye, minnu bɛna wulikajɔ kɛ tiɲɛ ni ɲɛnabɔcogow ye, minnu sɔnna Malidenw bɛɛ fɛ.
O de ye an y’a ɲɛnabɔcogo kɛ i ko ɲɛnabɔcogo bɛ se ka kɛ Mali bolo.
Wa an hakililatigɛla an ka jɔyɔrɔw kɔnɔ.
Ne bɛ Jamana ɛmɔgɔba n’a ka baarakɛkulu barikada u yɛrɛmahɔrɔnya kama.
An bɛna ta ka taa Malidenw bɛɛ ma yaasa mɔgɔ bɛɛ ka faamu ko mago bɛ yen, faraɲɔgɔnkan sɛbɛnnen bɛ Mali kɔnɔ yaasa ka taa ɲɛnabɔcogow ɲɛnabɔ, minnu ye kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen ye.
Hadama B. Fofana Mmu Aminata Sidibe, Jamana Jɔnjɔnw ka jiginni Cakɛda ( ANAC ) mara kolatigɛjɛkulu ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu perezidan ye nin kolatigɛjɛkulu ka sɛbɛn 29nan ɲɛmɔgɔya ɲɛmɔgɔya.
Nin kɛra alamisadon zuwɛnkalo tile 23 san 2021, A cakɛda ka lajɛba kɔnɔ.
A tun ye ka sɛbɛn kɛrɛfɛsɛbɛnw an’a waleyali jɔnjɔnw jira yann’a ka sɛbɛn kura baaraw daminɛ.
O la, mara kolatigɛjɛkulu perezidan, Mmu Aminata Sidibe, y’a hakilijigin kɛ a ka kumafalen senfɛ, k’a fɔ ko nin waati bɛ kɛ waati min na an ka jamana bɛ fangabulon, lakanako ani kɛnɛya gɛlɛya ɲɛsin, min kɔlɔsiliw ye sɔrɔ baaraw yɛlɛnni ye.
Ka da a la.
O ɲɔgɔnye baaraw ka kan ka kɛ, janko, baaraw kɛlenw sɛgɛsɛgɛli ani san 2020 baaraw ɲɛnabɔli sɛgɛsɛgɛli kan, baaraw labɛnnenw ka baaraw kɛcogoya san 2021 kɔnɔ, ani cakɛda ka labɛnni baarabolodali yɛlɛmani baarabolodali sɛgɛsɛgɛli kan.
A ka kuma fɔw la, Anac ka san 2020 baarakɛjɛkulu, min labɛnna, min labɛnna, min kɛra wari hakɛw ani wari hakɛw ye SEFAWARI dɔrɔmɛ 4 633 397 684 ye.
K’a kɛ sɔngɔ ye, wuliw kɛra sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 4 584 220 666 ye, k’a da sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 98, 94% kan, ka tɛmɛ ɲɛsigilenw ma.
Jɔnjɔnw bɛ sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 4 404 884 862 la, n’o bɛ jɔnjɔn kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen ye 96,9% ye, k’a sɔrɔ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw ye.
O n’a ta bɛɛ, a ka nafoloko yɛlɛmani yɛlɛmana n’a ta bɛɛ, k’a da a kan koronawirisi fiɲɛbanaba ye, min ye dɛsɛbɛn sɔrɔ ka se 60% sɔrɔ, ANAC ka baaraw la, mɔgɔ b’a jate.
Diɲɛ jɔyɔrɔjɔyɔrɔ sɛbɛn lakurayali, Perezidan Modibo Keyita – Senu (Aipmk-S)
lakanakɛcogow ani lakanakɛcogow kologɛlɛyali Mali kɔnɔn jɔyɔrɔtigiyɔrɔtigiyɔrɔw kɔnɔ, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la Bamakɔ Senu, min ye sɛbɛnkɛrɛnnenya filanan sɛbɛnni labɛnni yɔrɔ sɛbɛnna.
Kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya ɲɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛn fila, k’a kɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛn fila, k’a kɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛfɛrɛn fila, k’a kɛrɛfɛrɛfɛn fila, k’a kɛrɛfɛ
Tumutu ani Gawo jɔyɔrɔtigiw labɛnni, minnu y’a daminɛ ka jɔyɔrɔw sɔrɔ, minnu ka fara Kayi jɔyɔrɔtigi kan ; sɛgɛsɛgɛli dɔ kɛra Kayi ani Sikaso jɔyɔrɔtigiw yɛlɛmani kama.
ininkaliw daminɛna Kidali, Menaka ani Taawudeyiti jɔyɔrɔtigiw labɛnni nafolobɔ kama.
Baara bolodalenw siratigɛ la, ɲɛnabɔcogo kuraw sɔrɔli.
An b’a ka sɛgɛsɛgɛli bolodiɲɔgɔnna bolodiɲɔgɔnna bolodiɲɔgɔnna bolodiɲɔgɔnna bolodiɲɔgɔnna bolodiɲɔgɔnna bolodiɲɔgɔnna bolodiɲɔgɔnna bolodiɲɔgɔnna bolodiɲɔgɔnna bolodiɲɔgɔnna bolodiɲɔgɔnna bolodiɲɔgɔnna bolodiɲɔgɔnna bolodiɲɔgɔnna bolodiɲɔgɔnna bolodiɲɔgɔnna bolodiɲɔgɔnna bolodiɲɔgɔnna bolodiɲɔgɔnna bolodiɲɔgɔnna bolodiɲɔgɔnna bolodiɲɔnna bolodi
A y’o sinsin.
A bɔlen b’a la cakɛbulon ka baaraw kɔnɔn, minnu sɔrɔla kɛnɛyako gɛlɛya la, minnu daminɛna ka daminɛ ka tɛmɛ dɔwɛrɛ, k’a kɛ a yɛrɛmahɔrɔnya taabolo ye, awiyɛn taabolo yɛlɛmana ka kɛcogoya kɔnɔ, o kɛra san 2020 kɔnɔn 28,8% sɔrɔ, k’a da san 2019 kan.
Taamakɛbagaw ka taabolo fana y’a jiginni kɛ 57,3% ye san 2020 kɔnɔ, k’a da san 2019 kan.
O b’a ɲɛfɔ ni jagokɛjɛkɛyɔrɔw taamasiyɛnni ye, minnu bɛ taamadenw ta ka taa Mali la, k’a kɛ Kowidi – dizinɛfu ( 19 ) fiɲɛbanaba kɛlɛli hukumu kɔnɔ, k’a ta san 2020 marisikalo tile 19 la ka taa san 2020 zuluyekalo tile 25 la.
Adama Tarawore - Kidali dugu, Mali kɛmancɛmancɛmancɛman kɔnɔ, kɛra forobabaaraw taamasiyɛn ye kabini dɔgɔkun damadɔ.
Jamana minisiri caman ka taama kɔfɛ, Alize Bɛnkansɛbɛn kɔlɔsilikɛjɛkulu ka taama kɛra dugu kɔnɔ min tun banna gɔfɛrɛnaman mɔgɔw ma san 7 bɔli kɔnɔ.
Mɔgɔ b’a yɔrɔ jan waati la min na Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ Musa Mara tun b’a ka taama yɛlɛmana dugu kɔnɔ, san 2014.
Kabini nin don, kow y’a yɛlɛma ka taa sɔrɔdasi kuluw cɛ, minnu bɛ Kidali dugu ɲɛmɔgɔya ani cɛmancɛlafanga Jamana ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
Sanw kɔnɔ, yɛrɛmahɔrɔnyaɲɛmɔgɔw ka dusukasi ka sin Mali ma yɛlɛmana.
Sigida mɔgɔ yɛrɛw yɛrɛ bɛ mɔgɔ sɔrɔdasi kɔnɔ, wa diɲɛ kɔkɔrɔdonbagaw tɔgɔlamɔgɔw b’a dɔn ko yɛrɛmahɔrɔnya kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw ye sɔrɔdasiw ye, minnu tɛ foyi si sɔrɔ dugukolo belebele la.
Sanw den na, hakililaɲɔgɔn cɛsiri, min tun bɛ Ifuogofasu ni Imigahadi cɛsiri kɔnɔ, y’a dɔgɔya kosɛbɛ.
Gatiya t’a laɲini ka dugu minɛ ni fanga ye, ka ɲɛsin Elaji Gamu ma, wa a mɔgɔw ka kannabila ye k’u yɛrɛ bila dugu kɔnɔ.
Kɔlɔsilikɛlaw ka wulikajɔw kɛra dɔwɛrɛw ye, wa musow ani denmisɛnw tɛmɛniw, minnu bilala tele la maramafɛjɛkuluw fɛ, y’a dɔgɔya k’a dɔgɔya.
O n’a ta bɛɛ, Kidali tolen don i n’a fɔ muso fatura, n’a ka dusukunnako an’a yɛrɛfɛnw dɔnnen don.
Ka tɛmɛ tɛmɛnen na, a y’a ka kumaɲɔgɔnw bila kumalaseli dɔ fɛ, min bɛ sɔrɔdasi zoni fila sigili dantigɛ Gurima kɔnɔ Azawadi tɔnw ka Kolatilenjɛkulu ( SEMA ) fɛ.
A tɛ mɔgɔw ka fɔ la k’a fɔ ko kɛcogoya kɛcogoya ye, n’o ye kanu dantigɛli ye, SEMA ɲɛmɔgɔw ka fɔ la, minnu b’a fɔ ko u bɛ waleya ka bonya kɛ jamaw ye minnu bɛ ɲangiliw kɔnɔ.
Nka SEMA ka latigɛli ŋaniya tɛ bɔ Malidenw bolo, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la kaɲaka sigidajama dɔw.
Kaɲaka marabolo sigibagaw fanba bolo, a tɛ mɔgɔ sɔrɔ ko kulu maramafɛnw dɔ, minnu bɛ sɔrɔ ani k’u yɛlɛma Kidali, bɛ yɛlɛma ka mɔgɔw sɔrɔ Gurima kɔnɔ, n’a lakanabaliya bɛ sɔrɔ kaban.
Ka bɔ IFOGHW dugu la walasa k’u sigi dugukolo wɛrɛw kɔnɔ, o ye sɔrɔdasi fɛɛrɛ ye min tɛ gɔfɛrɛnaman bɛ fɛn fana la, o kɔlɔsili tɛmɛna k’a faamuya k’a fɔ ko SEMA y’a ɲɛsin nin sɛbɛn kɔnɔ.
Fɛn bɛɛ kɔnɔn, Fogu hakililaw y’u cɛsiri kalo laban ninnu na, hali n’o tɛ san 2020, yɔrɔ min na siɲɛ fɔlɔ siɲɛ fɔlɔ, Touarɛgi tɔgɔlamɔgɔw y’u sɔn Alize Bɛnkansɛbɛn, bɛn ani bɛnɲini kama, labɛnni taabolo ma Mali kɔnɔ.
Jamana kumaɲɔgɔnya ni bɛɛ sen bɛ min na Bamakɔ san 2019 desanburukalo la, Kidali tɔgɔlamɔgɔw ye sɛmɛntiya k’u bɛ Mali kɔnɔ, min bɛ kelen ani min tɛ bɔ a la.
Nin kuma kɛbagaw dɔlakelen, Musa Agi Atahɛri, ye sisan Denmisɛnw ani Farikoloɲɛnajɛw minisiri ye.
Kidali dugu mɔgɔ caman bɛ gɔfɛrɛnaman kɔnɔ, i n’a fɔ Alamudu Agi Iliyɛni, Malidenw sigilenw ka minisiri, minnu sigilen don kɔkan.
Nin IFOGƐSI dugu gɔfɛrɛnɛri kɔrɔ, perezidan ATT ka kɔnɔ, tɛ mɔgɔ tɔgɔ dɔnnen tɛ Kidali tuarɛgi cɛmancɛla kɔnɔ.
Ni minisiriw ani forobabaarakɛjɛkuluw ye Kidali siratigɛ lakɔlɔsi, sɔsɔ t’a la, gɔfɛrɛnaman ka nin portaw dayɛlɛli kosɔn zoni denmisɛnw ma, o kɛra gɛlɛya ye Jamana kama.
Umaru KONATE - K’a sɔrɔ diɲɛ tɔw bɛ tɛmɛ ɲɛmɔgɔya ka taa ɲɛmɔgɔya la, Mali,
A tɛmɛna ka taa ɲɛ ni Kameruni tɛmɛ ye.
Kabini san 1991, foyi si tɛ tiɲɛ ye nin jamana belebele kɔnɔ, min ye mɔgɔw yɛrɛmahɔrɔnya sɛbɛn u denw ma.
Mɔgɔ b’o kɛ, mɔgɔ b’o kɛ ani mɔgɔ b’o kɛ.
Nin ye kɛcogoya ye politiki cogoya yɛlɛmana cogo min na jamana kɔnɔ kabini san saba jɔyɔrɔ ye.
Ni politiki mɔgɔw b’u laɲini nin politiki gɛlɛya kɔnɔ, jama, ale, b’a laɲini, b’a laɲini ani k’a dɛmɛ suguya kɔnɔ kasɔrɔ tɛmɛnen tɛ min na.
Juguman na, a lakɔlɔsili tɛmɛna ka na.
Kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la Bamakɔ, mɔgɔw b’a miiri k’a fɔ ko mɔgɔw yɛlɛmani tɛmɛnen bɛ jamana ɲɛmɔgɔya la, o de bɛna ɲɛnabɔcogo sɔrɔ.
U (Bamako mɔgɔw) t’a dɔn ko taabolo de b’a la wa cɛw t’a la.
O de kosɔn, u bɛ waati bɛɛ siratigɛw kɔnɔ, k’a ɲini X walima Y ka bɔli ɲini, tuma min u tɛ fɛ ka bɔ a ka galabu la, kasɔrɔ u tɔgɔw hakililatigɛ t’a la.
O de kɛra 2020 kɔnɔ ni silamɛya diinɛw ɲɛmɔgɔ dɔw ka bɔliw ye minnu tɛ ɲɛsinnen kɔnɔ ani Ɛmusɛnki Ɛrɛfupe.
U ye gɛlɛya gɛlɛya sɔrɔ Jamana ɲɛmɔgɔya la walasa ka mɔgɔ caman bila siratigɛw kɔnɔ dɔgɔkun caman kɔnɔ, k’a ɲini perezidan Ibarahima Bubakari Keyita ka bila ɲini, min sigilen don demokarasi kɔnɔ, n’a ta bɛɛ.
U ka kɔlɔsili kɔnɔ, u ma se ka hakililatigɛ di Malidenw ma, minnu ye jamana nata ye IBEKA kɔfɛ. Nin sɛgɛsɛgɛsɛgɛli kɔnɔna la, Kati forobabaarakɛla denmisɛn dɔw y’u danaya kɛ utikalo tile 18 san 2020. Sɔrɔdasiyɛn daminɛna politiki kɛnɛ kan, min bɛna dusukasi ni dusukasi sɔrɔ Ɛmusɛnki Ɛrɛfupe ɲɛmɔgɔw bolo, minnu bɛna sɔrɔ u ka yɔrɔ la, sɔrɔdasi kɛlɛbagaw bɛɛ fɛ, minnu kɛra u ka yɔrɔ la,
U ka fɔ la, fanga tun seginna u hakɛ la.
Tiɲɛ na, mɔgɔ bisigikuma tɛ faga Mali la, nka a bɛ mɔgɔ bisigiyalen don halibi.
Demokaratiw, minnu bɛ fɛ ka fanga ta sira kɔnɔ.
Sɔrɔdasi denmisɛnw, minnu tɛ se k’u ka jɔyɔrɔtigiw ta ka ɲɛsin fasojama ma, min y’a ɲini ka dɛmɛ kɛ.
I n’a fɔ i n’a fɔ mɔgɔ sigilen bɛ cogo min na, kɔrɔfɔ gɛlɛya bɛ gɛlɛya kɛ, jama jigi b’a la ani k’a ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
A tɛ dɔgɔn!
Gɔfɛrɛnaman labɛnni kɔfɛ, kow tɛmɛna ka daminɛ.
Jamana cɛmancɛlafanga kolatigɛjɛkulu ( SEYƐNITE ) bilala sen kan cogoya kelenw kɔnɔ, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la Mali sigidajama ka faraɲɔgɔn cɛsiri kosɔn min bɛ ka gɛlɛya ka gɛlɛya kɛ cɛsiri ani bɛɛ kɛlenya gɛlɛya la, minnu yɔrɔ fɛ yɔrɔ la, o yɔrɔ fɛ.
Sɛbɛn ani danaya dɔ bɛ sigi Jamana ɲɛmɔgɔya la.
Cɛmancɛlafanga jɛkulu ani sɔrɔdasi sɔrɔdasi sɔrɔlen tɛ se ka taa ɲɛmɔgɔya kelen kɔnɔ.
Kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen ye mɛkalo tile 24 san 2021.
Seginni ka na daminɛna yɔrɔ la.
Cɛmancɛlafanga perezidan, M’Bah N’Daw, ani a ka minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ, Mukutari Wani, bilala ɲɔgɔn fɛ, cɛmancɛlafanga laban tile 9 kɔnɔ, o la, ka jama ka jigi bɔ.
Kɔlɔsiliw yɛlɛma ka sɔrɔ yaasa ka jigi segin ka na.
Sɔrɔdasi ɲɛmɔgɔ y’a latigɛ ka koɲɛ ta yɛrɛ ma.
O kama, ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw bɛ ka caya ni Mali sigidajama mɔgɔw bɛɛ ye.
Nin daminɛ kura kama, fan belebele kɛra Ɛmusɛnki Ɛrɛfupe la, min ye a ka fɛɛrɛtigi ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu perezidan sigi walasa ka Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ jɔyɔrɔ ta.
Nin taabolo hakililatigɛ ye tɔn tɔgɔlamɔgɔw bolo, minnu bɛ ka sebagaya wele kaban, o ye ɲininkali jɔnjɔnw ye, minnu jɔra filɛlikɛla caman bolo, minnu lakodɔnnen don.
Sogɛli Mayiga bɛna kɛ sɔrɔdasi koɲɛ ye, walasa k’a yɛrɛ mɔgɔw ka nafaw lakana walima k’a yɛrɛ jɔyɔrɔ k’a ka politiki hakilina lakana? Sogɛli Minisiri ɛmɔgɔ, o ye kɛlɛ ɲuman ye fasodenya yɛrɛminɛkulu kama.
ƐMUPEYƐRI,
Kabini san 1991, nin pariti b’a ɲini k’a yɛrɛ sɛbɛn sɔrɔ politiki sɛbɛnw kan.
A kɛtɔla Sogɛli sɔrɔ i n’a fɔ Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ, Kolonɛli Asimi Goyita y’a fɔ k’a fɔ k’a fɔ ko sɔrɔdasi yɛlɛmani politiki kɛnɛ kan o kɛra politikimɔgɔw ka dɛsɛ ye, minnu na Sogɛli bɛ sen na kabini san tan?
Kasɔrɔ hakililatigɛ t’a la, gɔfɛrɛnaman nata bɛna kɛ M5 ɲɛmɔgɔw mɔgɔba ye.
Sogɛli la, anw b’a fɔ ko pariti ncinin dɔ walima yɛlɛnminɛ jɛkulu ɲɛnabɔli bɛ fɛn wɛrɛ bɔ Jamana ta la bawo tiɲɛw ani ɲɛnabɔw tɛ kelenw ye.
Mɔgɔ minnu b’u sinsin k’a fɔ ko Sogɛli ye cogoya cɛ ye, u ka kan ka seginni ta.
Mɔgɔ kiri bɛ baara la wa a tɛ kɔrɔfɔ la.
Ɛmusɛnki Ɛrɛfupe fɛɛrɛtigi ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu perezidan y’a kɛ fanga fɔlɔsili kama, mɔgɔ b’a faamuya kosɛbɛ ko o tɛ k’a ka Mali dɛmɛ kɛ, nka k’a ka ŋaniya yɛlɛma tiɲɛ na.
Sogɛli bɛna ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn ni fɛn bɛɛ ye min tun b’a ɲini ka kɛ Ɛmusɛnki Ɛrɛfupe ka bɔliw senfɛ wa mɔgɔ ka gɛlɛya ka fɛn min ɲɔgɔnna.
Kɔkɔrɔdon caman, minnu fɔra o fɛ, tɛ se ka baara lakodɔn cɛmancɛlafanga ɲɛmɔgɔ kuraw ma, bawo, mɔgɔ bɛ dɛmɛ kɔkɔrɔdon ni walew ye minnu kɛra, wa a tɛ kumakanw fɛ, minnu sirilen don kɛnɛ kan walima marasiw fɛ.
Malidenw fanba t’u dogo si tile saba don.
Baarakɛyɔrɔ kɔlɔsili bɛ tɛmɛ don na.
Dɔgɔtɔrɔw bɔra dɔgɔtɔrɔw la, minnu jigi b’a la.
siratigɛw, minnu ni mɔgɔw ye, minnu bɛ ɲɔgɔn cɛ, bɛɛ ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
Jamana bɛɛ bɛ maramafɛntigi kuluw ka ɲɛsinnen kɔnɔ, wa ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw bɛ ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn sɔrɔ Bamakɔ.
Malidenw tɛ dɔgɔyɔrɔ kelen sɔrɔ.
O tuma, waati tɛ kɛ kɔrɔfɔlɔw walima politiki cɛsiriw minnu yɛrɛ tɛmɛnenw ye.
I n’a fɔ cɛmancɛlafanga perezidan kura y’a fɔ cogo min, sɔrɔdasi kelen min bɛ ɲɛsin o ye waati ye.
O tuma, walasa k’a sɛmɛntiya Malidenw ka miliyɔn 20 ma ko a bɛ se ka Mali kura sigi, Sogɛli ka kan fɔlɔ ka gɛlɛyaw bɔ, minnu bɛ sɛbɛnw bolo sariyasɔsɔ la, ka dɔ fara sɔrɔbagaw hakɛ kan an ka siratigɛw kɔnɔ, ka kɛnɛyɔrɔw lakana ani laban na, ka ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kɛlɛli taabolo bila, min tɛ se ka ɲɛsin ɲɔgɔn fɛ, ɲɔgɔnfɛnfɛnfɛnfɛnfɛn, mɔgɔfɛnfɛnfɛnfɛnfɛnfɛnfɛn
Politiki walima marakɛcogo tilennibaliya ani misali, a b’a lahidu di Malidenw ma.
Kelen ka kan ka bɔ ɲɔgɔn fɛ walima ɲɔgɔn fɛ?
Ni bɔlɔlɔsili ani misali ka kan ka kɛ, Sogɛli b’a dɔn k’a fɔ mɔgɔ min b’a miiri ko ale t’a kan ka kɛ wale ye.
A bɛ mɔgɔ minnu ni minnu ka kan ka bɔ, wa a misali t’a la ɲuman, n’an bɛ sɛbɛn a kɔfɛsɛbɛnw kɔnɔ.
K’a kɛ cɛmancɛlafanga ɲɛmɔgɔya ye. Bawo, k’a kɛ cɛmancɛlafanga ɲɛmɔgɔya ye Jamana ɲɛmɔgɔya ɲɛmɔgɔya la, k’a kɛ cɛmancɛlafanga ɲɛmɔgɔya ye.
Kolonɛli Asimi Goyita, a ka sɛbɛn kɛlen kɔnɔ, y’a da tulow kan, a ka kuma kɔnɔ, k’a bɛna kɛ Jamana kumaɲɔgɔnyaɲɔgɔn cɛmancɛlafanga ɲɛnabɔli kama kalo tɔgɔlamɔgɔw kɔnɔ, minnu tolen bɛ.
A ka fan na, a ka Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ y’a ka jamana sigibaw kuraw labɛnni ɲɛnabɔ, yann’a ka cɛmancɛlafanga ɲɛnabɔli kama kokɛcogo bɛɛ kɛ.
Sogɛli ka gɛlɛya ka taa ɲɔgɔn kan, bɛ yɛlɛma ka taa yɛlɛmaba kan, min t’a tɔgɔ fɔ.
Minisiri ɛmɔgɔ kura ka walew bɛ nin bisigikuma tiɲɛtigiya.
K’a yɔrɔ k’a kɛ fɛn min ye fangabulonkow yɛlɛmaniw labɛnni ye walasa ka kalataw labɛnni kɛnɛya ani jɛlenya ye, a bɛ waati kɛ ka bɔ taamaw la, minnu tɛ se ka dɛmɛ kɛ ka latigɛli kɛcogoya ɲuman ye.
Nin taamaw ani ɲininiw, mɔgɔ y’u ye kaban nin jamana kɔnɔ.
A kɛtɔla ka banni kɛ, Sogɛli bɛ cɛmancɛlafanga bɛnkansɛbɛn sɛbɛnnen kɔnɔ, n’a ka gɔfɛrɛnaman ye mɔgɔ mugan ( 28 ) mɔgɔw ye.
Min ye baarakɛyɔrɔ kura ka kumafalenw bɛɛ kɔnɔn, a yɔrɔ t’a sɔrɔ.
Gɔfɛrɛnaman kura bɛ M5 mɔgɔw, sɔrɔdasiw, kulu maramafɛntigiw ani mɔgɔba mɔgɔw de kɔnɔ, minnu jalaki bɛ diɲɛmɔgɔw ɲɛmɔgɔw fɛ.
O cogo la, politikimɔgɔw ani jɛrɛjɛkuluw fanba, jɔda jɔda bɛ min na.
O ko cogoya tɛ dɔwɛrɛ ye ka Jamana Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ ka dusukunnamɔgɔw kɛli la.
Kow hakɛ caman, minnu bɛ ɲininkaliw kɛ jamana nata kan, nin gɔfɛrɛnama kɔnɔ, min taamasiyɛnnen don kaban ni tiɲɛni ye.
Donani.
Lebedem.
An ka kan k’a miiri ko Alize Bɛnkansɛbɛn lakurayali bɛna kɛ fan kelen kama ani ka fan wɛrɛw bila.
Bɛnkansɛbɛn bolonɔbilala fan saba bɛɛ bɛnkansɛbɛn kɔnɔn sɛbɛnw bolo, minnu bɛ fɛ ka bila Bɛnkansɛbɛn kɔnɔ.
An ka kan ka Bɛnkansɛbɛn dayɛlɛ ni kalan kura ye.
Nin ye pandɔri sɔrɔ ye, min ka kan ka ban ka kɛ tiɲɛ na.
y’a lase SEMA mɔgɔw, minnu tun bɛ Bamakɔ, kunnafonidilajɛ dɔ senfɛ, kunnafonidilaw ka soba la, karidon tɛmɛnen.
U tun kɛra, dɔwɛrɛw cɛla, Atayi Agi Mohamɛdi bolofara ɲɛmɔgɔ, Mɛdi Alimulu Ulidi Ramadan, kumalasela, Sidi Agi Bayi ani Tila Agi Zayi tun ye SEMA bolofara mɔgɔw bɛɛ ye, minnu tun bɛ Bamakɔ, Bɛnkansɛbɛn waleyali kama kunnafonidilaw bolo, Alize baarataabolo Bɛnkansɛbɛn bolonɔbilali san 6 kama.
Alize Bɛnkansɛbɛn lakurayali koɲɛ na, SEMA mɔgɔw, minnu sen bɛ lajɛrɛ la, bɛ sɔnna k’a fɔ ko nin se ka kɛ banba ye, min ma kan abada ka dayɛlɛ.
U ka kumalasela Alimulu Ulidi Ramadan ka fɔ la, fan bɛɛ minnu bolonɔbilala b’u bolo dantigɛliw b’u bolo.
Bɛn Bɛnkansɛbɛn lakurayali bɛna to an bɛna se, an fana, ka fɛn bɛɛ lasɔrɔ min ma se ka bila Alize.
A y’o dantigɛ.
Tuma si bɛnkansɛbɛn na.
An ye diɲɛmɔgɔw ye, minnu y’an bila ka Bɛnkansɛbɛn bolonɔbila.
An tun t’a fɛ ka bolonɔbila.
Tila Agi Zayini y’o lamɛn.
Tɔn mɔgɔw bolo, Bɛnkansɛbɛn bɛ fɛn jɔnjɔnw jɔyɔrɔtigiw ta kaban, minnu ye Jamana yɛrɛmahɔrɔnya, Jamana kelenya, Jamana dugukolo bɛɛlenya ani Jamana fanga cogoya ye.
Ni fan dɔw b’a jate ko yɔrɔ ninnu dɔlakelen sɔsɔra, fan bɛ se ka wele bila Bɛnkansɛbɛn Kɔlɔsilikɛjɛkulu ( SEYƐSIYA ) la a yɛlɛmani kama.
Atayi y’o ɲɛfɔ walasa k’a ɲɛfɔ kunw an’a taabolo, minnu bɛna se ka Bɛnkansɛbɛn falen kɛ.
Ni yɔrɔ ninnu tɛ, yɛlɛmani wɛrɛ si tɛ.
Nin lakurayali bɛ se ka Bɛnkansɛbɛn dayɛlɛ ni kuma wɛrɛw ye, minnu tɛna sɔrɔ.
O bɛna kɛ sababu ye Bɛnkansɛbɛn lawaliyali tɛ.
y’a ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw taamasiyɛn, yann’a ka hakilijigin kɛ ko nin waleyali tɛna sɔrɔdasiw taali kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la Mali ni kulu maramafɛntigiw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
Politiki donni bɛɛ, gɛlɛya bɛɛ, min bɛ sɔrɔ ani min ma labɛn, o la, o kɛra gɛlɛya seginni ye.
O ye diɲɛ bɛɛ taabolo ye.
O kandi tɛ kɔnɔ, mɔgɔ tɛ se ka hakililatigɛ ko gɛlɛya tɛna kɛ.
A baarakɛjɛkulu ɲɛmɔgɔ, Atayi Agi Mohamɛdi, b’i sɛgɛsɛgɛ.
O n’a ta bɛɛ, SEMA tolen don cɛmancɛlafanga fɛ.
Cɛmancɛlafanga gɔfɛrɛnaman, ka tɛmɛ Cɛmancɛlafanga Perezidan fɛ, ma ban jaabi jira an ma, ka sin Bɛnkansɛbɛn lawaliyali ma.
A ma fɛn bɔ an na min b’a da a kan ko ŋaniya t’a la k’a kɛ.
A kolonɛli Asimi Goyita ye Alize Bɛnkansɛbɛn bilali la sen kan ni cɛmancɛlafanga perezidan ka kuma ye a ka kumaw kɔkɔrɔdon ye.
SEMA y’a fɔ a y’i labɛn ka taa Bɛnkansɛbɛn kɔfɛ fo ka taa SEYƐNITE ɲɛkɔrɔ.
Bi, SEMA bɛ se ka kunnafonidilajɛ dɔ labɛn Bamakɔ ani k’u hakilijigin di u yɛrɛmahɔrɔnya la ani lakanako bɛɛ la.
O b’a jira k’a fɔ ko tabu dayɛlɛna ani ko danaya daminɛna ka sigi.
Cakɛda ɲɛmɔgɔ, Atayi Agi Mohamɛdi, sɔnna o la.
Kureyisi Sise.
Bɛnkansɛbɛn bɛn ani bɛnɲini na Mali la, min bɔra Alize taabolo la san wɔɔɔrɔ, a bolonɔbilali kɔfɛ, a waleyali gɛlɛyaw. A bolonɔbilala mɛkalo tile 15 san 2015 o kɔfɛ o kɔfɛ san kelen zuwɛnkalo tile 20, Bɛnkansɛbɛn bɛn ani bɛnɲini na Mali la, min bɔra Alize taabolo la san wɔrɔ, a waleyali kɔfɛ, y’a kumalaseli caman kɛ.
Mali sɔrɔmuw ka kɛlɛsili kɔfɛ k’u ka Kidali dugu ta, banbaganciw yɛlɛma ani min y’a yɛlɛma k’a kɛ fiyako ye.
O waati ɲɛmɔgɔw ye kumaɲɔgɔnyaw daminɛ Alize ni SEMA banbaganci kɔrɔw ye diɲɛmɔgɔw ka ɲɛmɔgɔya kɔnɔ ani kalo tɔgɔlamɔgɔ 9 kɔfɛ, minnu y’a to fan fila bolofara kɛnɛ kan.
Mali ɲɛmɔgɔw ka ɲini na, Bɛnkansɛbɛn bolonɔbilali kɛra Bamakɔ, mɛkalo tile 15 san 2015 ani san kelen zuwɛnkalo tile 20, mɔgɔ minnu tun bɛ senbɔ.
San wɔɔrɔ a bolonɔbilali kɔfɛ, bɛn Bɛnkansɛbɛn, min bɔra Alize baarataabolo la, bɛ to ka bonya ni bɔli caman sɔrɔ u yɛrɛw fɛ, minnu y’u bolonɔbilali kɛ.
Wa, ni an ka kan ka san wɔɔɔrɔ laselisɛbɛn kɛ, k’a sɔrɔ cɛsiri min lakodɔnnen don ni bɛnkansɛbɛn bolonɔbilala kuluw ni Mali sɔrɔdasiw cɛ, a waleyali bɛ waati bɛɛ, hali n’a ta bɛɛ SEYƐSIYA wɛrɛw bɛɛ, wa tuma min b’a sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛ, kɛlɛw kunw bɛ kɛ sababu ye baarakɛbagaw (sɔrɔdasi kulu ani Jamana) ka gɛlɛya ye, minnu bɛ tali kɛ caman na, fan kelen ani fan wɛrɛ fɛ, jama ka nin gafe lakodɔnni tɛ.
O de bɛ kɛ sababu ye mɔgɔ minnu bɛ bɛnkansɛbɛn kɔnɔ.
K’a da a kan bi, Bɛnkansɛbɛn bɛ yɛlɛmana, yɛlɛmani belebele si ma se ka bila sen kan kasɔrɔ faraɲɔgɔnkankulu kɔrɔbagaw, minnu tɛ maramafɛnw kɔnɔ, y’u kologɛlɛya ani ka sɔrɔdasi fanga sɔrɔ, bi, Mali kaɲaka kɔnɔ ani k’u yɛlɛma kologɛlɛya tɔgɔlamɔgɔkuluw ma, minnu sigilen don Sahɛli la.
O bɔlen kɔ yen, o de ye Nizɛri perezidan kɔrɔ Mahamadu Isufu bila k’a fɔ ko sɔsɔli ma se, Bɛnkansɛbɛn bilali sen kan bɛ marabolo basigili la ani ko.
Kidali ye bagabagali ye Nizɛri kɔnɔ lakana kama.
Sidi Brahimi Ulidi Sidati ka kɔkɔrɔdon, min ye Alize bɛnkansɛbɛn bolonɔbilalen sɛbɛn, min bolonɔbilala Azawadi jɛkuluw ka Kolatilenjɛkulu ( SEMA ) tɔgɔ la, ye dɛsɛbɛn sɔrɔ, bolodiɲɔgɔnw kɔnɔ, minnu sen don, bɛn ani basigi ɲinini kama Mali kɔnɔ.
Ni Abudulayi Umaru Jɔpu ka taa ye Kɔkankow ani Diɲɛmɔgɔw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ baarada la, ani min ye nin Bɛnkansɛbɛn kɛbaga ye, an jigi b’a la k’a bɛna gɛlɛya di a waleyali kama.
Usumani Mahamani - Kɛlɛbolo fɔlɔw labɛnni, sigidajama cakɛdaw seginni, DEDEYƐRI, yiriwali baarabolodaliw kɛra, dɔwɛrɛw cɛla, kofɔlenw kɛra nin ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn senfɛ. Bɛnkansɛbɛn, bɛn ani bɛnɲini kama, min bɔra Alize taabolo la ani diɲɛmɔgɔw ye, ye ɲɛsigi sɔrɔ Kidali Kɔlɔlɔsilikɛjɛkulu ( SEYƐSIYA ) ka ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn 5nan kɛli la.
Fɔlɔ, kabini bɛnkansɛbɛn bolonɔbila san 2015 mɔgɔ jɔnjɔnw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
A ɲinini fɔlɔ tun kɛra sɛtanburukalo san 2019.
I n’a fɔ gɔfɛrɛnaman bolo ani kuluw maramafɛntigiw ani diɲɛmɔgɔw bolo, taama Kidali, mɔgɔ caman na, tun tɛ dɛsɛ, o tuma, ka nin tɛmɛni taamasiyɛn san kura la bɛn taabolo kɔnɔ.
O la, gɔfɛrɛnaman mɔgɔ wɔɔɔrɔ wɔrɔ ye taama kɛ.
Kolonɛli - mazɔri Isimayɛli Wage ( Jamana Bɛnɲini ), Mamadu Mohamɛdi Kulibali ( Jamana yɛlɛmani ), Mohamɛdi Saliya Ture ( Baara ni degelikalan ), Kolonɛli Modibo Kone ( Lakana ani Sigidalamɔgɔw ka Lakana ) Binu Funɛ Samake ( Musow ani Denw ka Dɛmɛ ) ani Mahamudu Ulidi Mohamɛdi ( Sɛnɛ, Kɛlɛya ani bagabagali )
.
A faseri kɔfɛ Sɔrɔ kan. San 2021 kalo fɔlɔ kɔnɔ, Fekola dugujukɔrɔ ye sanu ɔnsi 125 088 sɔrɔ, n’o ye sanu ɔnsi 7% ( ɔnsi 8 088 ) ye, ka tɛmɛ a bolodalen kan. BEDEGLODE Mali dugujukɔrɔfɛnw ka ɲɛmɔgɔw ye ntɛnɛndon zuwɛnkalo tile 14 tɛmɛnen, u ka san kunnafonidilajɛkulu sigilen kɔnɔ, san tile 3nan, sɛbɛn kɔnɔ.
A sababu ye jɔyɔrɔtigiw bolo ka sigidajama kɛlɛsɛbɛn kɛ, gɛlɛyaw an’u kɛcogoyaw.
U ye kunnafonidilaw ka jaabi ɲɛfɔli kan gɛlɛya kan, min sirilen don Minankoto yɔrɔ fɛnbɔ yamaruyasɛbɛn dili ka di Keɲeba ma.
A ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn tun labɛnna ni BedeGɔlidi Bili Litili ɛmɔgɔba ye, a mɔgɔɲɔgɔnw caman tun bɛ ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
A ka laseli kɔnɔ, ɛmɔgɔba y’a dantigɛ ko san 2020 kɔnɔ, BedeGɔlidi-Mali cakɛda ye dɛmɛ kɛ Mali sɔrɔ la ni sefawari miliyari 34 ɲɔgɔnna ye saraw ani hadamadenya nafamafɛnw la baarakɛlaw ye.
San 2016 – 2020 waati kɔnɔ, Bulu Litili, a ka dugujukɔrɔfɛnw cakɛda ye Sefawari miliyari 162 sɔrɔ Mali gɔfɛrɛnaman ma.
Sigidalamɔgɔw ka yiriwalinafolobɔ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw, DEZE ka fɔ la, bɛ sefawari miliyari 2,1 ɲɔgɔnna, ani sefawari miliyari 82 ɲɔgɔnna, minnu sɔrɔ fɛnw feereli la Mali kɔnɔ.
Fekola dugujukɔrɔfɛn, fɛnni ani kɛcogoyaw. BedeGɔlidi-Mali ɲɛmɔgɔ fɔlɔ y’a dantigɛ ko san 2020, Fekola dugujukɔrɔfɛn ye sanu ɔnsi 622.000 bɔ, n’o bɛ sanu tɔni 18 bɔ.
San 2021 kalo fɔlɔ kɔnɔ, Fekola dugujukɔrɔ ye sanu ɔnsi 125 088 sɔrɔ, n’o ye sanu ɔnsi 7% ( ɔnsi 8 088 ) ye, ka tɛmɛ ɲɛsigilen kan, a y’a ɲɛfɔ, yann’a k’a dantigɛ k’a fɔ ko san 2021 kɔnɔ, Fekola dugujukɔrɔ tun ka kan ka sanu ɔnsi 530 000 ni 560 000 cɛ ( tɔni 16 ɲɔgɔnna ), fɛnsɔngɔw la, minnu bɛ IYƐSI dolari 405 ni 445 cɛ ( SEFAWARI 245.000 ɲɔgɔnna ) ɔnsi kɔnɔ.
Segin bakuruba sɔngɔ ( PEYƐRIZE ) bɛ Lamerikɛn dolariwari 745 ni 785 cɛ ( SEFAWARI 432 000 ɲɔgɔnna ) ɔnsi kɔnɔ.
Sigida baara. San 2020 laban na, BedeGɔlidi tun bɛ Maliden 2 0 53 baara la ani fasoden 130 baara la.
O b’a jira k’a fɔ ko an ka baarakɛjɔ 90c/o ye Mali ye, a y’o dantigɛ, ani k’a fara a kan k’a fɔ k’a fɔ k’an tɛmɛna ka sigida baarakɛjɔw taamasiyɛnniw jɔyɔrɔtigiw kɔnɔ, n’a kɛtɔla ka baarakɛjɔw taamasiyɛn sigida ani jamana kɔnɔ.
hadamadenya jɔyɔrɔtigiyaw ani sigidajama yiriwali. O siratigɛ la, kumalaseli y’a jira k’a fɔ ko san 2021 baarabolodali kuraw bilala ani k’u ta Keɲeba sigidajama yiriwali ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu fɛ.
Kuma bɛɛ kɔnɔ, a bɛn’a pereperelatigɛ ko baarabolodali tan sɛbɛnna ani k’a sɛbɛntigiya ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu fɛ, Fadu, Medinandi, Tiniba, Malaya, Bilaliba, Kolɔnba ani Sokɔndɔ dugukolow ani lamɛnw na, n’a fara Fekola ani Bɛtekili kan.
Bulili ka fɔ la, a ka baarabolodaliw jɔnjɔn bɛɛ jate k’a ye Sefa wari miliyɔn 300 ye.
Fekola solɛri cɛmancɛyɔrɔ ka fɔ la, Bili Litili ka fɔ la, a ka fiyɛn min bɛ Fekola, o ye solɛri bolodalen filanan ye, min bɛ baara kɛ BedeGɔlidi dugujukɔrɔfɛn dɔ kɔnɔ.
Mali gɔfɛrɛnaman ye Fekola S.A ka dugujukɔrɔfɛnw bolodiɲɔgɔn jɔnjɔn jɔnjɔn ye. Nin baarakɛjɛkulu ka baaraw 80% minnu bɛ baara kɛ Keɲeba sɛrikili kɔnɔ, BedeGɔlidi bɛ minɛ ani 20% Mali Jamana bolo.
kunnafonidilaw ka ɲininkaliw kɛra, janko Minankoto fɛnbɔ yamaruyasɛbɛn banni cogoya kan, k’a da BedeGɔlidi ka wari miliyɔn 500 sarali kan, i n’a fɔ vi kɔnɔ.
A ka jaabi kɔnɔ, DEZE Buli Litili ye nin jalakiliw dantigɛ ko tiɲɛnenw ye.
A ka kɔrɔfɔw fɔ la, k’a bɔlen k’a fɔ k’a fɔ ko Bedegɔlidi Mali ka kunnafonidilaw kɔnɔ sɔrɔ foyi si ma di Minankoto yamaruyasɛbɛn ban kama.
AYƐMU Ture - K’a kɔdon kunnafoni dɔw ma, san 2021 mɛkalo tile 7 minisiriɲɛmɔgɔw cɛ minisiriso minisiriso minisirisariya n°2021 lawaliyali, min bɛ peyazi ani peyazi jɔyɔrɔw sigili kan ani k’u ka cɛmancɛyɔrɔw sigili, bɛ kɛ cogoya la.
Wa bisigikumaw, minnu bɛ tali kɛ sɛbɛn falenw ye, tɛ dɔwɛrɛ ye.
Fɔlɔ, jɔyɔrɔ jɔda don, ka minisirisariya kɔnɔn dɔn, yaasa ka gɛlɛya, min ɲɛnabɔra, faamuya kɛ.
Nin minisiriw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ latigɛlisɛbɛn, a ka sariyasen 2 kɔnɔ, b’a dantigɛ ko jɔyɔrɔ sigilenw bɛ tali kɛ a ɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw wele kɔfɛ, sariyaw labatoli la, minnu bɛ senna.
Sariyasen 3 b’a jira k’a fɔ ko peyazi jɔyɔrɔ sɛbɛnni kɛra peyazi warisoba sarali ye, min ka sɔngɔw sigilen don nin cogo la.
Silikɛli sabaw kama, sɔngɔ bɛ sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 250 sɔrɔ ani ka tɛmɛ tɛmɛnen na.
mobili kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw kama (250F sɛbɛn ani tɛmɛsɛbɛn fɛ).
takisiw ( Sefa wari 250 sɛbɛn ani tɛmɛsɛbɛn fɛ).
forobakɛyɔrɔw ka mɔgɔ minnu ka ca ka tɛ mɔgɔ 25 ye (250 F sɛbɛn ani tɛmɛsɛbɛn fɛ).
Kamiyɔni minnu bɛ tali kɛ baarakɛminɛnw ta ye (300 F sɛbɛn ani tɛmɛsɛbɛn fɛ).
Baarakɛw ani taamakɛw minnu ka mɔgɔ kan ka ca mɔgɔ 25 ye ( Sefa wari 300 sɔrɔ ani tɛmɛtɛmɛ fɛ).
jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ (jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ 300 )
A jɔda fana ka dantigɛlisɛbɛn dɔ la, ko cɛmancɛsɛbɛn sariya bɛ se ka lakurayali san kelen-kelen, taamafɛnw kɛcogoya magoɲɛsigi kɔfɛ, k’a kɛcogo yɛlɛmaniya kɔnɔ.
Wa peyazi jɔyɔrɔw kɔrɔfɛjɔyɔrɔw jamaw bɛ nafa sɛbɛnkasɛbɛn sɔrɔ, min ka diya cogoyaw an’a sɔngɔ sigilen don sirabakanw bɛ minisiri ka latigɛ fɛ.
O bɔlen kɔ yen, nin minisiri cɛ latigɛlisɛbɛn sariyasen 4 b’a fɔ ko peyazi ani pesazi jɔyɔrɔ, min ma dɛmɛ sɔrɔ, bɛ tali kɛ mobili ɲɛmɔgɔw fɛ, fo ka se baaraɲɔgɔn dɔ ka baara la.
Peyazi sɔngɔw, minnu bɛ bɔ nin latigɛlisɛbɛn sariyasen 2 waleyali la, bɛna tilali kɛ cogoyaw kɔnɔ, minnu sigilen don minisirisɛbɛn fɛ.
Ani fana, a ka sariyasen 7 ka fɔ la, ɲɛmɔgɔw ye nin minisiri waleyali jɔyɔrɔtigiw ye.
Jamana sirakanw ɲɛmɔgɔ, jamana dugukolow, dugukolow ani dugukolow taamakow ɲɛmɔgɔ, sirakanw ɲɛmɔgɔ zenerali, zandarama ɲɛmɔgɔ zenerali, polisi ɲɛmɔgɔ zenerali, fasodenya lakana ɲɛmɔgɔ, dugukolow maramafɛnw ɲɛmɔgɔ, maramafɛnw ka maramafɛnw ɲɛmɔgɔ, maramafɛnw ka maramafɛnw ɲɛmɔgɔ, maramafɛnw ka maramafɛnw ɲɛmɔgɔ.
Fɛn bɛɛ bɛ kɛ ɲuman!
Min ye a waleyali ko ye kɛnɛ kan, a kɛra cogoya la, ka fɔ k’a fɔ cogo min kɛra Sirabakankɛyɔrɔ ɲɛmɔgɔba, Lala Koyite, ka taama tɛmɛnen dɔ senfɛ.
ni hadamadenya baarakɛɲɔgɔnw fara ɲɔgɔn kan.
O sababu la, sirabakankɛyɔrɔ ɲɛmɔgɔba, Lala Koyite, y’a ɲini ka sɛbɛnbɔli sɛbɛntiyɔrɔw ani mankannin sɛbɛntiyɔrɔw kɛli la.
A ka fɔ la, sɛbɛn minɛnnenw bɛ fɛn bɛɛ kɔnɔ minnu ka kan.
Min ye sɛbɛn minɛnenw ye, u bɛ tɛmɛ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la ani waatini kɔnɔ, jɔyɔrɔ kuraw la, minnu sigira walima minnu sigilen don gɛlɛya kɔnɔ, walasa ka mago mago ɲɛnabɔ.
Nin sɛbɛn ninnu bɛ tali kɛ mɔgɔ tɔgɔ numɛri, peyazi jɔyɔrɔ yɔrɔ, taama ɛmɔgɔyaso ka sɛbɛn, walasa k’a ka tiɲɛtigiya hakililatigɛ.
Mmu Lala Koyite b’a hakililatigɛ k’a fɔ ko sɛbɛn falenw tɛ yen, k’a kɛɲɛsin kunnafoniw ma minnu sirilen bɛ, ani ko sɛbɛn mankutuw bɛna bɔ siratigɛ la kabini sɛbɛn falenw sarali bɛna sɔrɔ.
O la, ko bɛɛ bɛ ka ɲɛ ni ɲuman ye sisan!
Burama Keyita - A bɛ tali kɛ Bamakɔ dugukolo kɔnɔn kɛrɛnkɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw yɛlɛmancɛyɔrɔ dɔ labɛnni ye, min bɛna nata la.
Nin jɛkulu, min bɛna sigi Sanankɔrɔba komini kɔnɔ, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la Sinina, bɛna sen don Bamakɔ belebele la kominiw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ siratigɛ hukumu kɔnɔ.
Bamakɔ Disiriki mɛri, Adama Sangare ani SAER Gɔlɔpu Jaje ɲɛmɔgɔ, n’a bɛ fɔ a ma Amadu Sankare, ka ɲɛsin Dugujukɔrɔfɛnw, Kuranko ani jiko minisiri, Lamini Seyidu Tarawore, ka kumalaseli kɔnɔ, ye bolodiɲɔgɔnma sɛbɛn bolonɔbila alamisadon zuwɛnkalo tile 17 tɛmɛnen, ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn Kolekɛli la, min bɛ tali kɛ baarabolodali baarabolodali kan, min bɛ tali kɛ dugujukɔrɔfɛnw yɛlɛmani ɲɛmɔgɔyaso sigili ani ɲɛnabɔli kan.
Mɔgɔba caman tun bɛ mɔgɔya kɔnɔ, minnu cɛla E2S Energy Solution System ɛmɔgɔ, SAER Grɔpu mɔgɔ jɛkulu dɔ, baarabolodali kɛbaga, Fode Ibarahima Maguiraga ani Sanankɔrɔba mɛri bɛ minnu na.
Nin bolodiɲɔgɔnma kura, min bolonɔbilala Disiriki Miri ni SAƐRI ka Energy Solution Sɛsɛmɛni E2S ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ, bɛ kɛ Bamakɔ dugukolo kɔnɔnyeba dɔ labɛnni ye, min bɛ kɛ sɔrɔ k’a kɛ sɔrɔ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya ye.
Nin baarabolodali, min bɛ fɛ ka mɔgɔw ka bɔlɔlɔsili kologɛlɛya, sɔsɔli t’a la, bɛ ɲɛfɔ ɲɛmɔgɔw ka ɲɛmɔgɔya jira k’a ka mɔgɔw ka kɛrɛnkɛrɛnɛyɔrɔ labɛnni jama ka hɛrɛ kama.
O de la, SIV mɛri, Adama Berete, ye baaradaw ɲɛmɔgɔw wele, minnu bɛ waleyali baaraw ɲɛnabɔ, u ka magan si dɛsɛ, walasa ka laɲiniw, minnu ɲininen don nin bolonɔbilali fɛ, ka ɲɛnabɔ.
A ka baarabolodali laselisɛbɛn kɔnɔ, EEDEYƐSI ɛmɔgɔ, Fode Ibarahima Magiraga, y’a dantigɛ ko baarabolodali laɲini ye ka dɛmɛ don Bamakɔ Disiriki kɔlɔsilikɛlɛyali gɛlɛya ɲɛnabɔli la ani k’a hakililatigɛ k’a ka dɛmɛ fara ɲɔgɔn kan ni kɔrɔfɛnbɔli ye Mali kɔnɔ.
Nin jɛkulu, min bɛna sigi Sanankɔrɔba komini kɔnɔ, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la Sinina, bɛna sen don Bamakɔ Mɔgɔba la, sigida cɛɲɔgɔnya hukumu kɔnɔ.
A ka fɔ la, o yɔrɔ bɛna tɛgɛtɛrɛ 1500 ɲɔgɔnna sɔrɔ, walasa ka MW 40 sɔrɔ.
A labɛnni sɔngɔ bɛ jate k’a ye SEFAWARI miliyari 130 ye, a bɛna baaraw dɔrɔmɛ 6000 sɔrɔ, ka tɛmɛ ani ka tɛmɛ.
SEYƐRI Kulu ɛmɔgɔ, Jaje n’a bɛ fɔ a ma Amadu Sankare, y’a pereperelatigɛ k’a fɔ ko Sanankɔrɔba sugandili ka nin kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen don kɛcogoya la t’a la.
Bawo, a ka fɔ la, k’a kɔrɔn ni Gine – Sikasso – Bamako kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen jɔyɔrɔ jɔyɔrɔ ye ani min tɔgɔ bɛ fɔ a ma Bukili Kɔrɔn.
Kuranko bɔli min bɛ sɔrɔ EYƐMU tɔgɔyɔrɔ kɔnɔ, bɛna gɛlɛya.
Yaan’a k’a dantigɛ k’a fɔ ko a kɔnɔn cogoya lakana, nin baarabolodali lawaliyali kɔnɔ, ka tɛmɛ dɔwɛrɛ labɛnni an’a fɛn mɔgɔw bɛ minɛ nin laban na.
A y’a kuncɛ ka wele bila mɔgɔw bɛɛ ka bɛnkansɛbɛn na, baarabolodali ka ɲɛsigi ɲuman kama, jama ka nafa bɛɛ kama.
O cɛmancɛyɔrɔ labɛnni bɛna dɛmɛ sɔrɔ Bamakɔ dugu lakana la.
Kuma kɔnɔ, ka Bamakɔ kɛ dugukolo yɛrɛ ye. Disiriki mɛri, Adama Sangare, ka fɔ la, o siratigɛ la hakilinaw tɛ dɛsɛ, nka Jamana ŋaniya an’a bilasirali de tɛ dɛsɛ waati bɛɛ.
Yanni a ka nisɔntiya ni nin bolodiɲɔgɔnma bolonɔbila ye a ka dugujukɔrɔfɛnw ni EEDEYƐSI cɛ, k’a kɛ kɔrɔfɛjɔw yɛlɛmani cɛmancɛyɔrɔ dɔ sigili kama.
A laban na, a y’a ɲini mɔgɔ bɛɛ ka bilasirali kama baarabolodali ka ɲɛsigi kama.
Amure - Nin ye siɲɛ fɔlɔ ye, SEYƐSIYA ka ɲɔgɔnye bɛ kɛ Kidali, ɲinini caman kɔfɛ.
A kɛra Alizeri kɔkankow minisiri, SE Sabiri Bukadumu ka ɲɛmɔgɔya kɔnɔ, bɛnɲini minisiri, Kolonɛli Isimayɛli Wage ani Gɔfɛrɛnaman mɔgɔ wɛrɛw, Plateformu ani SEMA maramafɛnkuluw tɔgɔlamɔgɔw,
Minisima tɔgɔlamɔgɔ ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn na, ye Mali fan fɛ ani diɲɛmɔgɔw ka kunnafonidilaw fɛ mɔgɔw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ ka kɛɲɛ ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ ka kɛɲɛ ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
S.E.M. Zan-Yves Le Drian, Faransi Jamana ka Eropu ani Kɔkankow minisiri ani Afiriki kelenyatɔn Bɛn ani Lakana Komisɛri, S.E.M. Sɛmɛli Sɛrigi, y’a ɲini k’u sen don baaraw la, ka tɛmɛ kɛ Mahamati Salehi Annadifu fɛ, Diɲɛtɔn Sekeretɛri zenerali Tɔgɔlamɔgɔ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen y’a dantigɛ ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kɔfɛ ko « san duuru bɛ ne sen don SEYƐSIYA la ani nin ye siɲɛ fɔlɔ ye SEYƐSIYA sɔrɔ ni nin mɔgɔ minnu sen bɛ sen don
O bɛ fɛ k’a fɔ ko diɲɛmɔgɔw bɛɛ bɛ ɲɔgɔndɛmɛ kɛ Mali la ani a labɛnnen don ka Mali bilasira nin dakun kura kɔnɔ ani danaya de bɛ sɛmɛntiya, politiki ŋaniya yɛrɛ ye, min y’a jira.
Min ye Kolonɛli - mazɔri Isimayɛli Wage ko ye, Jamana Bɛnɲini minisiri y’a da tulow kan ko « danaya hakilina dɔ bɔra fɔlɔ la, ɲɔgɔn caman faamuya ka bɔ a la.
O la, jɔda b’a jira k’a fɔ ko y’a latigɛ ko Mali pariti bɛ to ka danaya kokɛtaw kologɛlɛyali kɛ ni wale kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw ye, ka taa lakana koɲɛw kan ani ka taabolo kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya kan, min sigira bɛɛɛ la, yaasa an bɛ se ka taa nin kan tiɲɛ na, ni gɛlɛyaw taamasiyɛn ye bɛɛ kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la.
Mohamɛdi Lamini Ulidi Sidadi, SEMA ɲɛmɔgɔya bɛ min na, ka fɔ la, « an ye baara kɛ Malidenw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
A labɛnni kɛra ni Kidali marabolo gɔfɛrɛnɛri ye, wa Malidenw de ye nin ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn labɛn, anw Malidenw de tun y’a lakana.
« SEYƐSIYA de bɔra siɲɛ fɔlɔ la, nin ɲɔgɔnye Kidali marabolo kɔnɔ, siga t’a la, o ye bɛn, bɛnɲini taamasiyɛn ye Mali denw ni ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
Nin ɲɔgɔnye ye Mali kɔnɔn bɛɛ kɛbagaw bɛɛ ka bɛn kama ŋaniya sɛbɛn », Habala AG Hamnatta, tɔgɔlamɔgɔ ka kumalasela y’o ɲɛfɔ.
« Ka Mali jɔnjɔn filɛ ka taa Kidali dugu kan, n’o ye dusukunnako ye an bolo.
Mali mɔgɔ ɲuman bɛɛ jɛlen don nin wale la ka taa labɛnni labɛnni seginni kan Mali kɔnɔ, Kolonɛli Modibo Kone, Sigidalamɔgɔw ka Lakana ani Lakana minisiri,
SEYƐSIYA taamasiyɛn ka kan ka kɛ DEDEYƐRI taabolo kan, fangabulonkow yɛlɛmaniw sennateli, dɔwɛrɛw cɛla.
An ka hakilijigin kɛ ko Jamana bɛnkankuluw fanba b’a ɲini ka Bɛnkansɛbɛn bɛn kama lakuraya.
Berɛhima Jalo Jamana ntolatan tɔn bɛ na kɛ a ka ntolatanɲɔgɔnkunbɛn sabanan ani laban ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn na FIFA donw hukumu kɔnɔ ( zuwɛnkalo 2021 ) ni Tinizi cɛ.
A ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn bɛ na kɛ tarata zuwɛnkalo tile 15 Hamadi Agɛrɛbi ntolatanyɔrɔ la Rades.
O ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn bila Esiptika jalatigɛli ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn saba ma.
Kiritigɛla, Ibarahima Nuredinin, bɛna dɛmɛ kɛ a bɛnkanɲɔgɔnw, Ahmad Tufik ani Hani Abedɛlfatata, fɛ.
Kiritigɛla, min bɛ yɔrɔ, bɛna kɛ tunisiyɛn Yusiri Buli ye.
Dɛsɛfɛn kɔ Alize ( 0 – 1 ), zuwɛnkalo tɛmɛnen, ntolatanɲɔgɔnkunbɛn fɔlɔ senfɛ, ntolatan si tɛ sɔrɔ ka sin ƐRIDE Kɔngɔ ma ( 1 – 1 ), alamisadon tɛmɛnen, Tinisi la, Mali Samatasɛgɛw bɛna ɲini ka bɔ Tunisikaw ɲɛkɔrɔ.
Mohamɛdi Magasuba cɛw ma sugandili wɛrɛ sɔrɔ ni sebagaya ye.
Nin ntolatan senfɛ, Tinizi bɛna kɛ ntolatanna ɲɛmɔgɔ caman ye, i n’a fɔ Yusɛfu Makini, Ferjani Sassi, Dyalan Brɔni walima Wahibi Kasari.
Alamisadon tɛmɛnen, Samatasɛgɛw ye ntolatan sɛbɛn sɔrɔ ka sin ƐRIDE Kɔngɔ Levariw ma (1-1).
A daminɛna kɔfɛjɔ kɔfɛjɔ kɔnɔ, mɔgɔ minnu tɛ sɔrɔlenw bolo, ƐFISE Nantes ntolatanna, Kalifa Kulibali, b’a sɔrɔ kasɔrɔ, bɛ daminɛni jaabi dayɛlɛ Agiliw bolo ( miniti 4nan ).
A labɛnni kɛra kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen ye, jamana tɔn ye ntolatan taamasiyɛn sɔrɔ, nka a ma se ka donni fila sɔrɔ.
Waati filanan kɔnɔ, Kiasumu de ye, min y’a latigɛ Kɔgɔdɔw ka celu kɔnɔ, n’a tun ye mobiliw sɔrɔ ka sin Dunbiya ma ( miniti 55nan ).
Leopariw tun b’u nɔgɔya ntolatan laban na wa u laban tun b’a la sɔrɔ a la Kolo fɛ, min sɔrɔla Munikɔrɔ fɛ.
Nka Karamɔgɔ Kasabalanka ka ntolatanna, Bɛn Malango, laban na, ntolatan tɛ sɔrɔ, n’a y’a ɲɔgɔn sɔrɔ Moutusami ka ntolatan sɔrɔ ( miniti 86nan ).

Alize bɛnkansɛbɛn kɔfɛ, a y’a ka ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn fɔlɔ bɛɛ kɛ Kidali, sɔsɔli fila kɛlen kɔfɛ ani kumaɲɔgɔn caman kɔfɛ fan bɛ bolonɔbilala fan kelen ani fan wɛrɛ fɛ, ɲɛmɔgɔ kuraw, minnu y’u ka danaya jira nin ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kɛli kama.
SEYƐSIYA ka ɲɔgɔnye, min sigilen don Bamakɔ kɔnɔ, ye Afiriki ani Eropikaw ka jamanaw caman ka ɲɔgɔnye ye, minnu na, Faransi ani Etazini tɔgɔlamɔgɔw, i n’a fɔ ONI tɔgɔlamɔgɔ Mali la, nka nin ɲɔgɔnye 5nan, min bɛ SEYƐSIYA ɲɔgɔnye la, kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen ye Faransi kɔkankow minisiri ka sen donni ye, min y’a kɛnɛ bila visiyokɔnferansi fɛ ani min ye SEYƐSIYA ka nin ɲɔgɔnye di Kidali ni taamasiyɛn ye.
Afiriki kelenyatɔn Bɛn ani Lakana Komisɛri fana tun kɛra sanfɛlɛ sanfɛ.
Nin ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kuntaala senfɛ, ɲininkaliw bɛɛ tun bɛ kumafalenw kɔnɔ, k’a fara Kidali sariya kan, min tolen don halibi koɲɛ caman ye, DEDEYƐRI ( Maramafɛn kɛlɛyali, Senbɔli kɛlɛyali, Senbɔli kɛlɛyali ) gɛlɛya min labɛnnen don.
Bɛnɲini minisiri, Kolonɛli Isimayɛli Wage, y’a jira k’a fɔ sisan k’a fɔ ko kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen marabolo kɔrɔ kɔrɔbaga 400 ye degelikaramɔgɔw la ka Mali maramafɛnw sen don, n’a bɛ fɔ ko labɛnnenw don.
A kofɔra fana hadamadenya cakɛdaw seginni kan Kidali nin siratigɛ la, Minisima y’a latigɛ k’i jɛkulu kɔnɔ yaasa ka nin baarabolodali nafolobɔ, dolari miliyɔn kelen sɔrɔ.
Ko min ye SEYƐSIYA ka nin ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn kunbɛn ye Kidali, o ye jamana tɔgɔlamɔgɔw yɛlɛnni ye dugu kan kabini kalo damadɔ.
An ka hakilijigin kɛ ko Mali darapo y’a ta Kidali dugu kan IBEKA ka fanga kɔnɔ Minisiriɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ, Dɔgɔtɔrɔ Bubu Sise, ka taama senfɛ.
Usumani M. Tarawore - Mali gɔfɛrɛnaman ye bolodiɲɔgɔn jɔnjɔn jɔnjɔn jɔnjɔn ye BedeGɔlidi kama, a ɲɛmɔgɔ, William Bili Litili, ka fɔ la Mali la.
BedeGɔlidi Mali ɲɛmɔgɔ, William Bili Litili, ani a ka baarakɛdenw ye kunnafonidilajɛ dɔ labɛn, zuwɛnkalo tɛmɛnen, dugujukɔrɔfɛnw cakɛda sigibaju la, walasa ka san 2020 sɛbɛn kɛ, ka gɛlɛyaw dantigɛ, minnu sɔrɔ, yann’a ka ɲɛnabɔcogoyaw bila.
Bili Litili ka fɔ la, sɔrɔko sebagaya, min sɔrɔla san 2020 la, nafa sɔrɔ baarakɛbagaw ani fan caman wɛrɛw ma, minnu sen bɛ Mali la, a y’o dantigɛ.
BedeGɔlidi ye SEFAWARI miliyari 34 saraliw ani hadamadenya nafamafɛnw kɔnɔ, miliyari 162 gɔfɛrɛnaman ye, sigidajamaw ka yiriwalinafolobɔ miliyari 2,1 ani fɛnw miliyari 82 sɔrɔ Mali la.
San 2020 kɔnɔ, Fekola dugujukɔrɔfɛn ye sanu ɔnsi 622 000 bɔ.
San 2021 kalo fɔlɔ kɔnɔ, Fekola dugujukɔrɔfɛn tɛmɛna a ka sebagaya ɲumanw kan, ni sanu ɔnsi 125 088 bɔli ye, k’a bɛn 7% ( 8 088 ) ma, ka tɛmɛ ɲɛsigilen kan.
San 2021 kɔnɔ, Fekola dugujukɔrɔ tun ka kan ka sanu ɔnsi 530 000 ni 560 000 cɛ, fɛn sɔngɔw bɛ minnu cɛ, minnu bɛ Lamerikɛn dolari 405 ni 445 cɛ, ɔnsi kelen ani ɲɔgɔndan sɔngɔ ( ƐRIZEYƐRI ) bɛ minnu bɛ Lamerikɛn dolari 745 ni 785 cɛ, ɔnsi kelen.
mɔgɔ bɛ se ka kalan kunnafoni sɛbɛn dɔ kɔnɔ, min bilala kunnafonidilaw ma.
Bili Litili ka fɔ la, BedeGɔlidi cakɛda bɛ jɔda jɔda kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya la sigida baarakɛlaw tali la ani sigidajama yiriwali la.
San 2020 laban na, BedeGɔlidi tun bɛ Maliden 2 053 baara kɛ ani cɛmancɛ 130 baara kɛ.
O b’a jira k’a fɔ ko an ka baarakɛjɔ 94 % ye Mali ye.
A y’o dantigɛ.

A ye bolonɔbilali baarabolodali kofɔ.
Dugujukɔrɔfɛn kɛnɛyako baarabolodali ( PEDEYƐRI ), degelikalan ni baaraɲɔgɔn cogoya baarabolodali Keɲeba sɛrikili kɔnɔ ( AYƐFEYƐKI ) ani bolodiɲɔgɔnya ni Inyɛsifu ye, denmisɛnw ani denmisɛnw ka yɛrɛmahɔrɔnya kama Mali la.
Kɛnɛba sigida yiriwali ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu ye baarabolodali kuraw sɛbɛn ani k’u ta san 2021.
K’a fara ɲɔgɔn kan, baarabolodali tan sɛbɛnna ani k’a sɛmɛntiya ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu fɛ, Fadu, Medinandi, Tiniba, Malaya, Baliba, Kolomba, Sokondo, Fekola ani Bɛtekili dugukolow ani hadamadenw nafa kama.
Baarabolodaliw mumɛ bakuruba ye Sefa wari miliyɔn 300 ye.

BedeGɔlidi Mali ɲɛmɔgɔ y’a cakɛda baarakɛlaw ka dusukasi an’u cɛsiri barika.
Siaka Dunbiya, BedeGɔlidi ( Kanada ) ka jamanaw cɛ perezidandankan, Bili Litili bɛ na Bamakɔ ka dugujukɔrɔfɛnw cakɛda segin, kabini Mohamɛdi Jara ka banni kɛra mɛkalo tile 17 tɛmɛnen, dugujukɔrɔfɛnw yamaruyasɛbɛn dili koɲɛ dɔ kɔfɛ.
BedeGɔlidi – Mali ɲɛmɔgɔ kura ye kunnafonidilajɛ dɔ labɛn, nin ntɛnɛndon zuwɛnkalo tile 14.
-maliweb.net- A ɲɔgɔnye laɲini, min y’a dantigɛ ni kunnafonidilaw ye, tun ye dugujukɔrɔfɛnw cakɛda ka baaraw jira kabini a sigili.
O n’a ta bɛɛ, kunnafonidilaw, minnu sirilen don Manankoto yɔrɔ fɛnbɔ yamaruyasɛbɛn bilali kura kofɔli la, y’a wele bila kumafalen kɔnɔ.
ɛmɔgɔ ka kuma fɔlenw na, k’a bɔlen k’a fɔ ko Bedegɔlidi Mali ka kunnafonidilaw b’a la, foyi si sɔrɔ Manankoto yamaruyasɛbɛn ban kama.
Lajɛlikɛla ka fɔ la, Manankoto yɔrɔ min bɛ Keɲeba la, fɛnbɔ yamaruyasɛbɛn sɔrɔla a ka baarada fɛ san 2012 dugujukɔrɔfɛnw sariyasun sigisariya kan.
Nka, san 2019 dugujukɔrɔfɛnw sariyasun sigibaju de kan dugujukɔrɔfɛnw minisiri ye fɛnbɔ yamaruyasɛbɛn di.
O n’a ta bɛɛ, Bedegɔlidi y’i sɔrɔ gɔfɛrɛnaman ka maganw bɛɛ ma.
Mɔgɔ yɛrɛ gɛlɛya si tɛ anw ni minisiri ye.
Bili Litili y’o dantigɛ.
Nka, ɲɛmɔgɔ b’a jate ko mara gɛlɛya tun ka kan ka kɛ.
Kiribulonba y’a minɛ.
Mohamɛdi Jara, ɲɛmɔgɔ kɔrɔ ka senbɔli kan, laselisɛbɛn b’a jate k’a y’i senbɔ a yɛrɛ ɲɛmɔgɔya la.
A ko cogoya tun ka gɛlɛn, o tuma a y’i senbɔ mɔgɔw ka hɛrɛ kama.
BedeGɔlidi ɲɛmɔgɔ kura y’o sɛmɛntiya.
Bi, Manankoto yamaruyasɛbɛn sɛbɛn bɛ Kiribulonba ɲɛkɔrɔ.
BedeGɔlidi ka ɲini, ka latigɛ ta, walasa ka sɔrɔbaga kura ka baaraw dulon, ma lamɛn kiriso mɔgɔw fɛ.
An bɛ kiritigɛli makɔnɔ nafolokow kan.
Bili y’o dantigɛ, min t’a ka sɛbɛn bila diɲɛ kiriso ɲɛkɔrɔ, n’o ka kan.

Komini tɔn ka kɔlɔsili y’a sababu kɛ, san fila ɲɛnabɔli kɔnɔ, ka se Sefa wari miliyɔn 208 ( Sefa wari miliyɔn 208, 143, 777 ) kan Mɛri kɛsu kɔnɔ.
Mɛri Mamuru Kulibali ka gɛlɛya gɛlɛya kosɛbɛ.
Jɔyɔrɔ belebele.
Nin jɛɲɔgɔnw fana.
K’a kɛ tiɲɛni ye!
Bi, an nisɔndiyara k’a fɔ ko an ye Buguni Mɛri baarakɛlaw ye.
K’a da a kan, dugujukɔrɔfɛnaman y’a jɔyɔrɔ sɔrɔ.
Nafolokow yɔrɔtigiw la, jɔnjɔn dɔ b’a fara Mɛri baarakɛlaw ka baara la.
Kasɔrɔ a tɛ mɔgɔw kɛcogoya kɔnɔ, minnu tɛ ban ka laban komini tɔn kɔnɔ.
A ka dugujukɔrɔfɛnmarabolow ɲɛnabɔli cogoya, n’a ka dugujukɔrɔfɛnmarabolow ɲɛnabɔbaga dɔ b’a ka dugujukɔrɔfɛnmarabolow ɲɛnabɔli cogoya gɛlɛya sɛbɛn ni nin kumakanw ye.
Yanni a ka fara a kan, emu.
fɛn min bɛ an ɲini an ka ɲɛmɔgɔw fɛ, o ye ka nin wulikajɔw kɛbagaw bila kiriso ɲɛkɔrɔ.
Wa kasɔrɔ a ma kɛ, an ka bɔ an ka dugujukɔrɔfɛjɛkɛyɔrɔ bɔli la, min ye Buguni dugujukɔrɔfɛjɛkɛyɔrɔfɛjɛkɛyɔrɔfɛjɛkɛyɔrɔ yɛlɛmaba kɔnɔ.
An ka kunnafonisunw ka fɔ la, Buguni Mɛri bɛ gɛlɛya kɔnɔ.
Kɔlɔlɔsiliw, ɲɔgɔn cɛ, ɲɔgɔn cɛ.
tun bɛna kɛ nin dugujukɔrɔfɛrɛnaman ka fatura yɔrɔ minɛnnen ye, n’a ta bɛ k’a lahidu kɛ ɲɔgɔnkunbɛn ɲuman ye.
Fɔlɔ, ɲɛnabɔcogo gɛlɛya.
Ka da an kumaɲɔgɔnw dantigɛ, a bɛ gɛlɛya sɔrɔ ni duuru ye.
Wa bi, san duuru bɛ gɛlɛya la.
K’a ta san 2017 zanwiyekalo la ka taa san 2019 desamburu la, an kumalaselaw b’a ɲɛfɔ, Buguni Mɛri, Mamuru Kulibali ani a ka tɔn ka farikoloɲɛnajɛ fɔlen kɛra nafoloko kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen ye, min y’a yɛrɛ bila Gabegi fɛ.
A gafew siratigɛ kan, baarakɛden dɔ b’a ɲɛfɔ Mɛri ka kɔnɔdon kɔlɔsilikɛyɔrɔ labɛnni tɛ kɛcogoya kan.
A b’a fara a kan, fɛn minnu bɔra DAO feere la, k’a jate sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 950 000 ma, ani karamɔgɔw ka saraw sarali, minnu tɛ bɔ Buguni Komini kɔnɔ, k’a jate sefawari miliyon 126,7 ma ( Sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 26 712 156 ) ma.
Wari wɛrɛw, minnu bilalen bɛ Buguni Mɛri ɲɛnabɔli kɔnɔ, dugujukɔrɔfɛnw yɛlɛmani taabolo taabolo sɛbɛnni tɛ wari hakɛ sɔrɔ, k’a sɔrɔ miliyɔn 53 hakɛ ye an ka faraɲɔgɔn cɛ ( SEFAWARI miliyɔn 53.999.750 ) ani sɔrɔ wari hakɛ sɛbɛnni t’a sɔrɔ miliyɔn 10 hakɛ sɔrɔ ( SEFAWARI miliyɔn 104.124. 250 ).
Wa, an ka kunnafonisunw ka fɔ la, tiɲɛ b’a la, ko Buguni Mɛri, Mamuru Kulibali, bɛ nafaw sɔrɔ a yɛrɛ la, ni sefa wari miliyɔn 3,8 ye ( Sefa wari miliyɔn 3 ani 75.000 ) hakɛ ye.
Magan kɔnɔ, Buguni Mɛri baarakɛlaw b’a jira k’a fɔ ko jɔyɔrɔtigiyaw, minnu bɛ tali kɛ komini tɔn ɲɛnabɔli kɔnɔ, ye sariyasunba ani sariyasunba taabolo ye.
Nafolokow gɛlɛyaw b’u fara a kan nafolokow ɲɛnabɔli la.
Wa an ka kumaɲɔgɔnw b’u tɛmɛ k’a fɔ ko Mɛri ɲɛmɔgɔw ka fanga baarakɛbagaw t’u jɔyɔrɔw an’u jɔyɔrɔtigiw ta bɛɛ, fɛn bɛɛ min kɛ ka dɛsɛ ka kɛ jaabiw sɔrɔli la, minnu jate b’a la.
O bɔlen na, dɛsɛw, minnu sɔrɔla fasodenya ɲɛnabɔli hukumu kɔnɔ, b’a bali Buguni dugujukɔrɔfɛrɛnaman ka baaraw di fasodenw ma, k’a kɛ cogoya la ani k’a kɛ cogoya ye.
Min ye dugujukɔrɔfɛnw ani dugujukɔrɔfɛnw ɲɛnabɔli ko ye, an ka kunnafonisunw b’a jira k’a fɔ ko Buguni Mɛri ma walew kɛ, minnu ka kan, ka laɲiniw sɔrɔ, minnu bɛ bila a ma, k’a fasodenw kunnafoni ani ɲɛnabɔli hɛrɛ, dugujukɔrɔfɛnw laseli senfɛ.
Baarakɛlaw taamasiyɛn dɛsɛli labɛnnen tɛ, o bɛ KUBU ka baarakɛlaw ka baaraɲɔgɔnma sɔrɔli kɛ kosɛbɛ.
Wa bi, dugujukɔrɔfɛnw kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen, i n’a fɔ a b’a la Buguni Mɛri kɔnɔ, tɛ dɛsɛ, k’a da a kan gafew, minnu ka kan, ka tɛmɛ kɛnɛ kan, walasa ka fɛnw kɔlɔsili ani lakana hakililatigɛ.
Ka da an kumalaselaw ka dantigɛlisɛbɛnw gɛlɛya la, Buguni Komini ɛmɔgɔyakulu ka kolatigɛjɛkulu ye nafaw di Mɛri Mamuru Kulibali, Mɛri biro mɔgɔw, sigida baarakɛlaw, baarakɛjɛkulu baarakɛjɛkuluw mɔgɔw, ani dɛmɛniw ma, fɛɛrɛ dɔw ma, minnu bɛ bila Jamana kɔnɔ.
Ani an ka kunnafonisunw ka hakililatigɛ.
Sɛgɛsɛgɛlikɛla, Buguni Mɛri la, y’a jira k’a fɔ ko Komini ɲɛmɔgɔyakulu bɛ nafaw di minnu na, minnu bɛ nafaw kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw na, nafoloko kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw ani dɔgɔtɔrɔfɛnw bɛ minnu na.
Nin nafaw sɔrɔbagaw ye.
Mɛri, dugujukɔrɔfɛnw biro mɔgɔw, sigida baarakɛlaw ani baarakɛjɛkulu baarakɛjɛkulu mɔgɔw.
Yanni a k’a pereperelatigɛ.
San 2010 zuwɛnkalo tile 28 laselisɛbɛn n° 005 / SEYƐSEBE kɔfɛ, Mɛri Mamuru Kulibali ye san 2017 mɛkalo tile 29 baarasɛbɛn n° 06 / SEYUBE bilasɛbɛn ta, min bɛ laselisɛbɛn bila Mɛri ka nafa kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnen kelen waleyali kama.
O la, sefa wari 125 000 bɔra kalo kɔnɔ Mɛri tɔgɔ la, min kan Sefa wari 75 000 ye nafoloko dɛmɛ ye ani Sefa wari 50 000 ye Mɛri ka kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenya ani talifoni sarali kama.
O n’a ta bɛɛ, nin nafaw tɛ labɛnnen don sariyasɛbɛn fɛ, min bɛ senna.
Wari hakɛ bakuruba, min sara Mɛri ma, sɛgɛsɛgɛli waati kɔnɔ, bɛ sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 3 ani 875 000 la.
Dɔwɛrɛ wɛrɛ la, an ka kunnafonisunw b’a fara a kan ko Buguni Mɛri ka wari Tɔgɔlamɔgɔ ma segin ka bɔ fɛn minnu bɛ tali kɛ fɛn weleyali sɛbɛnw ( DEWO ) feere la forobakɛbaga la.
An ka wari miliyɔn 1,8 mumɛ kan ( SEFAWARI miliyɔn (1 850 000), sɛgɛsɛgɛli baara ma sɔrɔ sɛgɛsɛgɛliw sɔrɔ, k’a da SEFAWARI miliyɔn 900 000 hakɛ kan.
Dawo feerew jɔnjɔnw bakuruba, minnu ma segin kɛ, ye Sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 950 000 ye.
Wa o tɛ fɛn o ye.
K’a yɔrɔ jan ka kan.
Buguni Mɔgɔmɔgɔyaso Mɛri Mamuru Kulibali fana tɛ ɲangiliw waleya sugufiyɛw kan, minnu waleyali tɛmɛnen don.
O cogo la, sɛgɛsɛgɛlikɛlaw n°046/KUBE DRMP – DEYƐSIPE SIKU 2018 min bɛ tali kɛ kalankulu saba ( 3 ) labɛnni baaraw ye.
biro ni barokɛyɔrɔ labɛnnen, kulu fila ( 2 ) ni latirini saba ye Jalanikɔrɔ lakɔliw kɔnɔ, Hɛremakɔni Kɔrɔnkankɔ, Buguni dugujukɔrɔfɛjɛkulu Komini kɔnɔ.
ani SEWUBE DREPE – DEYƐSPE SIKU 2018 min bɛ Dugunina lakɔlɔsiliw, Hɛrɛmako Sɛntrɛri ani Masablakura SESKOYƐMU labɛnni baaraw kofɔ, Buguni dugujukɔrɔfɛjamanaw komini kɔnɔ, ye bɛnkansɛbɛn waatiw tɛmɛn, kasɔrɔ Mɛri Mamuru ma minɛni ɲangiliw waleya.
Nin ɲangiliw, minnu tɛ waleya, bɛ sefawari dɔrɔmɛ 8 462 631 la.
O waati kɔnɔ, an ka kunnafonisunw y’a dantigɛ ko sɛgɛsɛgɛli baarakɛkulu ye laseliw sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛ, minnu bɛ tali kɛ fɛɛrɛfɛrɛw ani taamakow labɛnniw kan Buguni Mɔgɔfɛrɛmaraka Komini kɔnɔ, mara kontiw, nafolokow kunnafonisɛbɛnw ani mɔgɔfɛnw bɛnkansɛbɛnw kɔnɔ.
ɔgɔnkunbɛnw b’a jira k’a fɔ ko nafolokow baarakɛjɛkulu perezidan y’a mɔgɔ kɛrɛfɛjɛkɛrɛfɛjɛkɛrɛfɛjɛkɛrɛfɛjɛkɛrɛfɛjɛkɛrɛfɛjɛkɛrɛfɛjɛkɛrɛfɛjɛkɛrɛfɛjɛkɛrɛfɛjɛkɛrɛfɛjɛkɛrɛfɛjɛkɛrɛfɛjɛkɛrɛfɛjɛkɛrɛfɛjɛkɛrɛfɛjɛkɛrɛfɛjɛkɛrɛfɛjɛkɛrɛrɛfɛjɛkɛr
O cogo de la waati kɔnɔ, min sɛgɛsɛgɛli bɛ kɛ, SEFAWARI dɔrɔmɛ 5 ani 760 000 hakɛ kɔnɔ, min sɔrɔla feerew feerew la, Nafolokow ɲɛnabɔli baarakɛjɛkulu perezidan ye SEFAWARI dɔrɔmɛ 650 000 di sɛgɛnkɛrɛnnenw marabolo ma, o kɔfɛ sɛgɛsɛgɛli baarakɛjɛkulu ka tɛmɛnen kɔfɛ, o kɔfɛ SEFAWARI dɔrɔmɛ 1 ani 090 000 sɛgɛsɛgɛli sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɔfɛ.
Nafolokow ɲɛnabɔli ɲɛnabɔli baarakɛjɛkulu perezidan tɛ wari hakɛ bakuruba ye miliyɔn 4 ( SEFAWARI miliyɔn 4 020 000 ) ye.
Kɔlɔsiliw labɛnniw - Gabegiy, min bɛ sen na Buguni Mɛri kɔnɔ, bɛ ka tɛmɛ ɲɔgɔn kan.
O kɔnɔ, an ka kumaɲɔgɔnw b’a ɲɛfɔ ko Buguni Karamɔgɔyaso ɛmɔgɔ ye mɛri Mamuru Kulibali ka latigɛlisɛbɛn ma, ni sariyasɔsɔ ye, karensaɲɛmɔgɔw saraw bila, minnu y’u yɛlɛma ka bɔ Buguni dugujukɔrɔfɛjamanaw komini kɔnɔ.
O cogo la, sɛgɛsɛgɛli baarakɛjɛkulu y’a jate k’a fɔ ko, saraw kɛcogoyaw kɔnɔ, minnu sigilen don Karamɔgɔyaso fɛ, Buguni Mɛri, Mamuru Kulibali, ye dugujukɔrɔfɛjɛkuluw jɛkuluw ka saraw sarali latigɛ, minnu y’u yɛlɛma ka bɔ Komini kɔnɔ, kasɔrɔ sariyasɛbɛn min bɛ saraliw kɛli la ka tɛmɛna.
Wari hakɛ bɛɛ minɛnen kɔnɔ, sɛgɛsɛgɛli waati kɔnɔ, bɛ yɔrɔ ka tɛmɛ an ka franki miliyɔn 126 ye (126 712 156 SEFAWARI ) la.
Wa n’a ye nafoloko gɛlɛya ye, sɛgɛsɛgɛlikɛla tɔn y’a jira k’a fɔ ko Buguni Mɛri ka nafolokow ɛmɔgɔ ma labato dugukolo yɛlɛmancɛyɔrɔ dɔgɔyɔrɔ dɔgɔyɔrɔ ma, min sigilen don kunnafoniw kɔnɔ, a sɛgɛsɛgɛli waati kɔnɔ.
O la, sɛgɛsɛgɛlikɛlaw ka sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɔfɛsɛgɛli kɔfɛ, bɔliw, sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛnɛ kan kɛnɛ kan waati kɔnɔ, ani sɔngɔw laseliw ani sɔngɔw laseliw, minnu bɛ kɛnɛ kan, minnu bɛ bɔliw kan ka bɔliw kan ni minnu sigilen don laseliw kɔnɔ, b’a jira k’a fɔ ko Buguni Mɛri ka sɔngɔw Kɛbaga ye sɔngɔ minnu ka kɛnɛ kan, k’a kɛnɛ kan kɛnɛ kan, ka bɔli kɛnɛ kan ka bɔli kɛnɛ kan
Jɔnjɔnw hakɛ jɔnjɔn, jɔnjɔn min bɛ jɔnjɔn jɔnjɔn cɛ, min sigilen don laseliw fɛ ani wari hakɛ jɔnjɔnw fɛ, minnu sɔrɔla SEFAWARI 24 479 750 ye san 2018 ani san 2019 baaraw kɔnɔ.
I n’a fɔ o tun tɛ kɛ kɛcogo ye, dugujukɔrɔfɛnw yɛlɛmani wɛrɛw kama san 2018 ani san 2019 la, wari hakɛ sɔrɔli si ma sɔrɔ ka tɛmɛ miliyɔn 29 ye ( SEFAWARI miliyɔn 29 520 000 ) kan.
Wari hakɛ bakurubaw, minnu tɛ wari hakɛ sɔrɔ, bɛ sefawari miliyɔn 53,9 la (SEFAWARI miliyɔn 53 999 750).
Ani fana san 2017, dugujukɔrɔfɛnw yɛlɛmaniw siratigɛ la, ɲɛmɔgɔ ye miliyɔn 10 ( SEFAWARI 10 124 250 ) sɔrɔ sariyasɔsɔ, kasɔrɔ kunnafoni t’a la.
Sigida yiriwali kɛrɛnkɛrɛnnenw cɛ. Nin nafolokow ɲɔgɔnna jɔyɔrɔtigiw senfɛ, Buguni dugujukɔrɔfɛjamanaw ka Mɛri kɛsuw ye SEFAWARI miliyɔn 208 hakɛ sɔrɔ ( SEFAWARI miliyɔn 208 143 787 ) pereperelatigɛ an kumalaselaw b’o pereperelatigɛ.
Min bolo, dugujukɔrɔfɛnw yɛlɛmaba bɛ Buguni dugujukɔrɔfɛnw la, fana ye Mɛri Mamuru Kulibali ka ban k’u ka sewaɲɔgɔnkunbɛnw lasɔrɔli bali.
U b’a dantigɛ fana, Mɛri ma PEDESEYƐSI ( Sɔrɔko ani hadamadenyako yiriwali baarabolodali ) kɔlɔsilikɛjɛkulu dɔ sigi.
Yanni a k’a fara a kan ko a bɛ sɔrɔw di ni sariyasɔsɔ ye.
ani fana a tɛ Komini ka baaraw kɛcogoya yɛrɛ sɛgɛsɛgɛli kɛ.
O kɔfɛ, nin ɲɛnabɔcogo gɛlɛya, an ka kunnafonisunw b’a jira k’a fɔ ko Buguni Mɛri bɛ dɛsɛ.
A ka Mɛri, Mamuru Kulibali bɛ dɛsɛ, n’a ka mɔgɔw bɛ foroba jɔyɔrɔtigiya ye.
A bɛ dɔgɔn, fana, ɲangata ani ɲangata fɛ, minnu labɛnnen don ɲɛnabɔli kɛcogoya la.
Buguni Mɔgɔmɔgɔyaso ka gɛlɛyaw bɛ kɛ kuma damadɔw kɔnɔ.
baarakɛcogoya, nafolokow tilaliw ani hadamadenw ani nafolokow ɲɛnabɔli ɲɛnabɔli kɛcogoya la.
Sɛbɛn.
Ka tɛmɛ SEFAWARI miliyɔn 208 ye, Mɛri ka wele tɛ dɔwɛrɛ ye.
